
1a1(dkar chag): bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gsung bar du bsgrubs pa'i dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba bzhugs so// //
1b1(dkar chag): na mo gu ru mu nIn+d+rA ya/ zab zhi spros kun nyer zhi bde chen chos sku dang/ /dbyer med mi mthun rigs med
1b2(dkar chag): mtshan dpe sgra 'phrul sku/ /gang mos 'gro ba'i mos pa ji bzhin rtag 'char ba/ /sku gnyis zung 'jug gnyis med
1b3(dkar chag): gsung gang der phyag 'tshal/ /mdza' gnyis las 'das rten 'byung dbu ma'i lam bzang po/ /tshul khrims ting 'dzin
1b4(dkar chag): la brten yang yang goms pa las/ /rdul dang mun pa kun zhi so so rang rig yul/ /rang bzhin rnam 'gyur rkyen gyis
1b5(dkar chag): rab mtshon chos la 'dud/ /bden bzhi rten 'byung la mkhas snying rje'i gzhan dbang can/ /byang phyogs so bdun
2a1(dkar chag): phyin drug sku bzhi rim gnyis la/ /gus dang rtag tu sbyor bas goms pa lhur len pa/ /theg gsum dge 'dun tshogs mchog rnams la gus
2a2(dkar chag): phyag 'tshal/ /bde bar gshegs kun yon tan dbyer med kyang/ /rtsod dus tshe lo brgya pa'i ma rung 'gro /thugs rje'i zhags pas lhag par dam 'ching ba/ /
2a3(dkar chag): skyob pa mnyam med bu ram shing par 'dud/ /ston pa mchog des dka' ba brgya phrag gis/ /bsgrubs pa'i chos sku'i bdag rkyen las byung ba/ /mdo rgyud ma lus
2a4(dkar chag): mi brjed gzung kyi mtshor/ /legs bzung bka' bsdu mdzad rnams la phyag 'tshal/ /ldems dgongs rlabs 'khrug zab gting ring zhing/ /rgya chen spyod
2a5(dkar chag): pa'i mdza' dbus rtogs dka' ba/ /rnam dpyod snying stobs thabs mkhas kyis brgal nas/ /zab rgyas snying po bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal/ /thar 'dod
2b1(dkar chag): yongs la snyoms par stsol mdzad pa/ /klu sgrub thogs med la sogs rgya bod kyi/ /'grel mdzad lo paN chos rgyal blon por bcas/ /bstan pa gsal byed kun la gus phyag 'tshal/ /sde
2b2(dkar chag): snod gsum dang rgyud sde rnam bzhi'i don/ /mkhas blun bshad pa'i 'o chu 'dres pa rnams/ /so sor 'byed mkhas 'jam dbyangs gzhon nu'i sras/ /rgyal ba gnyis pa blo bzang grags
2b3(dkar chag): par 'dud/ /kun rtog spros pa'i sgrib g.yogs dang bral yang// /zhi drag sku yi spros pa sna tshogs pas/ /mchog dang thun mong dngos grub kun stsol ba/ /yi dam dkyil 'khor tshogs la gus
2b4(dkar chag): phyag 'tshal/ /'gro la rjes chags bzod glags med pa'i mdangs/ /rnam pa drag cing rtsub pa'i rngams brjid kyis/ /gdug can snying khrag 'thung la dpa' ba' i sku/ /dam can rgya mtshos g.yel
2b5(dkar chag): med byar mdzod/ /mngon mtho nges legs thob byed blang dor gnas/ /gsal bar ston pa mdo rgyud dka' ba'i gnad/ /'thor sdud rgyas 'grel 'khrugs sdebs legs bshad rnams/ /
3a1(dkar chag): par tu brkos pa'i dkar chag mdor bsdus 'chad/ /snying rje pad+ma dkar po'i mdo sde las/ /mi mjed zhing 'dir rnam 'dren stong dang lnga/ /'byung gsungs de nang tshe lo brgya ba'i
3a2(dkar chag): dus/ /snying stobs phul byung shAkya'i rgyal po byung/ /de yang sngon tshe rgya mtsho'i rdul gyur tshe/ /rtsod dus 'gro ba 'dren la dpa' ba' i blos/ /smon lam lnga brgya btab nas zhing 'di bzung/ /de tshe pad dkar
3a3(dkar chag): lta bur rgyal bas bsngags/ /bsngags ba ji bzhin gzhon nu don kun grub/ /rgyal srid 'byor pa rtsa ltar dor mdzad nas/ /rab byung dka' ba lo drug spyad byas nas/ /bdud kyi dbung bcom bla med
3a4(dkar chag): rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /de tshe lha yi lhar gyur kun gzigs thugs kyis 'gro ba'i khams la gzigs/ /'ching ba ma lus gcod byed smra bsam brjod 'das byis pas rtogs dka' ba/ /ji bzhin
3a5(dkar chag): bstan na snod min chud za btang snyoms bzhugs dgongs tshe/ /smon lam mthu ldan tshangs dang dbang pos dung dang gser 'khor phul nas bskul/ /de nas rigs can gsum gyi dbang po dang/ /
3b1(dkar chag): 'tshams par mi dang lha klu'i gnas rnams su/ /mdo rgyud drang nges tshad las 'das pa gsungs/ /gsang ba'i bdag po 'jam dbyangs kun dga' sogs/ /theg pa che chung bka' bsdu mdzad rnams kyi/ /mi brjed gzungS
3b2(dkar chag): kyis chad lhag med par bsdus/ /phyi rabs don du yi ge'i gzugs su bkod/ /de dag phal cher lha klu o rgyan gyi/ /gnas su bzhugs las 'phags yul dar ba dang/ /klu sgrub thogs med rjes 'brang
3b3(dkar chag): bcas rnams kyis/ /mdo rgyud dgongs 'grel mdzad pa khungs btsun rnams/ /bsil ldan ljongs 'dir skal bzang 'gro ba'i ched/ /legs sbyar lha yi skad las bod skad du/ /bsgyur ba'i srol dbyed thon
3b4(dkar chag): mi 'jam ba'i dbyangs/ /mi rje srong btsan bstan pa'i srog rtsa nyid/ /de nas rgyal rabs lnga nas 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ /mi yi gzugs 'chang khri srong lde'u btsan gyis/ /dka' ba brgya phrag du mas 'phagS
3b5(dkar chag): yul nas/ /bo d+hi satwa pad+ma 'byung gnas dang/ /bi ma mi tra ka ma shI la sogs/ /mkhas grub paN chen bgrang yas sbyan drangs nas/ /ye shes dbang po klu dbang bai ro sogs/ /rab byung brda sprod gtsug lag
3b6(dkar chag): kun la sbyangs/ /rnam par snang mdzad ka cog la sogs pa/ 'gro ba'i rnam 'dren rnams kyi thugs bskyed dang/ /smon lam 'bum phrag du ma'i rlung shugs kyis/ /rgyal ba'i dam chos srid pa'i mig 'bar
4a1(dkar chag): ba/ /byang phyogs mun pa 'thibs pa'i mkha' la drangs/ /ba lang ltar rmongs snying gi mun pa bsal/ /'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i 'dab stong nyams rtogs kyi/ /so 'phreng dngom pa bdud la 'phya ba bzhin/ /de
4a2(dkar chag): nas 'gro ba'i bsod nams min pa kun/ /gzugs su bgyis 'dra glang dar sgra gcan gyi/ /mjug mas phan bde'i 'od stong 'gyed par sgribs/ /'jig rten dge legs par tshal zum par byas/ /slar yang dam
4a3(dkar chag): chos 'dzin pa'i mthu grub pa/ /ye shes 'od dang rin bzang rab gsal sogs/ /chos tshul kunda'i gnyen gyur du ma dang/ /dI paM ga ra yab sras rjes 'brangs kyis/ /bslab gsum lus kyi rang bzhin mdzes
4a4(dkar chag): pa la/ /mkhas pa'i bya ba gsum gyi rin chen rgyan/ /rab mdzes dam pa'i skyes mchog bgrang yas kyis/ /gser ldan dga' ma'i khyon kun dog por byas/ /de yang ba mos reg pa'i chu skyes ltar/ /gyur
4a5(dkar chag): tshe shar phyogs btsong kha'i gtsug tor las/ /blo bzang legs bshad 'od spro grags pa'i dpal/ /phyogs kyi bu mo'i rna lung mdzes pa byung/ /de yis blo la rnam dpyod dpal byin pas/ /srid zhi'i dbul
4a6(dkar chag): sel bde legs mchod sbyin mkhan/ /mkhas btsun bzang po'i rnam thar gtsang ma can/ /'gro ba'i bsod nams zhing mchog mdza' yas kyis/ /bshad sgrub dpyid kyi dpal mo'i lang tsho la/ /thos bsam
4b1(dkar chag): sgom pa'i rtsed 'jos dus 'da' bas/ /dus mdza' 'dir yang rgya bod hor sog tu/ /chos srid 'byor pa rdzogs ldan dus la 'gran/ /de nas snang ba mdza' yas mi yi zol 'dzin chos kyi rgyal mtshan dang/ /phyag na pad+ma lnga rig paN chen ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho
4b2(dkar chag): yi/ /nyi zla zung gcig kha ba can gyi chu lha'i dogs su nub pa na/ /mdza' dbus phyi nang kun nas dam sri tsher ma dar btums mchog dman gyi/ /las smon smag rum stug pas 'dzam gling dge legs pad tshal zum? par byas/ /gnod 'tshe'i chu 'dzin
4b3(dkar chag): stug bos 'jig rten khyab byas dregs pa'i nga ro sgrogs/ /rno ngar mtshon cha'i gnam lcags rang gzhan kun gyi srog la za ba bzhin/ /ngan 'gro gsum gyi sdug bsngal 'dir lhags dmyal srung bya ba med par gnas/ /de tshe dam chos 'dzin pa'i
4b4(dkar chag): smon lam mdza' yas dang/ /dus ngan 'gro ba sgrol ba'i snying stobs phul byung ba/ /nyang stong po lha'i gnas su sgrol ma'i mngal sgo las/ /nyer thon bsod nams stobs kyis 'khor los sgyur ba byung/ /srid gsum za byed zhugs kyi phung po
4b5(dkar chag): lta bur mthu stobs bzod dka' der/ /blo gros nyam chung mun pa'i sems ldan lus med gnyen gyur pa/ /gangs can 'di na gtso bor grags pa'i skya ser dpung bsdoms nas/ /rang gi 'di phyi'i mdza' la ma brtags rgol bas rgyud bcas thal
4b6(dkar chag): bar brlag /dus mdza' i bsreg zar bud shing dmag dangs ltar/ /blo ngan rnams kyis ji ltar 'bad ba bzhin/ /'di yi dbung dang mnga' thang ches cher rgyas/ /khri skor bcu gsum kun la dbang bar gyur/ /che ba'i che mchog gnam bskos gong mas kyang/ /'di
4b7(dkar chag): yis mkhyen brtse nus pas thugs 'phrogs nas/ /tho ron pa'i li jun dbang che 'don bcas/ /bod 'bangs yongs kyi gtso bor mnga' gsol mdzad/ /gting mdza' mi mngon snying stobs chu gter dbus/ /mkhyen brtse'i rang bzhin rin chen gzi byin 'bar/ /chos srid mdzad
5a1(dkar chag): bzang nyi zla'i rna cha g.yo/ /mi dbang lhun po thub bstan gling bzhi'i rgyan/ /gang gi rnam dpyod gser sgong las 'khungs pa'i/ /rin chen sems kyi tshad med bzhi gdong gis/ /sngon med legs byas bye ba brgya bkod pa/ /blta phyir 'chi
5a2(dkar chag): med bdag pos mig stong sprul/ /gtsug lag khang bzhengs rten gsum mdza' yas bskrun/ /dge 'dun sde dang mnga' 'bangs bu ltar skyong/ /phas rgol tshar gcod chos rgyal 'di 'ong zhes/ /chos rgyal ral pa can de dbyings su yi bas/ /'di yi
5a3(dkar chag): gtsug rgyan mkhas shing grub rnams yin/ /yid la brnags pa bstan 'gror phan thabs nyid/ /mdzad pa dngos dang brgyud pas gzhan gyi don/ /'di lta'i mgon bcas bod 'bangs skal ba bzang/ /gang gi rlabs chen mdzad pa'i chu klung 'bum
5a4(dkar chag): blo gros chung du'i rdzing du mi chud pas/ /mdor bsdus de tsam de nang bye brag tu/ /bstan 'gyur 'di nyid par du 'khod tshul ni/ /nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'dam skyes dag la byams pa bzhin/ /snying rje'i rang bzhin can rnams dman pa'i 'gro la byams/ /
5a5(dkar chag): dam pa 'di ni gtso bor bkur bzhin 'bangs rnams kyi/ /bde dang sdug bsngal thams cad gzhan dang thun mong gyur/ /sa la gnas pa 'jig rten mes po 'dis/ /ma lus 'gro ba'i bde sdug rang rang gi /las kyi bgo skal kho nar nges pa'i tshul/ /thamS
5a6(dkar chag): cad gzigs pas gsung la yid ches rnyed/ /dkar nag las kyi 'brel pa phra zhib kun/ /'khrul med ston pa rgyal ba'i bka' kho na/ /de yi dgongs pa ji bzhin rnyed pa ni/ /tshad ldan mkhas pa'i dgongs 'grel la bltos pas/ /'phags
5a7(dkar chag): yul mkhas dang grub bas mdo rgyad kyi/ /dgongs 'grel mdzad pa snga phyir 'gyur ba la/ /yang dag ltar snang 'dres pa phyag rgya bzhis/ /'thad pas grub dang ma grub shan phye nas/ /thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen grub pa yis/ /
5b1(dkar chag): bka' dang bstan bcos 'gyur byang bam tshad bcas/ /khrigs su sdebs pa'i chos 'byung blo ldan rnams/ /snying nas dga' ba bskyed pa'i bstan bcos mdzad/ /de nas bshad ltar yang dag bstan bcos rnams/ /zha lu gser gyi lha khang nang bzhugs par/ /phyi mor bgyis
5b2(dkar chag): pa ser 'bras 'phyong rgyas su/ /bzhugs pa gzhir byas de la thams cad mkhyen/ /blo bzang rgya mtshos snga 'gyur mang tsam dang/ /snga phyir bod kyi mkhas pas mdzad pa dang/ /gsar du rgya las 'gyur ba'i chos tshan grangs/ /bdun brgya brgyad cu bsnan pa po ta lar/ /bzhugS
5b3(dkar chag): pa'i bstan 'gyur 'di la busta ka:/ nyis brgya nyer lnga bzhugs pa 'di thams cad/ /mchog dman gdul bya'i blo yis rim pa ltar/ /mngon mtho nges legs lam la dkri ba'i tshul/ /rgyal ba'i bka' la dpang por byas pa'i phyir/ /blang dor gnas la tshad mar
5b4(dkar chag): gyur par nges/ /de phyir blo gros rab gnas kyis zhus mdor/ /chos rnams thams cad bka' dang bstan bcos gnyis su 'dus/ /legs par bshad dang de yi dgongs 'grel ba/ /de yi dbang gis /'gro
5b5(dkar chag): ba'i sdug bsngal sman gcig pu/ /bde ba thams cad 'byung par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs de bzhin mngon pa mdzod las kyang/ /ston pa'i dam chos rnam gnyis te/ /lung dang rtogS pa'i bdag nyid do/ /de 'dzin byed pa smra byed dang/ /sgrub par byed pa kho na'o/ /zhes gsungs byang chub sems dpa' i spyod 'jug las/ /'gro
5b6(dkar chag): ba'i sdug bsngal sman gcig pu/ /bde ba thams cad 'byung ba'i gnas/ /bstan pa rnyed dang bkur sti dang/ /bcas te yun ring gnas gyur cig /ces sogs mdo rgyud bstan bcos mang po las/ /bde legs thams cad sangs rgyas bstan las 'byung/ /
5b7(dkar chag): bstan pa gnas pa bshad bsgrub kho nar nges/ /'chad cing mnyam bya bka' dang dgongs 'grel rnams/ /brda dag gzugs legs yi ge la bltos pas/ /tsher gcod rjes 'dzin kun shes rig gnas kyi/ /brjod don cha shas yongs rdzogs rgyu skar 
6a1(dkar chag): mgon/ /blo gros 'od dkar phan bde'i bsil sbyin mkhan/ /gzugs brnyan 'bum phrag spro ba'i bar 'di bskrun/ /sngon tshe kha bcan 'dir chos rgyal dang/ /mkhas btsun grub pa sus kyang blo yul du/ /'di ltar bsgrub ba'i
6a2(dkar chag): sems tsam ma byung ba/ /mi yi bdag po 'di yi skal bar dgongs/ /blo chen kun gyi snying la'ang 'jigs ster ba/ /rgya che grangs mang shin tu sgrub dka' ba'i/ /khur 'di bsnams la snying stobs go cha bgos/ /gces nor kun dang srog kyang phang
6a3(dkar chag): med mdzad/ /'di ni rang don stobs 'byor snyan grags dang/ /mtho ris nyid dang thar pa tsam phyir min/ /mdza' med 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal kun bsal nas/ /bla med byang chub chen por 'god phyir yin/ /'jig rten kun tu thub bstan rgyas ba dang/ /gangs
6a4(dkar chag): can mgon po rgyal ba yab sras sogs/ /zhabs pad brtan cing 'phrin las rgyas pa dang/ /dge 'dun sde rnams bshad bsgrub rgyas phyir yin/ /bstan ba'i sbyin bdag gnam bskos gong ma sogs/ /sku tshe mda' thang rigs rgyud rgyas pa dang/ /mdza' dbus
6a5(dkar chag): 'jig rten thams cad bde zhing skyid/ /thams cad rnam dkar las la 'god phyir yin/ /de ltar gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir bstan 'gyur rin po che yongs rdzogs par du brkob lta ci smos/ /bris pa'i rgyun yang shin tu dkon par brten bstan pa rin po che nyams
6a6(dkar chag): dmas kyis dwogs pa thugs la brnags nas dpal mi'i dbang bos ring mo nas thugs smon rlabs po ches mtshams sbyar zhing/ snying stobs btsan po rma med ba'i go chab gos nas gsung par gyi chos sbyin mi zad pa bstan 'gro'i phan bde'i rtsa lag tu sgrub pa'i
6a7(dkar chag): dgos pa ni/ rang gi tshe ring ba/ nad med ba/ longs spyod che ba/ rnyed grags la sogs pa 'di snang rang don nyi tshe ba'i ched du dmigs pa ma yin par/ sdug bsngal gsum gyis mnar ba'i rigs drug gi sems can mar gyur nam mkha' dang mnyam
6b1(dkar chag): pa nyam thag pa 'di rnams kyi gdung ba ma bzod par de dag gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi bde ba la sbyor ba'i ched du/ rang gi phyag na ci 'tshal ba'i zang zing gi dngos po yod rgu btsal sbrugs/ ci shor yang med kyi ser sna'i mdud pa yongs su grol te/ nor las
6b2(dkar chag): nor gyi snying po blang ba dang/ don med ba'i dngos po don ldan gyi phyogs su bsgyur ba'i chos sbyin gyi sgo 'phar yangs por phye nas/ phan bde 'byung ba'i sgo gcig pu/ mnyam med bu ram shing ba'i lung rtogs kyi bstan pa spyi dang/ khyad par zhwa ser gyi bstan
6b3(dkar chag): pa rin po che phyogs dus gnas skabs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas pa/ de 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rgyal ba yab sras kyis mtshon 'jig rten gyi khams gang nas su bzhugs pa de dag thams cad zhabs pad brtan cing/ 'phrin las gong du 'phel
6b4(dkar chag): ba/ gnam bskos 'jam dbyangs grong ma chen pos dbus bstan pa'i sbyin bdag rnams sku tshe brtan cing/ bzhed don chos bzhin 'grub pa 'jig rten gyi khams mdza' klas par nad mtshon mu ge'i nyer 'tshem lus zhi zhing/ skye rgu rnams gnas skabs
6b5(dkar chag): su rdzogs ldan phan bde'i dpal la spyod cing/ ring min nyid dus lam gyi yon tan rdzogs te bla med byang chub snying po'i go 'phang la bde blag tu spyod pa sogs dgos pa khyad bar can du ma la dmigs rgyal gsung dri ma med ba'i dgongs 'grel bstan bcos
6b6(dkar chag): gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir 'gyur ro cog gi glegs bam gsung bar du bsgrubs pa'i sku'i rgyu song la/ par shing gi sbyin bdag gtso bo lho phyogs nor 'dzin skyong ba 'brug pas mdzad cing/ byings shel dkar/ rdzong skyid/ gnya' nang/ mkhar
6b7(dkar chag): rta/ rong shar/ gting skyes/ phag ri/ do rdzong/ seng rdzong/ lha khang/ dar ma/ mtsho sna/ dwags kong sogs nas 'bad rtsol chen pos drangs pa'i par shing lu/ gas 'chus/ mdzer rul/ 'khyog sogs med pa/ thog ma nas dpe
7a1(dkar chag): ched dam 'byar bsrings pa dang mthun pa 'byor ba'i stag spang ngo bdun khri drug stong bzhi brgya dgu/ par yig bri stan sbyar shog dras ma dbus legs ngo tshig 'bum lnga khri nyis stong brgyad brgya bco brgyad/ de dag la yang smar zhus/
7a2(dkar chag): bskyar zhus/ yang tig /gzigs 'bebs bcas tshar bzhi re med thabs med par shog bu bzhi sbyor dras ma dbus legs ngo sum 'bum lnga stong drug brgya sum cu so drug dang shog bsdems glegs shing rgyur stag spang ngo chig stong brgya dang brgyad
7a3(dkar chag): shog sbyor la gro zhib btsags ma gshor khal bdun brgya bzhi bcu zhe bdun snag tsha'i rgyur sgron dreg skam snur rgyab pa khal brgya dang bcu tham pa/ snag sbyin/ 'dzugs rgyag /gas bsdoms sogs la sbyin mkhar 'degs khal bzhi brgya lnga bcu nga bzhi nyag bcu
7a4(dkar chag): drug /bar shing 'dul sbyongs la snum khal chig stong dgu brgya bcu tham pa/ bar bskos lag cha'i bzo rgyur bal lcags 'degs khal nyi shu dang/ lcags rdzog 'degs khal drug cu re dgu nyag drug /sol ba 'degs khal chig khri bzhi steng lnga brgya sum
7a5(dkar chag): cu so gcig nyag brgyad/ rgya tshes khal bzhi bre bcu/ lag cha brdar dpyad 'jam brdar ngo tshig stong bzhi bcu tham pa dang/ rtsub brdar ngo brgya dang brgyad cu gya lnga/ par shubs rgyur gtsang snam dkar po 'dom nyi khri lnga stong bzhi brgya bdun cu/ gong gsal gyi
7a6(dkar chag): las gra'i spyi khyab do dam mgo chings ngor dben khang bla ma/ ju rig kho sho'u chi/ las cha ba'i gras mi grangs nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ bar yig pa e nas dbu mdzad bstan 'dzin bag dro/ dbu mdzad a bar nor bu/ dbu mdzad chos bstan 'dzin/ byings bris pa brgya
7a7(dkar chag): dang bzhi bcu zhe lnga/ snye mo nas dbu mdzad blo bzang rnam rgyal/ dbu mdzad bkra shis phun tshogs/ dbu mdzad tshe ring bsam gtan/ byings bris ba bzhi bcu zhe dgu /zhus dag pa dge slong grags pa chos 'dzin sogs dge bshes nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ las
7b1(dkar chag): cha ba gra ba gnyis/ shog las dbu mdzad bkra shis/ byings bcu bzhi/ bar brkos la phun gling nas dbu mdzad bde legs bkra shis/ dbu chung chos 'byor/ byings bdun cu don bdun/ e nas dbu mdzad blo bzang kun thub/ dbu chung pad+ma bstan 'dzin/ byings nyis brgya
7b2(dkar chag): sum cu so drug /snye mo nas byings brgya dang bdun cu don drug /dbus gtsang dwags kong dang bcas ba'i rdzong gzhis khag nas bsdus pa'i byings par brkos pa sum brgya sum cu so lnga/ shel dkar shing 'gro ba dmu mdzad blo bzang/ byings sum chu/ lcags bzo ba bstan 'dzin sogs
7b3(dkar chag): mi grangs nyi shu rtsa bdun rnams kyi lcags mo bya lo hor zla gsum pa'i gral tshes nyer bdun bsdus rgyud kyi dgongs pa dang 'brel ba'i byed ba'i rtsis las res gza' dkar po dang/ rgyu skar gso ba'i lha mo gnyis rtse dgar rol ba 'chi med 'grub ba'i sbyor ba dang/ rnam dag grub
7b4(dkar chag): ba'i rtsis las res gza' gong bzhin dang/ rgyu skar khrums smad rnam par rtse bas nang 'phrod sbyor sogs phun sum tshogs pa'i nyin nas dbu brtsams rnga chen zhes pa chu pho khyi'i lo hor zla bcu pa'i gral tshes nyer lnga/ 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po btsong kha pa chen po bar
7b5(dkar chag): de longs skur bzhengs te mchog gi dngos grub brnyes pa'i dus ston lnga mchod chen mo'i nyin gegs med dpyis phyin par grub par gyur to/ /de tshe gtsang ma'i gnas kyi sangs rgyas mthong rnams dang/ /tshangs dang 'jig rten skyong ba bran g.yog bcas pas kyang/ /
