12b3(dkar chag): phyed re/ zhus dag pa grwa pa nyi shu/ par yig pa brgya dang sum cu so dgu/ par brkos pa dgu brgya/ shing bzo ba bcu/ lcags bzo ba gnyis/ las byed jam bcas khyon stong phrag gcig dang bdun cu don gsum la rer bkra shis kha btags/ dngul bal
12b4(dkar chag): Tam gsum re/ lug khog phyed re/ gong gsal dbu mdzad che chung/ zhus dag pa/ par yig pa/ par pa/ shing lcags kyi bzo ba/ jam btsas spyir dgu tshan nyi shu rtsa lnga yod pa'i dang por rta dang/ mdzod jus rgyab btags dkar po yug gis gtsos
12b5(dkar chag): pa'i dgu tshan/ gnyis par rta dang/ mdzod gos rgyan bzhi lu hi yug gis gtsos pa'i dgu tshan/ gsum par gong 'dra/ bzhi par rta dang/ mdzod jus rgyab btags ljang gu yug gis gtsos dgu tshan/ lnga par rta dang/ mdzod jus rgyab btags
12b6(dkar chag): ser po yug gis gtsos dgu tshan/ drug pa nas nyer lnga'i bar gos tshos kha sna tshogs yug res gtsos pa'i dgu tshan nyi shu tham pa/ lag g.yog brgya dang sum cu skor la ja bco lnga/ 'jam thug gsum/ mi rer kha btags/ dngul Tam re/ sha bzhi gling
13a1(dkar chag): re/ snying ri bla ma ngag dbang 'phrin las rig 'dzin gyis dngul srang bco lnga/ nyi shar jo bo dgon bla ma ngag dbang bsod nams lhun grub dang/ spyi pa bcas nas dngul srang bco lnga/ lha shing chos sbug grwa za chos 'dzin
13a2(dkar chag): gyis bzo rigs tshang mar mang ja gnyis/ sa dga' 'go pa sger lha mdun pas tshe 'das lha btsan don grub chog thu dar han bA thur gyi don du bzo rigs pa tshang mar mang ? gnyis/ zhal 'debs su rtsam ru'i khal brgyad cu gyi gnyis/ nas ru'i khal
13a3(dkar chag): brgya tham pa/ lug khog brgya tham pa/ shel chos grwa pa ja dpon blo bzang dge legs kyis kha btags drug spag lnga bcu nga bzhi/ dngul srang lnga bcu nga gsum/ dga' ldan khri rin po che a chi thu no min han gyis nang mdzod dri ma med pa nyi shu rtsa lnga /
13a4(dkar chag): dngul gyi maN+Dal thur srang nyi shu rtsa lnga yod pa gcig /g.yu legs zhel/ spos shel che chung sna tshogs/ 'phreng ba/ rgyan cha sna tshogs/ skya ser gyi gyon pa legs zhel sna tshogs/ /mchod chas/ sbu har sogs dngos rigs gtos che ba'i ri gong khyon
13a5(dkar chag): sdoms par dngul srang nyis brgya brgyad cu tham pa/ bya bral sman rams pha ngag dbang 'phrin las kyis dngul srang brgya tham pa dang mdzod btags/ smin grol gling mkhan rin po ches dngul srang lnga bcu tham pa/ brag yag sbrul sku rin po ches shan
13a6(dkar chag): gzhung 'khor drug bcu bdun/ bka' blon mdo mkhar zhabs drung tshe ring dbang rgyal gyis bkra shis pa'i kha btags/ wa nag gi zhwa mo ja lar dang bcas pa/ gan gos la ljang rgyan bzhi'i khal kha'i rtsag gzugs skud rta dang sram nag gi rgyan
13a7(dkar chag): ldan kha gsar/ gos sngon gser rkyang rgyan bzhi'i la pa shag nang dar khras byas pa/ gos mar khu mdog rgyan bzhi'i la ba shag nang dar ling sngo skyas byas pa/ gos mchin kha rgyan bzhi'i la ba shag nang rgya zam gyis byas pa/ lcam
13b1(dkar chag): gnyis kyis byu ru'i phreng brgyan ldan bcas gong gsal spyir ri gong dngul srang brgya dang drug cu re gcig /dngul rkyang srang brgya tham pa/ mda' dpon blo bzang dar rgyas kyis dngul Tam ka'i srang brgya tham ba/ sa skya nas bar ston gnang bar 'go ba dben khang bla mar mdzod
13b2(dkar chag): btags/ legs cha tshan dang por rta pho chen dang/ gos chen li khri me tog ma yug gis gtsos dgu tshan/ gnyis par ja 'khor drug gis gtsos bdun tshan/ zhib mkhar khal brgyad/ sha dod Tam brgyad/ kho sho'u chil? mdzod btags/ legs cha chen dang
13b3(dkar chag): por rta pho chen/ gos sngon yug gis gtsos dgu tshan/ gnyis par ja 'khor drug gis gtsos bdun tshan/ zhib mkhar khal brgyad/ sha dod Tam brgyad/ rdzong dpon gnyis la mdzod gsar/ spyir ja 'khor drug gis gcos dgu tshan/ rtsam khal
13b4(dkar chag): gnyis re/ sha dod Tam drug /rti zam par mdzod gsar/ ja sbag gsum gyis gtsos dgu tshan/ rtsam khal gnyis/ sha dod Tam gsum/ las byed zla ba can gsum so sor mdzod gsar/ spyir ja 'khor drug gis gtsos dgu tshan/ rtsam khal drug/ sha
13b5(dkar chag): dod Tam dgu /par brkos 'go ba'i gnyer ba gnyis so sor mdzed gsar/ spyir ja 'khor gsum gyis gtsos dgu tshan/ rtsam khal bzhi/ sha dod Tam bzhi/ drung yig gnyis dang/ 'bo kha ba gnyis bcas so sor kha btags/ spyir ja sbag gis gtsos pa'i dgu
13b6(dkar chag): tshan/ rtsam khal drug /sha dod Tam drug /khang gnyer lnga dang/ sgor ba gcig bcas spyir bdun tshan /rtsam khal drug /sha dod Tam gsum/ bya gshongs dka' chen la mdzod gsar/ ja sbag /rtsam khal gnyis/ sha dod Tam gnyis/ rtsa gnyer la
13b7(dkar chag): mdzod gsar/ ja sbag bcas dgu tshan/ rtsam khal gnyis/ sha dod Tam gnyis/ par brkos 'go pa'i g.yog byings gang yod la kha btags/ ja 'khor drug gis gtsos dgu tshan/ mi der rtsam gshor khal re dang/ sha dod Tam re/ rdzong gi g.yog
14a1(dkar chag): gnyer pa gnyis la kha btags re/ spyir ja sbag bcas dgu tshan/ mi rer rtsam khal re/ sha dod Tam re/ las byed zla ba can gyi g.yog gsum la rtsam khal re/ sha dod Tam phyed re/ spyir lnga tshan gcig /par brkos
14a2(dkar chag): pas mtshon zhus dag pa/ shing bzo ba/ thab chen mchen gnyis/ lcags bzo ba bcas las grang mi grangs gang yod la mi rer rtsam khal re dang/ bal Tam re lag sprod/ rgyar dod rta drel bdun/ spyir legs cha dgu tshan bcu gsum yod pa'i dang por rta
14a3(dkar chag): gcig dang/ mdzod gos dud kha me tog ma dpus legs yug gis gtsos dgu tshan/ gnyis pa nas dgu pa'i bar rtas gtsos pa'i dgu tshan brgyad/ bcu pa nas bcu gnyis pa'i bar gos yug gis gtsos dgu tshan gsum/ bcu gsum par ja
14a4(dkar chag): gzhung ma 'khor drug brgyad dang/ /gos ser me tog ma dpus leD yu gis gtsos dgu tshan/ dbu chen bzhi/ dbu chung gnyis bcas spyir ja rdum bcas bdun tshan gcig /par shing sum cu nas brgyad yan'bul mi spyir gos dmar yug bcas bcu gcig
14a5(dkar chag): tshan gcig dang/ ja 'khor drug bcas dgu tshan gnyis/ bdun tshan le tshan drug/ lnga tshan gsum/ nyin 'khyongs la 'bras thug gcig ja ko pi rtse'i mang ja drug/ skya thug gcig/ chang tshod sum brgya/ zhal 'debs rtsam ru'i khal sum brgya
14a6(dkar chag): bzhi bcu zhe gnyis/ ding ri she spe mgar ba'i btsun ma bsod nams chos 'dzom gyi don du pho rta zeg pa na brgyad pa gcig dang kha btags/ 'bras spungs spyi so nas kha btags/ dngul srang bco lnga/ snum ru'i khal sum cu/ dam ring nyin
14a7(dkar chag): mkhar ba nam mkha' tshe dbang gis zhal 'debs dngul srang sum cu so brgyad dang/ bzo rigs tshang mar mang ja gcig /yang bskyar bla brang rgyal mtshan mthon po nas par ston gnang bar/ 'go pa dang/ las byed zla ba can gsum/
14b1(dkar chag): rdzong sdod/ rta zam /rtswa gnyer bcas la nyung ja sbyor bcu bdun dang/ 'bras thug gsum/ 'go ba gnyis so sor mdzod btags/ dngul srang gsum dang zho phyed brgyad/ lug khog gsum re/ spyir dgu tshan gnyis kyi dang por gos jus lo nyi yug
14b2(dkar chag): gis gtsos pa'i dgu tshan/ gnyis par gos rgyan bzhi dmar po yug gis gtsos pa'i dgu tshan/ las byed gsum la bsod btags re/ dngul srang gsum/ lug khog gnyis re/ spyir dgu tshan gnyis kyi dang por gos dus rgyab btags ljang gu
14b3(dkar chag): yug gis gtsos pa'i dgu tshan/ gnyis par gos dmar 'brug tshang nyal ma yug gis gtsos pa'i dgu tshan/ rdzong sdod gnyis dang/ rta zam pa/ rtswa gnyer bcas so sor bsod btags/ dngul srang phyed do/ lug khog re/ spyir gos dmar 'brug tshar nyal
14b4(dkar chag): ma yug gis gtsos pa'i dgu tshan/ 'go pa gnyis las byed gsum/ rdzong sdod/ rta zam/ rtswa gnyer bcas kyi g.yog /zhus dag pa grwa pa/ rdzong las byed drung yig /khab gnyer/ 'bo kha ba/ sgo ra ba/ shog las pa/ shing bzo ba/ par brkas ba/
14b5(dkar chag): lcags bzo ba/ thab chen gyi ma chen/ chod pa ngo g.yog bcas spyir ja thengs bco lnga/ 'bras thug gcig/ 'jam thug gnyis/ 'go pa gnyis kyi g.yog bcu drug/ las byed gsum gyi g.yog bzhi so sor kha btags/ dngul ba la Tam gnyis/
14b6(dkar chag): lug khog gi bzhi gling re/ rdzong sdod gnyis/ rta zam pa/ rtswa gnyer bcas kyi g.yog las byed gong gsal bcas sum cu skor la so sor kha btags/ dngul bal Tam phyed gnyis re/ lug khog gi bzhi gling re/ dpu chen bzhi la bsod btags/ dngul
14b7(dkar chag): srang re/ lug khog re/ dbu chung bzhi so sor bkras btags che ba/ dngul ba la Tam lnga re/ lug khog phyed re/ zhus dag la grwa ba nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ shog las pa bcu drug/ par brkos pa byings mi grangs brgyad brgya dang bdun cu don lnga/ shing bzo ba
15a1(dkar chag): brgyad/ lcags bzo ba gnyis/ thab chen gyi mchen gnyis/ tshong pa ngo bo gcig /bzhes spro bzo? mi grwa pa gnyis bcas khyon mi grangs dgu brgya sum cu so sor bkra shis pa'i kha btags/ dngul bal Tam gsum te/ lug
15a2(dkar chag): khog phyed re/ dgos cha sgrub mi tshong pa'i g.yog gnyis so sor kha btags/ dngul bal Ta ma re/ lug khog gi bzhi gling re/ gong gsal dbu mdzad che chung/ zhus dag pa/ shog las pa/ bar brkos pa byings/ shing bzo ba/ lcags bzo ba/ thab
15a3(dkar chag): chen gyi ma chen/ tshong pa ngo bo/ bzhes spro bzo mi bcas spyir dgu tshan nyi shu rtsa gcig la bzang gos bcad ldan rgya yig ma/ Tam ka ma/ gos jus rgyab btags mdzod gos bcas sna tshogs yug re yod pa'i dgu tshan nyi shu rtsa gcig dang/ rta bdun/ lag
15a4(dkar chag): g.yog brgya dang bcu gcig la ja bco lnga/ 'jam thug gsum/ mi rer kha btags/ dngul bal Tam re/ lug khog gi bzhi gling re rnams/ shel stod sprul sku rin po che bsod nams phyogs glang gis par ston dang/ 'gyed zhal 'debs sogs snga phyi gnyis
15a5(dkar chag): byung bar ja 'degs khal nyi shu rtsa bzhi nyag bzhi/ mar 'degs khal bdun cu don gnyis nyag bcu gsum/ tshwa ru'i khal lnga/ 'bras ru'i khal bcu bdun bre bcu/ thug rdor lug khog dgu /'gyed bal Tam nyis stong nyis brgya drug /mdzod btags bzhi dang/
15a6(dkar chag): bsod btags bcu bzhi dang/ bkras btags chig stong drug cu re drug /zhal 'debs su bzang gos rgyan bzhi'i rtsag pa dang/ mo gos sogs pho ma'i gyon pa sna tshogs/ kong rna pad 'dab cha tshang/ mu tig gi dpral thod/ ltag mtshar/ spyi nar/ ske
15a7(dkar chag): rgyan spos shel/ byu ru/ g.yu sogs pho mo'i rgyan cha'i rigs sna tshogs/ sag thag/ me mda'/ dpa' dam sogs mtshon cha'i rigs bcas dngos po gtos che ba byung bar gong gsal bar ston gyi ja mar nas 'di yan gyi ri gong thog dngul ngo thog
15b1(dkar chag): bsnan ba bcas khyon dngul srang stong phrag gcig dang lnga'i rtsis/ nag chu mkhan po rab 'byams pa dpal 'byor gyis ja 'khor drug lnga/ pho rta gcig /mkhar rta sman khang ba'i pad mas bzo rigs pa tshang mar mang ja gcig dang/ 'bras tsha gcig/ 'go pa gnyis
15b2(dkar chag): so sor kha btags re/ ja sag tha'i ji dpon tshe dbang rdo rjes mdzod btags/ dngul srang lnga bcu/ pho rta lnga/ nags shod mkhan po gshegs pa'i don du gos dmar yug/ shangs bkra shis rtse ba'i thang lha dang nyi zla dbang mo gnyis kyis mdzod btags/ sman
15b3(dkar chag): yug mdzod gos sngo sang yug/ mdzod gos sngo nag yug/ mdzod gos mchin kha yug/ lha rtse rdzong sdod spel? rkyang tsho kho lo tha'i ji dang/ mdar bsam 'grub pa gnyis kyis shag mtshal thur srang nyi shu rtsa bdun dang/ snum ru'i khal nyi shu tham pa dang bra
15b4(dkar chag): bcu gsum/ ka thog sprul sku tshe dbang nor bus bal Tam drug brgya/ gser thur srang gang/ dngul gyi leg skor g.yu'i phra ldan/ bka' blon 'brong rtse bas kha btags che ba/ lcags bya'i smon brjod kyi 'bru thob ru'i khal brgyad brgya lnga bcu nga gnyis gzhung
15b5(dkar chag): 'bul gyi ma zhus pa/ nang so dar nyan dge slong gis rta bcu tham pa/ mda' dbon pad chal bas kha btags che ba/ rgyan bzhi dmar po uyug /sman khab smu phu bas mgo ba/ rdzong sdod/ rta zam rtswa gnyer/ bar bris sogs mi grangs dgu brgya skor dang/
15b6(dkar chag): bu lag mi grangs nyis brgya skor la 'gyed 'chang zhabs tog la gong phab dngul srang brgya dang drug cu re lnga/ zhal 'debs su mgron gnyer phun tshogs kyi pho rta bzhi dang/ lcam gyi snam dkar 'dom sum brgya tham pa/ bkra shis pa'i kha btags/
15b7(dkar chag): gzhan yang rlon 'tsho rje drung/ ding ri yul chung a ya shar pa'i lhun grub/ 'bras spungs har gdong dge slong byams pa/ rgyal rtse logs bris ba'i btsun ma o rgyan sgrol ma/ dkar rgyud chos ston/ lo bstan/ bkra shis bde ldan pa'i g.yog tshangs
16a1(dkar chag): skyid/ shangs dga' ldan bkra shis chos 'khor gyi grwa pa blo bzang chos 'byor/ dpal 'byor rgyal mtshan/ shel chos grwa pa 'jam dbyangs chos 'phel bcas nas kyang che 'byor chung 'byor gyi 'brel thogs tsam bgyis pa rnams so// //
16a2(dkar chag): de ltar bsod nams zhing mchog bla na med/ /bstan 'gro'i phan bde gsal byed bstan 'gyur gyi/ /rta ljang can 'di bsod nams rlung shugs kyis/ /'dzam gling yangs pa'i mkha' la legs par drangs/ /'di la go rim thog mar bstan pa'i bdag /gang
16a3(dkar chag): der shes nas bsngags pa'i bstod tshogs dang/ /de nas rgyud sde bzhi yi rnam gzhag dang/ /de nas mdo phyogs theg pa che chung dang/ /de nas phyi nang thun mong gtan tshigs dang/ /sgra dang bzo gso ma nges sna tshogs dang/ /bsngo ba smon lam bcas pa'i gzhung
16a4(dkar chag): tshad grangs/ /rim bzhin 'chad la dpyod ldan gus pas nyon// //ka pa la khyad par du 'phags pa'i bstod pa slob dpon mtho btsun grub rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de ba dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis gtan la
16a5(dkar chag): phab pa/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon shes rab go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza randA na dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ thams cad mkhyen pa dbang phyug chen po'i bstod pa zhes bya ba mtho btsun grub rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza randA na dang/ lo tsA ba rin
16a6(dkar chag): chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ lha las phul du byung bar bstod pa slob dpon bde byed bdag pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de ba dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la/ dpal brtsegs kyi bcos shing gtan la phab pa/ de'i rgya cher bshad ba slob dpon
16a7(dkar chag): shes rab go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza randA na dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'phags ma nor rgyun mas mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas kyi bstod pa/ paN+Di ta rgyal ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ chos sku la gnas
16b1(dkar chag): pa'i yon tan thun mong ma yin pa'i bstod pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ shi len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ lotsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid la bstod pa dpal gyi go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba
16b2(dkar chag): shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ bdud btul ba la bstod pa rab dga' i lha'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa'i tshogs kyi skor la/ chos kyi dbyings su bstod pa dang/ dpe med par bstod pa dang/ 'jig rten las 'das par bstod pa dang/
16b3(dkar chag): sems kyi rdo rje'i bstod pa dang/ don dam par bstod pa dang/ sku gsum la bstod pa rnams paN+Di ta nag po pa dang/ nag tsho tshul rgyal gyi 'gyur/ sku gsum la bstod pa'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+ha ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sems can
16b4(dkar chag): mgu bar bya ba'i bstod pa jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho tshul rgyal gyi 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma'i bstod pa paN+Di ta thig le bum pa dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bsam gyis mi khyab par bstod pa/ bstod pa las 'das par bstod pa/ bla na med
16b5(dkar chag): pa'i bstod pa/ rje btsun 'jam dpal gyi don dam pa'i bstod pa/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi snying rje la bstod pa/ gnas chen po brgyad kyi mchod rten la bstod pa mi 'dra ba cha gnyis/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi tshul la bstod pa/ phyag 'tshal ba'i bstod pa/
16b6(dkar chag): dmyal ba nas 'don pa'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta ti la ka dang/ pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur rnams so/ /slob dpon ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa'i bstod pa'i skor la/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la bstod pa bsngags par 'os pa bsngags pa zhes bya ba paN+Di ta sarba
16b7(dkar chag): dz+nyA de ba dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ de'i le'u bcu gsum pa la padmA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dkon mchog gsum la bkra shis kyi bstod pa paN+Di ta bidyA ka ra sid+ha pra b+ha dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i
17a1(dkar chag): 'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi mtshan la bstod pa dang/ gcig las 'phros pa'i bstod pa dang/ sangs rgyas sum cu rtsa lnga'i bstod pa mtshan rin po ches spras pa zhes bya ba rnams slob dpon na mA tri tsi tras mdzad pa'o/ /dge bsnyen mdza' yas lhas
17a2(dkar chag): mdzad pa'i tshig brgyad pa'i bstod pa/ slob dpon ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa'i dkon mchog gsum gyi bstod pa/ de'i 'brel pa slob dpon rgyal ba'i sras kyi mdzad pa paN+Di ta dz+nyA na shAn+ti dang/ lo tsA ba dpal gyi lhun bo'i sde'i 'gyur/ dkon mchog gsum
17a3(dkar chag): gyi bstod pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ brgya lnga bcu pa'i bstod pa slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+ha ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon dga' byed snyem pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta
17a4(dkar chag): sh+rad+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ gaN+DI'i bstod pa slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta rgyal ba'i sde dang/ lo tsA ba d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ spel mar bstod pa zhes bya ba slob dpon ma ti tsi tra dang/ slob dpon phyogs
17a5(dkar chag): glang gnyis kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra ka la sha dang/ lo tsA ba bsod nams bzang po'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bstod pa/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i bstod pa slob dpon dkon mchog 'bangs kyis mdzad pa/ yon
17a6(dkar chag): tan mdza' yas par bstod pa slob dpon dkon mchog 'bangs kyiS mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de ba dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa/ yon tan mdza' yas par bstod pa'i 'grel pa dang/ yon tan mdza' 
17a7(dkar chag): yas pa'i don gyi tshig le'u byas pa gnyis phyogs glang gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de ba dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gis 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa/ sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das pa la bstod pa dpal chos kyi
17b1(dkar chag): grags pas mdzad pa/ bshags pa'i bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+hA kA ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
17b2(dkar chag): sangs rgyas dbang bskur ba zhes bya ba'i bstod pa lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das la bstod pa dpal rdo rje 'dzin gyi dbyangs/ 'di rgyud dag las phyung ba yin/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon zhi ba 'chos mdzad pa dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta
17b3(dkar chag): bi dyA kA ra pra b+hA dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i bstod pa dang/ de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi bstod pa gnyis/ pad+ma ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa brgyad
17b4(dkar chag): la bstod pa slob dpon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa/ rab tu snga bar nam langs pa'i bstod pa dang/ gnas chen po brgyad kyi mchod rten la phyag 'tshal ba'i bstod pa gnyis kha che'i rgyal po sh+rI ha ri sha de bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rA dza sh+rI dz+nyA na mi tra dang/ khi'u?
17b5(dkar chag): gang yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur/ bskal bzang sangs rgyas stong gi bstod pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan brjod rgyan gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba kha che paN chen gyis mdzad pa/ sbyor ba bzhi'i lha'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta ratna kI rtis mdzad pa/ bal po mahA pa
17b6(dkar chag): na'i rang 'gyur/ bdag nyid chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan la bstod brgya gar gyi mkhan po su ga ta? sh+rIs mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang/ shAkya'i dge slong kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ bla ma dam pa chos kyi rgyal po
17b7(dkar chag): la bstod pa/ paN+Di ta lak+Sh+mI? ka ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba shong ston gyis bsgyur ba/ dus mchod bzhi'i tshig le'ur byas pa kha che'i paN+Di ta shAkya sh+rIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis 'gyur/ tshigs
18a1(dkar chag): su bcad pa gcig pa'i 'grel pa phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa/ zha lu lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ shAkya thub pa'i bstod pa bcu pa paN chen nags kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ /lo tsA ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i
18a2(dkar chag): 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/ /rgyud sde'i lha so so'i bstod pa rnams ni rang rang so so'i skabs su bri bar bya'o/ /yon tan mdza' yas rgya mtsho mnga' ba yi/ /mchod gnas bla med rnams kyi bstod pa'i tshogs/ /sdeb sbyor snyan dngags
18a3(dkar chag): rgyan gyis rab mdzes pa/ /'grel pa dang bcas drug cu re bzhi bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chags tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las thun mong ba'i mchod pa brjod pa'i tshul gyis bstod pa'i tshogs bkod pa'i skabs te dang po'o/ /da ni
18a4(dkar chag): rig pa'i gnas lnga las/ nang rig pa'i bstan bcos las/ 'bras bu sngags dang rgyu mtshan nyid kyi theg pa'i skor las/ dang po 'bras bu sngags kyi theg pa'i skor ni// //ka pa la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ kha che'i paN+Di ta so ma nA tha dang/
18a5(dkar chag): bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po 'bro dge slong shes rab grags kyis bsgyur ba las/ mkhas pa chen po shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis bcos shing gtan la phab pa'o/ /'di ni rtsa 'grel phyogs gcig tu bsdebs na bsod nams che zhing/ ding sang bshad nyan dang ba'i phyir phan che
18a6(dkar chag): ba la bsams nas 'dir bris pa yin gyi/ rgyud kyi rgyal po 'di bstan bcos kyi khongs su gtogs nas bris pa ni ma yin no/ /bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel bshad rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya
18a7(dkar chag): ba/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi mdzad pa'i phyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi le'u dang/ nang sems can khams kyi le'u gnyis/ 'gyur rgyud dang 'dra ba bzhugs so// //kha pa la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad ba'i
18b1(dkar chag): dbang gi le'u dang/ sgrub thabs kyi le'u dang/ ye shes kyi le'u rnams/ 'gyur snga ma dang 'dra ba bzhugs so// //ga pa la 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sprul pa'i sku pad+ma dkar pos mdzad pa'i don dam bsnyen pa zhes bya ba/ kha che'i paN+Di ta zla ba mgon pos bsgyur nas gtan la
18b2(dkar chag): phab pa dang/ dpal ldan dri ma dang bral ba'i 'od kyi rgyud la 'jug pa'i bshad sbyar mi g.yo ba'i snying po snang ba zhes bya ba dbang lo tsA ba blo brtan gyis bsgyur ba dang dus kyi 'kho lo'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i bka' 'grel pad+ma can zhes bya ba dpal dus 'khor zhabs chen pos mdzad pa
18b3(dkar chag): kha che'i paN+Di ta som nA thaS bsgyur ba dang/ dbang mdor bstan pa'i 'grel bshad don dam bsdus pa zhes bya ba phyag rgya chen po grub pa'i slob dpon dpal nA ro'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta d+harma d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba las/ slar
18b4(dkar chag): yang sgra tshad pa rin rgyal gyis bcos shing gtan la phab pa dbang mdor bstan pa'i bshad pa legs pa'i bu dpal 'dzin dga' bas mdzad pa/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi gnas brtan chen po byang chub sems dpa' nags kyi rin chen dang/ rtses thang lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal gyis
18b5(dkar chag): bsgyur ba rnams bzhugs so// //nga pa la dbang mdor bstan pa'i 'grel pa dus zhabs pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta zla ba mgon po dang/ 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ dbang mdor bstan gyi bka' 'grel shlo ka sum brgya drug cu pa bu ston gyi 'gyur/ dbang rab byed kyi
18b6(dkar chag): 'brel pa rdo rje'i tshig 'byed pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad pa 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sgrub pa'i thabs yan lag bzhi pa zhes bya ba dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi shwa sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dus
18b7(dkar chag): 'khor gyi sgrub thabs yan lag bcu gcig pa dus zhabs pa chen pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zla ba mgon po dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sgrub ba'i thabs dang/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga gnyis slob dpon sA d+hu pu tras mdzad pa paN+Di ta wA gI shwar
19a1(dkar chag): gupta dang/ lo tsA ba rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor gyi dkyil chog yid 'ong phreng ba zhes bya ba dus zhabs pa chung bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi na sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba mchims yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/
19a2(dkar chag): paN+Di ta bud+d+ha sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor gyi sgrub thabs lhan cig skyes pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rol pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra dang/ rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ rdzogs pa'i rim pa ston pa'i skor la/ byang chub sems dpa' phyag na
19a3(dkar chag): rdo rjes mdzad pa'i sbyor drug/ dpal rab 'byor zhi ba dang/ cog ro ting 'dzin bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di phyag rdor stod 'grel las gung du phye bar snang ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis bris 'dug pas bris/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i snying po'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs bram ze bsod
19a4(dkar chag): snyoms pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rI b+ha dra ba d+hi dang/ gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag dus zhabs chen pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha ka ra b+ha dra dang/ gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ sbyor ba yan lag drug gi man ngag dpal a nu pa ma rak+Shi tas
19a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba mi mnyam bzang po'i 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon nyi ma dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ dus 'khor gyi man ngag nyi zla sgrub pa zhes bya ba rigs gsum mgon pos/ paN+Di ta ba kun na la gsungs pa/ bi b+hu
19a6(dkar chag): ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ ye shes spyan sgrub dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ rnal 'byor gsum gyi snying po gsal ba zhes bya ba/ 'jam dbyangs grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta so ma nA tha dang/ lo tsA ba 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ sbyor ba yan lag drug
19a7(dkar chag): gi man ngag dus zhabs snyan rgyud ces bya ba/ paN+Di ta so ma nA thA sh+rI dang/ 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ sbyor ba yan lag drug gi 'grel pa sbas pa mig 'byed ces bya ba/ slob dpon a wa d+hu tI pas mdzad pa/ zla ba grags pa'i 'gyur/ sbyor ba yan lag drug gi man ngag
19b1(dkar chag): tsilu? paN+Di tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sa man+ta sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ sha ba ri pa'i sbyor drug bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ sbyor ba'i phreng ba rtsa mi? sangs rgyas grags pas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba dge tshul shes rab dpal gyi 'gyur/ nang gi snye ma paN+Di ta bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ras mdzad pa/ de nyid kyi rang
19b2(dkar chag): 'gyur/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i rtsa ba'i ltung ba byang chub sems dpas mdzad pa/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i sdom tshig slob dpon a b+ha yA ka ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ri bo pa dang/ lo tsA ba kheng gad 'khor lo grags kyi 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bstod pa rgyun chags zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta legs
19b3(dkar chag): pa'i grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi na ya sh+rI mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba ldan ma tshul khrims seng+ge'i 'gyur/ brgyad brgyad drug cu rtsa bzhi'i rnal 'byor ma'i gtor chog /paN+Di ta kIrti tsin+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor la 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i rtsis kyis bstan
19b4(dkar chag): bcos paN+Di ta 'jigs med 'byung gnas spas pas mdzad pa de nyid dang/ ding ri chos grags kyi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta rA hu la sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyis bcos pa/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rtsis kyi man ngag yan lag lnga'i rtsis dang/ nyi zla 'dzin pa'i rtsis dang/
19b5(dkar chag): gza' lnga so so'i rkyang rtsis kyi man ngag paN+Di ta chen po shAkya sh+rI b+ha dras mdzad pa/ dpal ldan mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas la sogs pa rgyud sna tshogs pa rnams kyi rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa dpe med srung bas mdzad pa/ la stod ding ri gla 'khor mkhan pa khrod du/
19b6(dkar chag): rgya gar shar phyogs dza ga ta la'i paN+Di ta chen po bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra dang/ gnyal? gyi lo tsA ba mi mnyam bzang pos bsgyur ba/ rnal 'byor yan lag drug gi brjed byang yon tan gyis 'gengs pa zhes bya ba/ mkhas pa chen po gnas brtan nyi ma dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar
19b7(dkar chag): shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta sh+rI bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ras bsgyur ba/ 'di gnyis kyi zhu chen dbang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pas mdzad ba rnams bzhugs so// //ca pa la dbang mdor bstan gyi 'grel pa paN+Di ta rnam rgyal dbang bos mdzad pa/ dbang blo brtan gyi 'gyur/ sbyor drug gi man
20a1(dkar chag): ngag rdo rje tshig gi snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba dang/ de'i 'grel pa gnyis paN chen shAkya sh+rIs mdzad pa de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dpyal chos bzang gis 'gyur/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i rab gnas tshogs 'khor/ sbyin sreg gsum slob dpon dus 'khor zhabs
20a2(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwar dang/ lo tsA ba rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod dus 'khor lugs su bshad pa grub thob nyi ma dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ bdud rtsi thigs pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta nor bu dpal ye shes dang/ nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang/
20a3(dkar chag): chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa bdud rtsi thigs pa sgron ma gsal ba zhes bya ba a nu pa ma rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ga ta sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba d+harma kIrti dang/ rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa mi'i dbang po
20a4(dkar chag): grags bas mdzad pa dang/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa dri ma med pa'i 'od byang chub sems dpa' pad+ma dkar pos mdzad zer ba dge slong bsod snyoms pa'i 'gyur/ mtshan brjod phan yon gyi 'grel pa sngags kyi snying po bsdus pa dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/ 'di gsum
20a5(dkar chag): bod ma yin bar snang ste/ snga ma rnams kyis dris snang bas bzhugs su bcug pa yin/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i mngon par rtogs pa byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so/ /shes dang shes bya dbyer med dus 'khor lo//
20a6(dkar chag): phyi nang gzhan gsum bden gnyis dbyer med par/ /ston pa'i bstan bcos rjes 'brang dang bcas pa/ /mchog tu gyur pa lnga bcu rtsa gnyis bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ thabs shes rab gnyis su med
20a7(dkar chag): pa'i rgyud dus 'khor gyi skabs te/ sngags skor gyi le'u dang po'o/ /de ltar thabs shes rab gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi skor gyi bstan bcos rnams bkod nas/ da ni rgyud sde sgo drug pa rnal 'byor gsang mdza' i rgyud/ bde mchog gi rgyud kyi skor gyi bstan bcos
20b1(dkar chag): la// //cha pa la bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi stod 'grel byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dpal rab 'byor zhi pa dang/ lo tsA ba cog? gru ting nge 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur ba las/ shong lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pas bcos shing dag par byas pa/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi
20b2(dkar chag): 'grel pa sgrub pa'i thabs kyi gleng gi zhi zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po la ba pas mdzad pa 'gos kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha dras mdzad pa paN+Di ta mi mnyam rdo rje dang/ lo tsA ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ dang? mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' 
20b3(dkar chag): 'grel rin po che'i tshogs zhes bya ba slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta tA ra ka lak+Sha dang/ lo tsA ba gu? na sh+rI'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //ja ba la bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' 'grel dpa' bo'i yid 'ong zhes bya ba slob dpon skal ldan grags pas mdzad pa/
20b4(dkar chag): paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' 'brel slob dpon lang+ga rgyal ba bzang pos mdzad pa/ shlo ka bdun brgya ba/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs gnas pa'i man ngag thams cad rgya cher 'grel pa
20b5(dkar chag): zhes bya ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon lha spas kyis mdzad pa/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa yon tan ma lus pa'i gnas zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chos skyong dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud dang/ de'i
20b6(dkar chag): dka' 'grel slob dpon kong+ga nas mdzad pa gnyis sbyar ba'i 'grel pa/ gnyi ga'i bshad sbyar zhes bya ba slob dpon ta thA ga ta rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i 'grel ba de kho na nyid mkhas pa zhes
20b7(dkar chag): bya ba/ rtag ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ sdom pa'i rgyud nyung ngu'i mtshams sbyor paN+Di ta sum ti kIrtis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba grags 'byor? shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi rgya cher bshad pa tshig don rab
21a1(dkar chag): tu gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta pa ra he ta dang/ lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //nya ba la bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel ba in+d+ra b+hu tis mdzad pa dang/ bde mchog nges
21a2(dkar chag): par brjod pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon shu rang ga badzras mdzad pa /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur gnyis bzhugs so// //ta pa la bde mchog gi bshad rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/
21a3(dkar chag): paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel de kho na nyid brtan par byed pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po nor bzang gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ /gsang ba rdo rje'i
21a4(dkar chag): rgyud kyi 'grel ba Da bi he ru kas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ratna badzra dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ gsang chen pad+ma zhes bya ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa kha tsha'i mkhan po longs spyod rdo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid kyi rang 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/ /phyi ma 'di bde mchog dang/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi
21a5(dkar chag): rgyud 'grel du 'dod pa ci rigs su snang zhing/ so sor dbye dka' bar snang na'ang sdom pa 'byung ba'i rgyud phyi ma'i phyi ma zhes bshad pa dang/ mkha' 'gro ma ni rdo rje phag mo'o zhes sogs bde mchog dang mthun pa shas che bar snang bas 'dir bkod do// //tha pa la rdo rje
21a6(dkar chag): mkha' 'gro'i 'grel pa mchod ba gcig bzhugs so// //dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i 'grel pa gru gzings zhes bya ba slob dpon pad+ma badzras mdzad pa/ shlo ka stong phrag brgyad pa paN+Di ta dza ya sen dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi yon tan gyi 'gyur bzhugs so// //
21a7(dkar chag): na pa la sdom pa 'byung ba'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel pad+ma can zhes bya ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon ratna rak+Shi tas mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpal gyis rang 'gyur du byas pa la/ shong blo brtan gyi bcos pa/ he ru ka sngon 'byung gi 'grel pa/ yi ge nyung du zhes
21b1(dkar chag): bya ba/ paN+Di ta zla ba gzhon nus mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ta thA ga ta rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsA ba d+harma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor ma kun tu spyod pa'i rgyud kyi bshad sbyar/ slob dpon ta thA ga ta rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor ma'i kun tu spyod pa'i bshad
21b2(dkar chag): pa tshig don rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pA ra he ta dang/ lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta stong nyid ting nge 'dzin dang/ lo tsA
21b3(dkar chag): ba shes rab ye shes kyi 'gyur/ de ltar rgyud so so'i 'grel pa rnams bkod nas/ sgrub thabs dkyil chog /man ngag la sogs pa'i bskor ni/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i bstod pa/ bde mchog gi sgrub thabs de kho na nyid kyi snying po zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' phyag
21b4(dkar chag): na rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta so ma nA thas/ gnyal mi shes rab mchog gi don du bsgyur ba/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug lU i pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog gi sgrub thabs dpal bcom ldan 'das mngon? par rtogs pa zhes bya ba paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra tha?  rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur la
21b5(dkar chag): paN+Di ta nA ba ko Ti pa dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bcos pa/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po rig pa'i brtul zhugs pa dpal dA ri ka pas mdzad pa/ b+hang+ga la'i paN+Di ta ku mA ra badzra dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong nyi ma rdo rje'i 'gyur/
21b6(dkar chag): dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i cho ga de kho na nyid la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rig pa'i brtul zhugs pa/ dpal dA ri ka pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mAr badzra dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong nyi ma rdo rje dang/ spyil cog gi tho gar dge mdzes kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bstod pa don
21b7(dkar chag): thams cad grub pa rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma badzra dang/ lo tsA brgya brtson seng+gi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra badzra dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rdo rjes bcos pa/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi dkyil chog
22a1(dkar chag): dbang gi bya ba mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta kriSh+Na pa dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nya badzra dang/ lo tsA ba mal gyo blo gros grags kyis
22a2(dkar chag): 'gyur/ rdzogs rim ston pa 'khor bo? sdom pa'i rim pa lnga pa slob dpon rdo rje dril bu bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kriSh+Na pa dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bcos pa ste/ de dag la dril bu skor gsum du grags so/
22a3(dkar chag): slob dpon rdo rje dril 'dil? bgyi? sangs rgyas byung gnas bzang? po dang lo tsA ba 'gos lha lhar? bces? kyi 'gyur ?  kyang 'jug pa rnyed na slar? rdzong/ bu pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog lus dkyil gyi mngon par rtogs pa dang/ rim lnga'i rang 'grel gnyis/ paN+Di ta sum ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ bde mchog
22a4(dkar chag): lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ni ska laM ka dang/ lo tsA ba dpyal chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog lha lnga'i sgrub thabs rin po che yid bzhin gyi nor bu zhes bya ba slob dpon rdo rje dril bu bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi
22a5(dkar chag): dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ bde mchog phyag gnyis pa lhan cig skyes pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta radna rak+Shi dang/ lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i bstod
22a6(dkar chag): pa rgyal po in+d+ra b+hu tis mdzad pa dang/ bde mchog lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha la bstod pa rin po che'i sgyu 'phrul sbyin pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i bstod pa rgyun chags rtog
22a7(dkar chag): ge ba chen po chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma Ni ka sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ bde mchog sbyangs pa'i yon tan bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs rin po che gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po la ba pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba
22b1(dkar chag): mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rin po che rab tu gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po la ba pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ nag po pa'i skor la/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs
22b2(dkar chag): nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa/ shlo ka brgya nyi shu brgyad pa dang/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i dkyil chog nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas chos? kyi 'gyur/ yang dkyil chog de nyid paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo chen rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
22b3(dkar chag): bde? mchog 'khor lo'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nu'i 'gyur te/ bskyed pa'i rim pa skor gsum mo/ /rdzogs rim skor gsum la/ dpyid kyi thig le nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba mar
22b4(dkar chag): pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ gsang ba'i de kho na nyid rab tu gsal ba brtul zhugs spyod pa nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur la paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi dbang phyug gis bcos pa/ rim pa bzhi pa nag po spyod pa
22b5(dkar chag): pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur te/ nag po chos drug tu grags so/ /bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ngag gi dbang phyug dang/ lo tsA ba klog skya shes rab brtsegs kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs
22b6(dkar chag): so// //pa pa la rdo rje sems dpa' i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba'i bde mchog gi sgrub thabs slob dpon lU i pas mdzad pa/ rgyal bo in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad ba'i bde mchog gi rgyun bshags bsdus pa/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i snying po'i de kho na nyid grub pa slob dpon dzA land+ha ra
22b7(dkar chag): pas mdzad pa bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag dang/ phyag rgya chen po'i man ngag gnyis ri khrod chen po'i gsung/ rtsa mi'i 'gyur/ bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs in+d+ra b+hU ti 'bring bos mdzad pa/ r+Na mi'i 'gyur/ sdom pa bshad pa zhes bya ba slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa
23a1(dkar chag): 'or? ston chos 'byung gi 'gyur/ bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa'i 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi 'dzag pa zhes bya ba/ bde mchog shes par byed pa zhes bya ba/ bde
23a2(dkar chag): mchog gi mngon par rtogs pa slob dpon byang chub rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha dra sh+rI bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon DoM? bi? he ru kas mdzad pa jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bde mchog
23a3(dkar chag): gi sgrub thabs lU i pas mdzad pa'i 'grel pa pradz+nyA rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'kho lo sdom pa'i phyi rol mchod pa'i cho ga /gtor ma'i cho ga /lag mchod kyi cho ga /dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga
23a4(dkar chag): ste/ pradz+nyA rak+Shi ta'i chos bchir grags pa rnams /paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang gi bya ba'i rim pa/ paN+Di ta chen po slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rje'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ 'di ni lo tsA ba chen po thams cad mkhyen pa bu
23a5(dkar chag): ston zhabs kyi bka' drin las/ brda sprod pa'i tshul la blo'i snang ba cung zad skyes pa/ lo tsA ba d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra'i 'gyur/ bde mchog lhan skyes mar me mdzad kyi mdzad pa nag tsho'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi sbyin sreg gi spyi'i gsal byed pad+ma dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi sAts+tshI cho ga
23a6(dkar chag): ba'i lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta lang+ga rgyal ba bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang/ pa ri lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi chog paN+Di ta lang+ga rgyal ba bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta 'jam dpal dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong ba ri'i
23a7(dkar chag): 'gyur/ dpal lhan cig skyes pa'i bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa tai lo pas mdzad ba mi nyag lo tsA'i 'gyur/ dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs nA ro pas mdzad pa/ dpal he ru ka'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba
23b1(dkar chag): rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi bkra shis slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta tA ra ka la shu dang/ zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid kyi snying po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dang byed go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya ka dang/ lo tsA ba blo
23b2(dkar chag): ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ he ru ka'i rnam dag slob dpon sh+rAd+d+ha ka ra wa rmas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs bram ze b+hingka? ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gzhon nu bum pa'i rang 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti
23b3(dkar chag): dang/ mar pa chos dbang gis bcos pa/ bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ mai tri pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgya gar phyag na rdo rje dang/ ba reg thos pa dga' i 'gyur
23b4(dkar chag): la/ ba ri lo tsA bas bcos shing/ slad kyi paN+Di ta bud+d+ha sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bcos shing gtan la phab pa/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs 'khor lo sdom pa'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa 'khor lo
23b5(dkar chag): sdom pa'i rab gnas slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badzra pA Ni dang/ rma ban chos 'bar kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog bcu gsum pa nags rin gyis mdzad pa/ lU i pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog gi mngon rtogs kyi 'grel pa/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba tshul
23b6(dkar chag): khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa'i bde mchog lha bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs dang/ lha lnga ma'i sgrub thabs gnyis paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ nag tsho tshul
23b7(dkar chag): khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ de'i rdzogs rim ston bar byed pa rdo rje gdan gyi glu rtsa 'grel jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal pa'i 'gyur/ spyod pa'i glu rtsa 'grel jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/
24a1(dkar chag): bde mchog lU i pa'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon a b+ha yA kar guptas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ratna rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsA ba zhang grub pa dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ dbang gi rab tu byed pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob
24a2(dkar chag): dpon a b+ha yA kA ra guptas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab dpal gyi 'gyur/ bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs rang byin gyis brlab pa zhes bya ba slob dpon a b+ha yA ka ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ratna rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal
24a3(dkar chag): gyi 'gyur/ bde mchog gi sgrub thabs dpal nyin mor mdzad kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su b+hU ti shan+ti dang/ lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog gi sbyin srog gi cho ga slob dpon nyin mdad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud las btus pa'i
24a4(dkar chag): sgrub thabs byang chub kyi sems kun tu gzigs pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon ka lA ka bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kri ka ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i lhan cig skyes ba'i de kho na nyid snang ba slob dpon dpag med rdo rjes mdzad
24a5(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di ta dI baM ka ra rak+Shi ta dang/ mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom ba'i snying po'i de kho na nyid bsdus pa dang/ lhan cig skyes pa'i de kho na nyid snang ba dang/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i de kho na nyid kyi man ngag dang gsum slob dpon ku sa li bas
24a6(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ snga ma paN+Di ta ngag gi dbang phyug dang/ phyi ma gnyis paN+Di ta badzra bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa gnyis su med pa'i man ngag rnal 'byor gyi gtum mo slob dpon dge ba'i mgon pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA
24a7(dkar chag): gI shwa ra dang/ mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ lbu i pa'i mngon par rtogs pa'i 'grel pa sdom pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rjes mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa khyad par gsal byed/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga gnyis de bzhin
24b1(dkar chag): gshegs pa rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi chog yid 'ong phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga mnyes pa'i snying po zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bde mchog
24b2(dkar chag): gi man ngag ye shes 'byung ba zhes bya ba kA ya s+tha pa ga yad+ha ras mdzad pa de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog sdom 'byung gi sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta k+ShAn+ti sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba shong blo brtan gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //pha pa la
24b3(dkar chag): mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i sgrub thabs rin po che pad+ma rA ga'i gter zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dza ya se nas mdzad pa/ d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ rkang pa bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad pa'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta dza ya se na dang/ d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i gtor chog rin
24b4(dkar chag): po che asma garb+ha dang/ maN+Dal gyi cho ga rin po che ma ra ga ta dang/ dbang bskur ba'i cho ga rin po che dbang gi rgyal po dang/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga rin po che me shel dang bzhi dza ya se nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes rdo rje'i 'gyur/ rang byin gyis brlab pa'i
24b5(dkar chag): man ngag gi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ku mA ra sh+rIs mdzad pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i man ngag zhal nas snyan du brgyud pa yid bzhin gyi nor bu zhes bya ba mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi bstod pa shu kla ka la shas mdzad pa/ lo tsA
24b6(dkar chag): ba bsod nams bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs la bstod pa bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i bstod pa bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mahA dza na dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom
24b7(dkar chag): pa'i bstod pa slob dpon mai tri las mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi rgyun bshags rgyas pa slob dpon b+hu ri pas mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi dkyil chog rgyal po'i sras dpal 'jigs byed lha'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta
25a1(dkar chag): de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur/ dbang bskur ba'i rim pa'i cho ga paN+Di ta bde ba'i rgyal pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bA ra he ta dang/ lo tsA ba nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/
25a2(dkar chag): paN+Di ta ma na ka sh+rIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nu'i 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi
25a3(dkar chag): cho ga/ slob dpon dbu ba blo ldan gyis mdzad pa/ lhan cig skyes pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po dz+nyA na sh+rIs mdzad cing/ pho brang zhi ba 'od kyis bsgyur ba/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa'i sgron ma bzhi'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta sh+rI
25a4(dkar chag): d+ha ra nyid kyis mdzad cing bsgyur ba'o/ /de ltar bde mchog yab bka' i skor rnams bkod nas/ yum gtso bor gyur pa'i skor la/ dpal rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rgyal po seng+ge'i gdan can khyab 'jug sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta 'jigs med lha dang/ lo tsA ba
25a5(dkar chag): shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ grub pa'i rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal po in+d+ra b+hu tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nA len+d+ra ba dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sngags kyi de kho na nyid nges par bstan pa/ rgyal po in+d+ra b+hu ti chen
25a6(dkar chag): pos mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba ye shes rdo rje'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs lcam lak+Sh+mI ka ras mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dmar mo'i sgrub thabs ri khrod dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs in+d+ra b+hu tis mdzad pa/
25a7(dkar chag): paN+Di ta bai ro tsA na'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs zhal gnyis ma chung ba ri khrod dbang phyug gi mdzad par grags pa paN+Di ta bsod nams 'byung gnas bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ phag mo'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid ye
25b1(dkar chag): shes yang dag par grub pa zhes bya ba zhal gnyis mche bar grags pa paN+Di ta stong nyid ting nge 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ra ru tse dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ don grub ma chub ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon a wa d+hU tI pas mdzad pa dang/ don grub ma
25b2(dkar chag): che ba'i sgrub thabs ye shes dbab ba zhes bya ba dpal stong nyid ting nge 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ dbu bcad ma chung ba'i sgrub thabs lha mo dpal gyi blo gros mas mdzad pa dang gsum/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ra ru tse dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab gyi 'gyur/ dbu bcad ma'i sgrub thabs che
25b3(dkar chag): ba zhes bya ba dpal birba pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ra ru tse dang/ lo tsA ba rma tan? chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i gsang ba sbyin sreg gi cho ga sangs rgyas byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ra ru tse dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ gzhung drug sbyin
25b4(dkar chag): sreg dang bcas pa 'di dag bod na grags pa'i rim pa ltar bkod pa'o/ /rigs ldan ma'i de kho na nyid nges pa zhes bya ba oDyan du grub bas mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta dA paM ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA na'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma mchod pa'i cho ga /'phags mo ru sbal zhabs kyi sgrub thabs grub
25b5(dkar chag): thob sha pa ri bas mdzad pa dang/ de'i man ngag phag mo thugs kyi sgrub pa dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta A nan+ta kar dang/ lo tsA ba dpyal chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ mkha' spyod ma dmar mo'i sgrub pthabs/ grub thob rngon pa bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ni ska laM ka dang/ dpyal chos kyi
25b6(dkar chag): bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i gzhan don slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga dang/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dbang mdor bsdus pa dang/ rdo rje phag mo'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga dang gsum grub thob sha ba ri dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gau taM sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba
25b7(dkar chag): nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ zhal gnyis ma chung ba'i 'grel pa rnal 'byor gyi rjes su 'brang ba zhes bya ba grub thob bA rik bas mdzad pa dang/ paN+Di ta klu'i sbyin pa'i rnal 'byor gyi snying po'i don bsdus bstan pa dang/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i man ngag slob dpon dA ri ka pas 
26a1(dkar chag): mdzad pa dang gsum/ paN+Di ta dA na sh+rI la'i rang 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma keng rus ta ra Na zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad pa dang/ de'i 'grel pa ku mA ra bo d+his mdzad pa dang/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs
26a2(dkar chag): slob dpon dza land+ha ra? pas mdzad pa/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i phag mo'i sgrub thabs dang/ oDyan nas byung ba'i phag mo'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ phag mo dkar mo'i sgrub
26a3(dkar chag): thabs kong+ga sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsA ba ba ri chos grags kyi 'gyur/ phag mo dkar mo'i bstod pa slob dpon kong+ga sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ratna rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsA ba zhar grub pa dpal gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i bzhed pa'i
26a4(dkar chag): sbas pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga /slob dpon kong+ga byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pa la ha'u dang/ pa ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dgongs pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon kong+ga byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badzra pA Ni dang/ lo tsA ba
26a5(dkar chag): mtshur? dznA? na a ka ra'i 'gyur/ phag mo'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg gcig 'di bod ma 'dra'o/ /rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon shes rab bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrta dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rig pa
26a6(dkar chag): 'dzin pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta phyag na rdo rje dang/ lo tsA ba mtshur gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma mchod pa la sogs pa mdor bsdus pa'i man ngag /paN+Di ta badzra pA Nis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang lo tsA ba mtshur gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i
26a7(dkar chag): sgrub thabs kyi cho ga don thams cad grub pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i las dang po pa'i sgom pa mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/
26b1(dkar chag): lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ 'di nA ro mkha' spyod kyi gzhung yin/ gzhan don slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga /paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra b+ha renda ru tses mdzad pa de nyid dang/ ye shes rdo rje'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs lha sum cu so bdun ma dang/
26b2(dkar chag): de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga gnyis sh+rI u ma pa ti t+tras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra gu b+ha dang/ lo tsA ba rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ phag mo'i mngon par rtogs pa'i snye ma zhes bya ba paN+Di ta dge ba'i 'byung gnas spas pa zhes bya bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dA na shI la'i
26b3(dkar chag): rang 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bde ba mchog gi sdom pa la 'jug pa nges pa don gyi dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba/ slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ pradz+nyA sh+rI dz+nyA na'i rang 'gyur/ de kho na nyid yang dag par grub pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa de kho na nyid
26b4(dkar chag): bshad pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta brtson 'grus dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu sh+rI dang/ dze ta kar+Na dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma phag mo khros pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di
26b5(dkar chag): ta bud+d+ha sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis 'gyur/ mkha' spyod dkar mo'i bstod pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ mai tri mkha' spyod kyi rjes gnang gi cho ga /gzhan don slob ma rjes su bzung
26b6(dkar chag): ba'i cho ga gnyis dza ya se nas mdzad pa/ /phag mo dmar chung ma'i sgrub thabs sa ra ha pas mdzad pa/ phag mo rin chen rgyan gyi sgrub thabs jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta dI paM
26b7(dkar chag): ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ rgya brtson seng gi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bstod pa paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba khu ne tso'i 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo mdor bsdus pa'i bstod pa paN+Di ta dag gi dbang phyug dang/ klog
27a1(dkar chag): skya lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ ye shes dbab pa'i cho ga /dpal rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dgongs pa'i gsang ba sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon a b+hi yuk+tis mdzad pa/ gzhan yang a b+hi yuk+tas mdzad zer ba'i phag mo'i las tshogs/ lag mchod rnams
27a2(dkar chag): bzhugs so/ /lag mchod rnams ni the tshom gyi gzhir snang ngo/ /bde mchog 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel nyi shu lnga/ /yab skor gtso bo brgya phrag gcig dang lnga/ /yum gyi skor la lnga bcu rtsa dgu ste/ /gril bas brgya dang brgyad cu rtsa brgyad bzhugs/
27a3(dkar chag): bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ bde mchog gi skor te le'u gnyis ba'o// //ba pa la rgyud sde lnga pa kye rdo rje'i rgyud kyi skor la/ kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje snying pos
27a4(dkar chag): mdzad pa'i le'u lnga pa yan chad paN+Di ta dA na shI la dang/ lo tsA ba 'bro seng dkar shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta su b+hu ti sh+rI shAn+ti dang/ lo tsA ba cog gru ting 'dzin bzang pos zhus te gtan la phab pa las/ slad kyi paN+Di ta 'jigs med lha dang/ lo
27a5(dkar chag): tsA ba snyel cor shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ dbang blo gros brtan pas bcos pa dang/ le'u drug pa man chad 'bro'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i dka' 'grel pad+ma can zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mtsho skyes kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta k+Shi ti garb+ha dang/ lo tsA ba khu ston
27a6(dkar chag): dngos grub kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i rnam 'grel slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha dras mdzad pa paN+Di ta pu N+ya kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba se rtsa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //ma pa la dgyes pa rdo rje'i dka' 'grel rnal 'byor rin po
27a7(dkar chag): che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba brtul zhugs spyod pa nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kriSh+Na pa dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ brtag gnyis kyi 'grel pa kha sbyor shin tu dri ma med pa zhes bya ba slob dpon DAng+ga da shas mdzad pa paN+Di ta bi ma la sh+rI
27b1(dkar chag): b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba shod blo brtan gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //tsa ba la kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa ku mu ti slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa rdo rje tshig gi snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba dpal nA ro pas mdzad pa/ kha che shAkya
27b2(dkar chag): sh+rI dang/ dpyal chos bzang gi 'gyur la/ dbang blo brtan gyis bcos pa/ kye rdo rje'i dka' 'grel dran pa'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba/ slob dpon nag po pa chung bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dpal ldan zla ba dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo
27b3(dkar chag): rje'i 'grel pa slob dpon pad+ma'i myu gu rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pad+ma A ka ra dang/ lo tsA ba mtshur dbyig gi rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i 'grel pa mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon ratna a ka ra shAn+ti pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shIn+ta b+ha dra dang/
27b4(dkar chag): lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i dka' 'grel spyan 'byed ces bya ba/ d+harma kIrtis mdzad zer ba rnams bzhugs so/ /'di rgyu gar ma min par 'dug ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris pa'i stobs kyis bris zin 'dug pas 'dir bzhugs
27b5(dkar chag): su bcug pa yin no// //tsha gong ma la kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa rab tu gsal ba'i kha sbyor zhes bya ba slob dpon kA ya s+tha bgres pos mdzad pa/ glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur// //tsha 'og ma la dgyes pa rdo rje'i dka' grel
27b6(dkar chag): rdo rje'i tshig btu ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon kA ma d+he nus mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya de ba dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi don bsdus pa gsham cung ma tshang ba gcig /'dir dgyes rdor gyi 'grel pa nA ro pa'i gsung gi
27b7(dkar chag): 'od zer las skyes pa/ zhes bya ba ni brdzun par snang bas ma bris so/ /thun mong ma yin pa'i bshad rgyud rdo rje gur gyi dka' 'grel zhal nas rgyud ba zhes bya ba/ rgyal po in+d+ri b+hU tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nyi ma sbas pa dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/
28a1(dkar chag): gur brtag pa dang po'i bshad bya slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ gur gyi dka' 'grel de kho na nyid rgyas pa zhes bya ba lha'i rigs kyi blo gros chen pos mdzad pa/
28a2(dkar chag): ga ya d+ha ra dang/ 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dgyes rdor bde mchog la sogs rgyud sde mang po'i thun mong gi bshad rgyud dpal sam+bu Ti'i 'grel pa la/ slob dpon in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa'i yang dag pa'i lta ba'i dran pa'i snang ba zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta sh+rI badzra bo d+hi
28a3(dkar chag): dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla pa'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //dza pa la sam+bu Ti'i 'grel pa man ngag gi snye? ma zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbes pas mdzad pa/ shlo ka stong phrag brgyad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/
28a4(dkar chag): rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags kyi 'gyur la/ kha che paN chen dang/ dpyal chos bzang gis bcos pa la/ dbang lo tsA ba blo brtan gyis dag par bcos pa bzhugs so// //wa pa la sam+bu Ti'i rgya cher bshad pa rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba rnal 'byor
28a5(dkar chag): gyi dbang phyug dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ kye'i rdo rje'i rgyud phyi ma phyag rgya chen po thig le'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa zab pa'i don gsal ba rmad du byung ba zhes bya ba oDyan gyi slob dpon zab pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shes rab gsang ba dang/ lo tsA ba gre g.yung drung
28a6(dkar chag): snying po'i 'gyur/ phyag rgya chen po thig le'i 'grel pa dga' ba'i spyan zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta shes rab gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ ye shes thig le'i rgyud kyi le'u nyi shu rtsa gsum pa yan chad kyi
28a7(dkar chag): 'grel pa dpal rang bzhin dga' ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba'i dka' 'grel/ slob dpon rdo rje gsang bas mdzad pa/ shes rab gsal ba'i rang 'gyur/ ye shes thig le'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel gsang ba'i de kho na nyid ces bya ba slob dpon dz+nyA na par ma
28b1(dkar chag): yis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba byang chub 'byung gnas kyi 'gyur/ rnyog pa med pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon gzhon nu zla bas mdzad pa dang/ de kho na nyid kyi rgyud kyi dka' 'grel rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon ma hA su kha ta badzras mdzad pa de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba byang
28b2(dkar chag): chub 'byung gnas kyis bsgyur ba/ 'grel chung phran brgyad la/ dgongs pa'i skad kyi 'grel pa slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu g+ho Sha dang/ shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ glu'i de kho na nyid ces bya ba rdo rje glu'i 'grel pa slob dpon
28b3(dkar chag): mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ratna badzra dang lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje'i glu bshad pa zhes bya ba slob dpon sgron ma can gyi sdes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ mngon par rtogs pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba dang/ kye'i rdo rje'i de
28b4(dkar chag): kho na nyid rnam par phye ba dang/ bshad rgyud kha sbyor dang/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro las rtsa'i skabs bshad pa ste/ rtsa'i 'grel pa gnyis paN+Di ta ratna badzra dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ dur khrod kyi bshad pa gnyis ratna sh+rI mi tra dang/ shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ brda nges par
28b5(dkar chag): gzung ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba dang brgyad do/ /yang slob dpon rnal 'byor pas mdzad pa'i dur khrod brgyad kyi bshad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+hA ka ra badzra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dpal rin po che snye ma zhes bya ba'i rgya cher 'grel
28b6(dkar chag): pa zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po sh+rI gupta'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ de nyid kyi rang 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/ /de ltar rgyud so so'i dgongs 'grel rnams bkod nas spyi'i dgongs 'grel sgrub thabs dkyil chog lam rim la sogs pa'i skor la// //
28b7(dkar chag): zha pa la dgyes pa rdo rje lha dgu'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon mtsho skyes kyis mdzad pa/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa leng shAkya brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i mar me'i rtse mo lta bu'i man ngag/
29a1(dkar chag): paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i bstod pa dang sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dam tshig lnga pa pad+ma 'byung gnas kyis
29a2(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ ba ri chos grags kyi 'gyur/ dpal kye rdo rje la b+ha dra rA ga'i bstod pa/ slob dpon pad+ma badzras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di
29a3(dkar chag): ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs slob dpon byang chub snying pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI baM ka ra rA dza dang/ lha mu ne btsan po'i 'gyur/ slob dpon byang chub snying pos mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga /slob dpon Da bi he ru kas
29a4(dkar chag): mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid bcu pa/ jo bo rje dang/ dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ Do bi he ru kas mdzad pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i 'du ba bsgrag pa/ pradz+nyA sh+rI dz+nyA na'i rang 'gyur/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga DaM bi he ru kas mdzad pa paN+Di ta dz+nyA na A kA ra dang/ lo tsA ba mar
29a5(dkar chag): ba chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje lha dgu'i sgrub thabs/ DoM bi pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ rtses thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs gyi 'grel pa kha che dngul gyi bum pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ rtses thang lo tsA ba'i
29a6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba sgra gcan gsang pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ rtses thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ DoM bi pa'i slong mo'i 'grel pa/ paN+Di ta dzai ta kar+Na dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur /dpal
29a7(dkar chag): he ru ka phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon a la la badzras mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i dran pa gcig pa'i man ngag slob dpon gan+ta ri pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA in+d+ra ru tse dang/ lo tsA ba 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs
29b1(dkar chag): kyi 'grel pa dag pa rdo rje sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon dza land+ha rims mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs yan lag drug pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ratna sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba
29b2(dkar chag): shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i sgrub thabs bzang po yongs su bzung ba zhes bya ba slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa dang/ 'byung po thams cad pa'i gtor chog mi thub zla bas mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/
29b3(dkar chag): de kho na nyid bzhi'i man ngag gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ ti lo pas mdzad pa ratna sh+rI'i rang 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyi rgyal po slob dpon a wa d+hU tI pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs 'khrul pa spong ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung
29b4(dkar chag): gnas zhi bas mdzad pa dang/ lhan cig skyes pa'i dga' ba yang dag par sbyor ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ dpal rab 'byor zhi ba dang/ lo tsA ba ting 'dzin bzang po'i 'gyur dang/ lhan cig skyes pa'i rnal 'byor gyi rim pa kun mA rA ka la
29b5(dkar chag): shu'i rang 'gyur gnyis 'gyur tha dad pa ma gtogs pa chos gcig tu 'dug pas phyi ma bzhugs/ de'i 'grel pa bram ze tha ga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta man+d+ra ka la 'gyur gong ma ? ? ?/ shu'i rang 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs rnam par dag pa'i gter zhes bya ba a wa d+hU
29b6(dkar chag): tI gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ rtses thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ slob dpon kAmpa las mdzad pa'i dgyes ba rdo rje'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid bzhi'i rim pa zhes bya ba paN+Di ta bai ro tsA na rak+Shi ta dang/ glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ he ru ka zhal gcig pa'i sgrub thabs
29b7(dkar chag): slob dpon yan lag med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badzra pA Ni dang/ lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ dgyes ba rdo rje'i sgrub thabs slob dpon bde ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba d+harma tsan+d+ra'i 'gyur/ dpal kye rdo rje'i bya ba'i rim pa rin chen 'bar ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub
30a1(dkar chag): thabs slob dpon pradz+nyA in+d+ra ru tses mdzad pa/ de nyid dang shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa'i dgyes pa
30a2(dkar chag): rdo rje'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i gzhung 'grel gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga zhes bya ba/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa dang/ ro sreg gi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas
30a3(dkar chag): mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos kyi 'gyur/ rab gnas kyi cho ga'i tshul slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa dang/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i
30a4(dkar chag): rim pa slob dpon nag po bas mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i mchod rten gyi cho ga dang/ gshin gyi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzai ta kar+Na dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dgyes rdor gyi
30a5(dkar chag): dkyil chog he ru ka 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon nyin mo'i 'byung gnas zla ba'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dpal he ru ka'i man ngag rang byin gyis brlab ba zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta stong nyid ting nge 'dzin rdo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab ye shes
30a6(dkar chag): dang/ skye? rtsa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ he ru ka 'byung ba zhes bya ba kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon stong nyid rdo rjes mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po pur+Na kIrti dang lo tsA ba sna nam rdo rje bla ma'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon tA ra sh+rIs
30a7(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i dbang gtan la dbab pa/ slob dpon dzai ta ri pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba gyi dze zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dze ta ris mdzad pa'i gur nas gsungs pa'i khro bo
30b1(dkar chag): bcu'i rig pa'i cho ga /paN+Di ta dzai ta kar+Na dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ grub thob byin pa mdzad pa'i gsang ba'i dbang dang/ dbang chen po'i rim pa gsum pa dang gnyis/ dgyes pa rdo rje phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta su ma ti sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba
30b2(dkar chag): shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ gsung bsdus pa dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyang zer/ dpal kye rdo rje'i mngon par rtogs pa'i thig le rnam par grags pa'i mkhas pa gnas brtan shAkya srung ba'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba skyob pa dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ chos spyod mdor bsdus pa'i

34a6(dkar chag): thob dpal rgyan pas mdzad pa/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bla ma'i zhal snga'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon mkhas pa 'dul ba byin gyis mdzad pa/ he ru ka phyag rgya gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ ro bsreg pa'i sgrub thabs kyi cho ga /sgyu 'phrul chen
