34b1(dkar chag): gnyis te/ gsang ba yid bde'i chos skor dri ma med/ /bcu phrag gnyis dang bcas pa'i drug bzhugs so// //bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ sgyu ma chen mo'i skor te le'u lnga
34b2(dkar chag): pa'o// //ya pa la rdo rje bdud rtsi'i dka' 'grel slob dpon dri med bzang po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud kyi bshad pa slob dpon yon tan bzang pos mdzad pa/ smri
34b3(dkar chag): ti'i 'gyur/ rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa bdud rtsi 'dzag pa zhes bya ba grub thob b+ha gos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta tA ra pA la dang/ lo tsA ba mchims yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur la/ phyis paN+Di ta shI la ku dzha badzra dang/ lo tsA ba klog skya shes rab brtsegs
34b4(dkar chag): gyis bcos pa gsum bzhugs so/ /he ru ka dpal rdo rje bdud rtsi yi/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po'i rnam bshad dri ma med/ /mkhas grub rnams kyis mdzad pa rnam pa gsum/ /shin tu khyad par 'phags pa legs par bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro
34b5(dkar chag): cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ rdo rje bdud rtsi'i skor te le'u drug pa'o// //sangs rgyas thod pa'i skor la/ sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel ye shes ldan pa zhes bya ba grub thob chen po sa ra ha'i zhal
34b6(dkar chag): snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ slob dpon pad+ma badzras mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel de kho na nyid kyi zla ba zhes bya ba las le'u gnyis pa yan chad ji tsam rnyed pa dang/ sangs
34b7(dkar chag): rgyas thod pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel mi 'jigs pa'i gzhung 'grel slob dpon a b+ha yA ka ra guptas mdzad pa/ ding ri chos grags kyi 'gyur yin nam zer ba'i 'gyur rnying la dpar blo brtan gyis hor khong bas bas shing zhus chen mdzad pa/ bram ze chen po
35a1(dkar chag): sa ra ha pas mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas thod pa lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i sgrub thabs/ 'byung bo thams cad pa'i gtor chog /dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rim pa gsal ba rnams paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba gyi dze zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ ri
35a2(dkar chag): gi a ra l+li'i sgrub thabs/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur rnams so/ /dpal ldan sangs rgyas thod pa zhes bya ba'i/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po'i rnam bshad rnam pa gsum/ /sgrub dkyil gtor cho ga ri gi'i sgrub thabs te/ /chos skor dri
35a3(dkar chag): ma med pa bdun bzhugs so/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ sangs rgyas thod pa'i skor te le'u bdun pa'o// //sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi skor la/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi 'grel
35a4(dkar chag): pa rgyud gyi 'grel ba rgyud kyi don rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba oDyan gyi rgyal po dngos grub brnyes pa brgya byin sdong pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bidyA ka ra sid+ha dang/ lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi 'grel pa sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyan zhes bya ba
35a5(dkar chag): slob dpon rab tu dga' ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// //ra pa la sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rAd+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam
35a6(dkar chag): sbyor gyi rgyud ji snyed pa'i 'grel pa shes rab snang ba zhes bya ba shlo ka drug stong lnga brgya bdun cur? slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtI rang 'gyur/ 'di mnya sbyor gyi rgyud phyi ma'i 'grel par snang gi rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa min par snang ngo/ /sangs
35a7(dkar chag): rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dka' 'grel slob dpon rab zhi bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+ha ka ra warma dang/ d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ slob dpon ku ku rA dzAs mdzad pa'i rdo rje sems dpa' i gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang /rnam?
35b1(dkar chag): par snang mdzod kyi gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang/ he ru ka'i gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang/ pad+ma gar dbang gi gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang/ rin chen nyi ma'i gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang/ rta mchog rol pa'i gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang drug /paN+Di ta bidyA ka
35b2(dkar chag): ra sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rjes su 'jug pa'i cho ga lnga pa slob dpon ku ku rA dza sa mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rI badzra ha sa dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon
35b3(dkar chag): ku ku rA dzas? mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gu len+d+ra gu dra dang/ lo tsA ba dran pa nam mkha' i 'gyur la lha rin po ches bcos pa/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi tshogs 'khor gyi cho ga rgyal po in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta A nanda garb+ha dang/ lo tsA ba dran pa nam mkha' i 'gyur la lha rin
35b4(dkar chag): bo ches bcos pa/ he ru ka'i sgrub thabs slob dpon thu bo rA dza hastis mdzad pa dang/ he ru ka'i sgrub thabs slob dpon hUM mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bidya sid+ha dang/ lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ yang de nyid rdo rje bzhad pa dang/ rma rin chen mchog gi 'gyur dang gnyis/
35b5(dkar chag): sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi man ngag yan lag bzhi don snang bar byed pa zhes bya ba slob dpon hUM mdzad grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rdo rje bzhad pa dang/ rma rin chen mchog gi 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba slob
35b6(dkar chag): dpon hUM mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bidyA ka ra sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ khrag 'thung chen bo'i sgrub thabs yang dag par grub ba zhes bya ba slob dpon hUM mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba gnubs nam mkha' i snying po'i 'gyur/
35b7(dkar chag): sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sems can thams cad la bskyed pa zhes bya ba kha che rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ye shes rdo rje dang/ lo tsA ba gnyan bsod nams kyi 'gyur rdo rje sems dpa' i sgrub thabs rgyal po in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa dang /bde 
36a1(dkar chag): kha chen po rdo rje sems dpa' i sgrub thabs dang/ rdo rje sems dpa' rjes su dran pa'i cho ga slob dpon thu bo rA dza ha stis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so/ /sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam par sbyor ba yi/ /mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog rgyud 'grel lnga/ /sgrub
36a2(dkar chag): thabs la sogs chos skor bcu dgu ste/ /mnyan sbyor chos skor nyi shu rtsa bzhi bzhugs/ bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi skor te le'u brgyad pa'o// //la pa la sgrol ma rnal
36a3(dkar chag): 'byor chen po'i rgyud ltar du bshad pa la/ sgrol ma lha lnga'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma badzra dang/ lo tsA ba dar ma rin chen gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma spyi'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ lha mo sgrol ma
36a4(dkar chag): phyag 'tshal nyi shu rtsa gcig ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ yang de'i so so'i sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa slob dpon nyi ma spas pas mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta many+dzu sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba mal gyo blo gros grags kyi 'gyur/ oDyan nas
36a5(dkar chag): 'byung ba'i man ngag gi rim pa'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ kha che paN chen gyi phyag dpe las bsgyur ba/ slob dpon nyi ma sbas bas mdzad pa'i phyag 'tshal nyi shu rtsa gcig ma'i sgrub thabs/ kha che paN chen shAkya sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba byamS
36a6(dkar chag): pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sA d+hu kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba ldan ma tshul khrims seng
36a7(dkar chag): ge'i 'gyur/ lha mo dam tshig sgrol ma'i bstod pa/ sgrol ma me tog phreng 'dzin gyi bstod pa/ slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa snga 'gyur/ sgrol ma me tog phreng 'dzin gyi bstod pa slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen
36b1(dkar chag): gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka na ka warma dang/ lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur la/ slad kyi paN+Di ta ma Ni ka sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyis bcos pa/ me tog phreng 'dzin tsheg par bdun mar bcas pa/ paN+Di ta zla ba gzhon nu'i rang 'gyur/ lha mo sgrol
36b2(dkar chag): ma la smre sngags kyi gsol 'debs kyis bstod pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ slob dpon de bzhin gshegs pa'i srung pas mdzad pa'i phreng 'dzin lta lnga'i
36b3(dkar chag): spyi sgrub/ so so'i sgrub thabs la/ sgrol ma dkar mo la brten nas stong nyid bsgom pa/ sngon mo la brten nas lta ba ngan pa sun 'byung ba/ ser mo la brten nas tshom rkun bcing ba/ dmar mo la brten nas shes rab bskyed pa/ ljang ser la brten nas 'chi ba blu ba dang drug/ de bzhin
36b4(dkar chag): gshegs pa'i srung bas mdzad cing/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba cag? gru mya ngan med pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'dir sgrub thabs bla med du bkral 'dug pas/ bstod pa me tog phreng 'dzin yang bla med du bkod do/ /lha mo sgrol ma la bstod pa don thams cad grub pa zhes bya ba slob
36b5(dkar chag): dpon ma ti ci tras mdzad pa/ 'di gur gyi rdo rje sgrol ma dang cha mthun par byas 'dug pas bla med du bkod do/ /sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rim pa'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta mahA dza na dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od kyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i dkyil 'khor lha bcu'i sgrub pa'i thabs slob
36b6(dkar chag): dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol bas mdzad pa/ 'brog mi lo tsA'i 'gyur/ oDyan sgrol ma'i skor la/ 'phags ma gnas kyi dbang phyug ma'i sgrub thabs/ mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje ldan mas gsungs pa/ paN+Di ti saM g+ha ma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lotsA ba 'jam dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rje'i 'gyur
36b7(dkar chag): dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa/ 'phrog mi lo tsA'i 'gyur/ oDyan sgrol ma'i skor la/ 'phags ma gnas kyi dbang phyug ma'i sgrub thabs/ mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje ldan mas gsungs pa/ paN+Di ta saM g+ha ma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba 'jam dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rje'i 'gyur
36b8(dkar chag): oDyan sgrol ma'i mngon rtogs kyi rim pa zhes bya ba dang/ oDyan sgrol ma'i rim pa gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba zhes bya ba dang/ oDyan sgrol ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang skur ba'i cho ga mdor bsdus pa paN+Di ta pA ra he tas mdzad pa rnams/ paN+Di ta saM g+ha ma sh+rI dang/ lo tsA
37a1(dkar chag): ba 'jam dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rje'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma dpa' mo gcig ma'i rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs dang/ oDyan sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje ldan mas gsungs pa gnyis paN+Di ta pA ra he ta dang/ lo tsA ba nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'di sngar gyi dang 'gyur
37a2(dkar chag): la mi 'dra ba'i khyad chen po 'dug pas bris/ gtor ma'i cho ga nyung du dang/ zhing gi dbang phyug ma'i mchod pa'i rim pa/ paN+Di ta pAr he ta dang/ lo tsA ba nag tshe shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ de kho na nyid kyi tshig le'ur byas pa'i man ngag dang/ de'i 'grel ba slob dpon su dza ya sh+rI b+ha
37a3(dkar chag): das mdzad pa gnyis/ mahA mA ya'i rdzogs rim de dang cha 'dra bar 'dug na'ang/ nag tsho'i lugs la/ oDyan sgrol ma'i rdzogs rim du bzhed do/ /gnas chen brgyad kyi lha mo sgrol ma la bstod pa/ slob dpon mi bskyod rdo rjes mdzad pa ste gsum paN+Di ta pA ra he ta dang/ lo tsA ba nag cha
37a4(dkar chag): shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ zhing gi dbang phyug ma'i bstod pa blon po'i rigs shin tu dga' ba'i paN+Di tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ye shes rdo rje dang/ lo tsA ba nag tsho chen po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje dril bu'i mtshan nyid dang/ thod pa mchod pa'i cho ga gnyis/ paN+Di ta pAr he ta dang/ lo
37a5(dkar chag): tsA ba nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'di oDyan sgrol ma'i chos skor du mdzad do/ /rmi lam sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon zla ba'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ga ta sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i 'chi kha ma'i man ngag paN
37a6(dkar chag): chen shAkya sh+rIs? mdzad pa/ de nyid dang lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'phags ma sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shA kya sh+rI bA dra dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa
37a7(dkar chag): 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs kha che paN chen gyis mdzad pa/ dpyal padmo can gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa paN+Di ta zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa tshig rkang bcu gnyis pa/ sgrol ma u pre tA ra'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di 'dod byams brtan ? ta
37b1(dkar chag): nags kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang po tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma drag mo'i sgrub thabs rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang chos 'khor lo tsA'i 'gyur/ ral gcig ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ sgrol
37b2(dkar chag): ma'i gtong chog bsdus pa/ sgrol ma ral gcig ma'i blo 'phel rtag pa rdo rjes mdzad pa gsum/ dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ ral gcig ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rol pa'i sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ ral gcig ma dmar mo'i sgrub thabs kun
37b3(dkar chag): spangs rdo rje zhes bya bas mdzad pa paN+Di ta mi dbang bzang po dang/ legs pa'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ ral gcig ma dmar mo'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga nag po spyod pa bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mi dbang bzang po dang/ gzhon nu shes rab kyi 'gyur/ mchog gi sgrol ma ral gcig ma'i sgrung thabs
37b4(dkar chag): paN+Di ta dA na shI la dang/ khu rnal 'byor pa'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma lha lnga'i sgrub thabs rin po che gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ratna da ti dang/ lo tsA ba rma ban gyi 'gyur/ thugs rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs dngos grub phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes
37b5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yong rdo rje dang/ pa ri lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i nang gi gtor chog slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa dang/ phyir bzlog gi 'khor lo dang/ sgrol ma gsang grub slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rnams/ paN+Di ta ratna da ti dang/ rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ thugs
37b6(dkar chag): rje sgrol ma las sna tshogs kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ khwa gdong ma srang mda' nag mo zhes bya ba slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i man ngag me long dangs pa zhes bya ba/ rma dang/ ba ri'i 'gyur/ de rnams sgrol ma rnal 'byor bla med du bkral ba'i skor
37b7(dkar chag): rnams so/ /ma rgyud spyi dang 'brel pa la oDyan gyi rnal 'byor ba dang/ rnal 'byor ma'i rang byung gi longs spyod dur khrod kyi rtog ba zhes bya ba birba? pas mdzad pa las btus pa/ bradz+nyA sh+rI dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ slob dpon don yod rdo rjes mdzad pa'i rjes chags kyi sbyor bas de kho na nyid
38a1(dkar chag): kyi rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag ces bya ba dang/ las kyi phyag rgya brtag pa'i man ngag gnyis paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dbang chos kyi rten 'brel 'gro ldog nA dngos mdzad pa/ bla ma te pu pa dang/ rma ban gyi 'gyur/ byang chub kyi
38a2(dkar chag): rgyud du ma dang 'brel yang khyad par ma rgyud rdo rje rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa'i 'chi ba blu ba'i man ngag shlo ka sum brgya phrug cu pa/ jo bo rdo dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di phyi nang gi
38a3(dkar chag): rgyud du ma dang 'brel yang khyad par ma rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro dang/ gdan bzhi dang 'grel par snang bas 'dir bkod do/ /rmi lam brtag pa pi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ pad+ma dra ba dpal 'byung gi sgrub thabs rgyal ba dpal ye shes kyi mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta su man sh+rI dang/
38a4(dkar chag): bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ pad+ma dra ba'i rim pas bcom ldan 'das kyi dkyil 'khor mchod pa'i cho ga rgyal ba dpal ye shes ming gzhan pad+ma rdo rje zhes bya ba bas mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po su man sh+rI b+ha bra dang/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen
38a5(dkar chag): grub kyi 'gyur/ /ma rgyud dang phyogs mthun pa mgon po nag po'i skor la/ nag po chen po'i rgyud drag po'i brtag pa dur khrod chen po zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa dang/ nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dngos grub rin chen 'byung gnas
38a6(dkar chag): zhes bya ba dang/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga ye shes kyi me sbyar ba dang gnyis paN+Di ta sa man+ta sh+rIs mdzad pa de nyid dang/ rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po yab yum can gyi sgrub thabs klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes
38a7(dkar chag): kyi 'gyur/ dpal nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa dang/ mgon po bya rog gdong can gyi nang sgrub dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta A b+ha yA ka ra gupta dang/ lo tsA ba rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs bram ze
38b1(dkar chag): mcho sred kyis mdzad pa/ byin gyis brlab pa'i nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs sha ba ri pas mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor du dbang skur pa'i chog /bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nag po ro 'dzin dang/ gyi ljang dbu dkar po'i 'gyur/ mgon
38b2(dkar chag): po nag po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba pradz+nya kI rti'i 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i gter chog dI paM ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa de nyid ding/ 'brom ston pa'i 'gyur/ lha mo nag mo'i sgrub thabs lo ka sh+rI 'gyur/
38b3(dkar chag): lha mo rim tI dmag zor gyi man ngag /A tsAdya dmar po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ yang nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs cha gnyis/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa rkang brgyad 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ nag
38b4(dkar chag): po chen po'i bstod pa a ba d+hU tI bas mdzad pa/ nag po chen po la bstod bskul sangs rgyas grags pas mdzad pa/ bya rog ming can dang/ bya rog gdong can la bstod pa/ rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags pas mdzad pa se lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'di gnyis rtsom mkhan bod kyis
38b5(dkar chag): brtsams pa yin kyang/ saM skri ta'i skad du brtsams shing/ bod skad du bsgyur ba yin pas/ sngar gyi rnams kyis bris 'dug pas bris so/ /nag po chen po'i bstod pa rkang pa brgyad pa paN+Di ta bai ro tsA na badzra dang ding ri chos grags kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa brgyad pa
38b6(dkar chag): gru sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ dung sol ma'i sgrub thabs nA ro pas mdzad pa lo ka sh+rI'i 'gyur/ dpal ldan lha mo nag mo la bstod pa brgyad pa zhes bya ba bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so/ /sgrol ma bla med skor la lnga bcu drug /ma rgyud spyi 'grel bdun dang bad dra'i gnyis/
38b7(dkar chag): mgon? po nag po'i skor la nyi shu ste/ /gril pas chos skor brgyad cu rtsa lnga bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ sgrol ma la sogs pa'i skor gyi le'u ste dgu pa'o// //rnal 'byor chen po thabs kyi
39a1(dkar chag): rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa'i skor la/ dang po mngon po klu sgrub kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i 'phags skor la// //sha pa la gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon chen po klu sgrub kyi mdzad zer ba'i le'u bcu bdun
39a2(dkar chag): pa yan chad man+ta ka la shu'i rang 'gyur/ le'u bco brgyad pa gzhon nu bum pa'i rang 'gyur gnyis bzhugs so/ /'grel pa 'di slob dpon klu sgrub kyi mdzad ma mdzad rtsod pa can du 'dug na'ang/ bod ma ma yin par 'dug cing mtshan bzang po la g.yar 'dug
39a3(dkar chag): pa'i don la dbu ru bzhugs so bcug pa yin no// //sa pa la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i 'grel pa sgron ma gsal ba zhes bya ba'i rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin
39a4(dkar chag): chen bzang po'i 'gyur la/ 'gos kyi g.yang khral cung zad 'tshal ba las slar yang zhus chen bgyis pa'i 'gyur gsum la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA? ka ra warma dang/
39a5(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang 'dus rgyud phyi ma le'u brgyad pa'i 'grel pa thams cad kyi sgron ma/ paN+Di ta snyan grags bzang pos mdzad pa/ smri ti'i rang 'gyur 'di the tshom gyi gzhi zhig snang ngo// //ha pa la rgyud
39a6(dkar chag): dgongs pa lung ston gyi nang gi rdo rje bzlas pa'i rgya cher bshad pa zhes bya ba dang/ ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa'i rgyud las 'byung ba'i rgyan bdun rnam par bkrol ba dang gnyis/ sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rmas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sgron ma
39a7(dkar chag): gsal bar byed pa'i gsal byed ces bya ba'i dka' 'grel zhes bya ba slob dpon thugs rje'i dpal gyi zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ sgron ma gsal ba mdor bshad pa'i sa gcod snying gi me long zhes bya ba/ mkhas
39b1(dkar chag): pa ku mA ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gzhon nu bum pa dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ sgron ma gsal ba'i dka' ba btus pa'i 'grel pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon legs ldan 'byed kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rgya ba mchog dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyi
39b2(dkar chag): 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //a ki gnyis la/ sgron gsal gyi TIk+ka dgongs pa rab gsal zhes bya ba/ slob dpon b+ha bya kIrti'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa shlo ka stong phrag bcu drug pa/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra'i rang 'gyur/ sgron gsal le'u dang
39b3(dkar chag): po'i 'grel bshad slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad zer ba 'di bod ma 'dra bar 'dug na'ang/ sngar gyi rnams kyis bris 'dug pas bris so// //khi pa la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad rgyud rdo rje phreng ba'i rgya cher 'gral pa zab mo'i don
39b4(dkar chag): gyi 'grel pa zhes bya pa paN+Di ta a laM ka ka la shas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ steng pa lo tsA bas bsgyur ba las/ le'u bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi pa'i phyed yan chad kyi 'grel pa ji tsam rnyed pa bzhugs so/ /'di'i 'phrod rung du yang btsal bar bya'o/ /de ltar rgyud
39b5(dkar chag): 'grel gyi skor rnams bkod nas/ da ni sgrub thabs dkyil chog man ngag la sogs pa'i skor la// //gi pa la sgrub pa'i thabs mdor byas pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur
39b6(dkar chag): sgrub pa'i thabs mdo dang bsres pa zhes bya ba slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nyi shu pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad zer ba/ paN+Di ta su b+hA sh+rI ta dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen
39b7(dkar chag): bzang po'i 'gyur/ dbang bzhi pa'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAn+ti garb+ha dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i byang chub sems kyi 'grel pa tshigs bcad ma/ paN+Di ta gu Na A kA ra dang/
40a1(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rab zhi ba shes gnyen gyi 'gyur la/ phyis paN+Di ta kan ka wa rma dang/ pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bcos pa/ byang chub sems 'grel lhug pa ma paN+Di ta dza ya A nanda dang/ lo tsA ba khu mdo sde 'bar? gyi 'gyur/ rdzogs rim rim pa
40a2(dkar chag): lnga pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur la/ yang paN+Di ta ka ma la gupta dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bcos pa/ rim lnga'i don 'grel spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma slob dpon Arya de bas
40a3(dkar chag): mdzad pa paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ shlo ka stong sum brgya pa /sems la dmigs pa'i rim pa'i don 'grel sems kyi sgrib pa sbyong ba'i rab tu byed pa zhes bya ba 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa paN+Di ta dz+nyA na kA ra dang/ lo
40a4(dkar chag): tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ sgyu lus kyi don 'grel bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba dang/ 'od gsal gyi don 'grel mngon par byang chub pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba gnyis/ slob dpon Arya de bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rd+d+hyA ka ra warma
40a5(dkar chag): dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i ro sreg gi cho ga slob dpon Arya de bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ slob dpon Arya de bas mdzad zer ba'i yar la ha la sogs tshul
40a6(dkar chag): bzhir bshad pa/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ bskyed rim rnam gzhag rim pa/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nyi shu pa paN+Di ta thig le bum pa dang/ lo tsA ba pa tsha ba nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ las kyi mdza' rnam par 'byed
40a7(dkar chag): pa slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma Ni ka sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ paN+Di ta de wen+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa rim pa lnga'i khongs su bsdu ba zhes bya ba slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta A laM ka ka la sha dang/
40b1(dkar chag): lo tsA ba nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa rnal 'byor yid 'phrog /ma ga d+ha'i paN+Di ta thub pa dpal bzang pos mdzad pa/ dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po'i phyag dpe'i rgya dpe las bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon zla ba grags
40b2(dkar chag): pas mdzad pa'i rdo rje sems dpa' i sgrub thabs 'di sgrub pa mdor byas kyi 'grel pa rin chen 'phreng ba'i gsham na yod pa/ zhes bya ba shlo ka rkang pa dang bcas pa'i brgya phrag gnyis pa/ paN+Di ta ta thA ga ta rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsA ba klog skya gzhon nu 'bar gyi 'gyur la/ slad kyi 'chi? ta pI paM
40b3(dkar chag): ka rar? k+Shi ta dang/ ba ri lo tsA bas bcos pa/ rdo rje sems dpa' i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa la li badzro'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ bi b+hA ti tsan+d+ra'i rgya dpe la bltas nas/ lo tsa' ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ khro bo bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sgrub thabs dpal ldan
40b4(dkar chag): zla ba gags pas mdzad pa paNdita sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i mngon par rtog pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa zhes bya ba slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad zer ba 'di ni the tshom gyi gzhi cig snang ngo/ /gsang 'dus kyi dkyil
40b5(dkar chag): 'khor gyi cho ga shlo ka phyed dang brgyad brgya pa slob dpon sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas
40b6(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur rdo rje sems dpa' mchod pa'i cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ nag po pas mdzad pa'i rab gnas
40b7(dkar chag): 'gos kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje 'chang chen po'i lam gyi rim pa slob dpon sgra dbyangs bcu gcig pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i gtor chog za hor gyi mkhas pa shAn+ta de bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang 
41a1(dkar chag): lo tsA ba 'gos kyi 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i sbyin sreg gi tshig /slob dpon rang 'jigs rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ da ni sgrub skor de dag gi 'grel pa'i
41a2(dkar chag): skor la/ sgrub thabs mdor byas kyi 'grel pa rin chen 'phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ karma badzra'i rang 'gyur/ sgrub pa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba dz+nya? na badzras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra dang/ lha btsun pa'i 'gyur/
41a3(dkar chag): dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha'i sku la bstod pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug mi gnas rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rd+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ byang chub sems 'grel gyi rnam bshad smri tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid kyi
41a4(dkar chag): 'gyur dang pa smra ba zhes bya bstod pa rin chen bzang pa'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //di pa la sgrub thabs mdor byas dang rim lnga gnyis ka'i 'grel ba slob dpon b+ha bya kI rtis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rgyal ba mchog dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyi
41a5(dkar chag): 'gyur/ rim lnga'i bshad pa nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon klu byang gi mdzad zer ba/ paN+Di ta karma badzra dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ 'di'i phyi mo slar rnyed na rdzong 'di slob dpon klu byang gi mdzad ma mdzad the tshom za bar 'dug kyang/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di
41a6(dkar chag): tas mdzad par 'dug pas bris so/ /rim lnga'i 'grel pa nag po dam tshig rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ rim lnga'i dka' 'grel don gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon brtson 'grus bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/
41a7(dkar chag): lo tsA ba shes rab brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i dgongs 'grel zla ba'i 'od zer zhes bya ba slob dpon a d+ha yA kA ra guptas mdzad pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ras rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/ /sgrub thabs mdor byas kyi dka' 'grel/ paN+Di ta bi? b+hu ti tsan+d+ras mdzad pa/ bod kyi lo tsA
41b1(dkar chag): ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa don gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba klu'i byang chub kyi mdzad zer ba 'dir rdzun ma yin par 'dug na'ang/ sngar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris 'dug pas bris so/ /spyod bsdus sgron ma'i bshad pa slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen
41b2(dkar chag): gyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa'i rdo rje sems dpa' i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa/ ta thA ga tas mdzad pa/ dI pika ra rak+Shi ta dang/ khams pa ba ri lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa kha che'i paN+Di ta lag smris mdzad pa paN+Di ta chen po tar ka la sha'i
41b3(dkar chag): sras man+ta ka la sha nyid kyi bsgyur ba rnams bzhugs so// //de ltar 'phags skor la 'grel pa bco lnga dang/ sgrub thabs la sogs kyi skor sum cu rtsa brgyad de/ chos skor lnga bcu rtsa gsum mo/ /slob dpon ye shes zhabs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i gsang ba
41b4(dkar chag): 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi skor gyi rgyud kyi 'grel ba'i sgor la// //ci ba la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi le'u bco brgyad pa'i phyed kyi rtsa ba'i rgyud rdzogs pa'i 'grel pa man ngag gtan la dbab pa zhes kyang bya/ slob ma la phan pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rab tu
41b5(dkar chag): zhi bu'i ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ 'di slob dpon ye shes zhabs kyi dngos slob tshe 'di nyid la mya ngan las 'das pa'i gang zag bzhi'i ya gyal rab tu zhi ba'i bshes gnyen dang gcig mi gcig dpyad do/ /le'u bco brgyad pa'i phyed kyi rtsa ba'i rgyud rdzogs pa man chad kyi
41b6(dkar chag): bgal pa slob dpon bi shwa mi tras mdzad pa/ gsang 'dus rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon tha gnas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang d+harma badzra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //chi ba la gsang 'dus rtsa
41b7(dkar chag): rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa'i 'grel pa rin po che'i ljon shing zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po tse lu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka ma la gu hya dang/ lo tsA ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ gsang 'dus rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa/ rgyud phyi ma le'u bco brgyad
42a1(dkar chag): pa dang bcas pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon sman pa'i bu rgyal bas byin gyis mdzad pa gnyis bzhugs so// //ji pa la gsang 'dus le'u bcu bdun pa'i 'grel pa dri ma med spas bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pu N+ya sh+rI mi tra dang/ lo tsA
42a2(dkar chag): ba dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ le'u bco brgyad pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon zla ba'i 'od kyis mdzad pa/ pu N+ya sh+rI dang/ dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ yang dag rig byed ces bya ba rgyud phyi ma rnam par bshad pa slob dpon sman pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kam la
42a3(dkar chag): gu hya dang/ lo tsA ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad sbyar snyim pa'i me tog ces bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa'i le'u bcu gsum pa yan chad rnams bzhugs so// //
42a4(dkar chag): nyi pa la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad sbyar snyim pa'i me tog gi le'u bcu bzhi pa man chad/ paN+Di ta shAn+tA badzra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa'i 'grel pa zla ba'i 'od zer
42a5(dkar chag): zhes bya ba slob dpon dga' ba'i 'byung gnas go chas mdzad pa/ 'di ye shes zhabs kyi rjes su 'brang bya ba'i dmigs bsal mi 'dug na'ang/ lha'i skyed cho ga la sogs ye shes zhabs lugs dang mthun par byung zhing/ sngar gyi mkhas pa dag gis
42a6(dkar chag): kyang ye shes zhabs lugs kyi phyogs su bris 'dug pas 'dir yang de bzhin bris so/ /de ltar rgyud so so'i 'grel pa rnams bkod nas/ spyi'i man ngag la sogs pa'i sgrub skor la// //ti pa la rim pa gnyis pa zhes bya ba'i de kho na nyid bsgom
42a7(dkar chag): pa'i zhal gyi lung/ 'jam dpal zhal lung chen por grags pa sangs rgyas dpal ye shes zhabs kyis bsdus pa/ paN+Di ta ka ma la gu hya dang/ lo tsA ba lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ zhal gyi lung chung ba sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis
42b1(dkar chag): bsdus pa dang/ sgrub thabs kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta shud+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bsnyen bsgrub yan lag bzhi'i sgrub thabs kun tu bzang mo zhes bya ba sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis
42b2(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ smri ti dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ he ru ka'i sgrub thabs slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ de'i rang 'grel/ 'di gsum la sgrub pa'i thabs kun tu bzang mo gsum zhes zer ro/ /grol ba'i thig le sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad
42b3(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di ta ka ma la gu hya dang/ la tsA ba lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ bdag grub pa la 'jug pa slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAn+ta badzra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ chu sbyin dbang po'i sgrub thabs gsum slob
42b4(dkar chag): dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta dza ya sen dang/ lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ sbyin sreg gnyis kyi cho ga dang/ gtor cho ga mi nub pa'i sgron ma dang/ tshogs 'khor gyi 'khor lo sna tshogs 'khor lo dang/ rin chen 'bar ba dang/ rtsa
42b5(dkar chag): ba'i ye shes chen po dang/ tshigs su bcad pa'i mdzod dang/ byang chub sems kyi thig le dang/ bkra shis kyi rnam bshad chen po dang/ rgyud kyi rnam bshad dang/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho gnyis brgya lnga bcu pa rnams la lung dang mthun pa'i chos bcu bzhi zhes bshad
42b6(dkar chag): ? la/ rgyud kyi rnam bshad ni ma mdzad/ dkyil cho ga ni kha cher khyer nas/ rgya gang na med par bshad/ gzhan rnams la gong du smos ba rnams ma gtogs pa bod du 'gyur ba mi snang ngo/ /stad stabs kyi bkod pa slob dpon chen po ye shes zhabs kyi zhal snga nas

61a6(dkar chag): 'byor skyangs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dpal ldan rgya che ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil chog /kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga rab gnas kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba
61a7(dkar chag): rdo rje 'byung ba'i 'grel pa rdo rje 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i don bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mu nin+d+ra b+ha dras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi don bsgom pa'i don bsdus pa/ ku mA
61b1(dkar chag): rak la sha'i 'gyur/ bya ba bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rigs kyi byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kIrti tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'di rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yin pas 'dir bris so/ /de nyid bsdus pa dpal mchog dang po
61b2(dkar chag): dang/ /sgyu 'phrul dra ba la sogs dgongs 'grel ba'i/ /mkhas grub gsum gyi gzhung lugs rjes 'brang bcas/ /bcu phrag gnyis la bdun gyis brgyan pa bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ rnal 'byor gyi
61b3(dkar chag): rgyud de nyid bsdus pa dang/ dpal mchog dang/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i skor gyi le'u bcu drug pa'o// //rtsa ba'i rgyud de nyid bsdus pa'i rdo rje dbyings kyi dum bu las 'phros pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du bkral ba'i skor la// //
61b4(dkar chag): si pa la mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa 'grel chung zhes grags pa/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'grel pa bar ma mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgya cher
61b5(dkar chag): bshad ba mtshan gsang sngags kyi don du rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa shlo ka nyis stong lnga brgya pa/ smri ti'i rang 'gyur la/ phyis paN+Di ta badzra pA Ni dang/ klog skya shes rab brtsegs kyis bcos pa la yang gnyan gyis bcos/
61b6(dkar chag): mtshan brjod 'brel chen slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ ka ma la gupta dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/ //hir la mtshan brjod 'grel pa zla ba bzang po gragS
61b7(dkar chag): ba'i dpal gyis mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta sh+rI mahA dza na dang/ lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel ba bsdus pa'i gsal ba zhes bya ba o rgyan gyi slob dpon a ba d+hU tI pas mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi
62a1(dkar chag): bzang bo'i 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa mtshan don gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba slob dpon gnyis med sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'jam dpal
62a2(dkar chag): mtshan brjod kyi bshad 'bum smri tis mdzad pa de nyid kyi rang 'gyur / mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i man ngag gi 'grel pa slob dpon gzhon nu grags pas mdzad pa / paN+Di ta de wa rA dza dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab bla ma'i 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag
62a3(dkar chag): par brjod pa'i 'grel pa gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ bla ma mngon shes can dang/ 'gos lhas btsas dang/ shes rab brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa tshul gsum gsal bar byed pa'i
62a4(dkar chag): sgron ma zhes bya ba/ 'di gnyis rgyud sde spyir bkral bar bya zhing the tshom gyi gzhi'o/ /mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa DoM bi he ru kas mdzad pa/ dge tshul khyung grags kyi 'gyur /'di'ang the tshom gyi gzhi zhig snang/ 'jam dpal gyi 'grel pa ratna A kA ra
62a5(dkar chag): guptas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kA la tsakra dang/ lo tsA ba dz+nyA na garb+ha? dang/ 'brog jo sras dang/ chos kyi brtson 'grus la sogs pa'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/ /de ltar mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa'i skor rnams bkod nas/ da ni de dag gi rjes su 'brang
62a6(dkar chag): ba'i sgrub thabs dang/ dkyil cho ga dang/ man ngag gi skor la// //i pa la mtshan brjod 'grel pa chung ba'i rjes su 'brangs pa nam mkha' dri med chung ba zhes grags ba'i skor la/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i dkyil 'khor
62a7(dkar chag): gyi cho ga nam mkha' dri ma med ces bya ba rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil chog dang / yang dkyil chog 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs dang/ byang sems rdo rje dbugs 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi chog dang/ rnam par snang mdzad dbugs dbyung ba'i
62b1(dkar chag): dkyil 'khor gyi chog dang/ mi bskyod pa dbugs 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang/ snang ba mdza' yas dbugs 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang/ rin chen 'byung ldan dbugs 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang/ don yod grub pa dbugs
62b2(dkar chag): 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i khrus kyi cho ga /mtshan brjod kyi chu sbyin dang/ zas kyi rnal 'byor dang/ 'byung po'i gtor chog /maN+Dal gyi cho ga /skor ba bya thabs/ yan lag bdun pa'i tshogs bsag pa'i thabs/
62b3(dkar chag): mtshan brjod gdon pa'i man ngag /dge ba'i rtsa ba bsngo ba'i man ngag /mi rtag pa bsgom pa'i man ngag /'khor ba las yid 'byung ba'i man ngag/ shes pa dus gsum las bzlog pa'i man ngag /skyabs su 'gro ba'i cho ga /sems bskyed pa'i cho ga/
62b4(dkar chag): byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i man ngag tshad med pa bzhi bsgom pa'i man ngag /dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas la lta ba'i man ngag /dbang po thams rjes su dran pa drug bsgom pa'i man ngag /dbang po 'bring gis rten 'brel yan lag bcu gnyis bsgom pa'i
62b5(dkar chag): man ngag /dbang po rab kyis de kho na nyid bsgom pa'i man ngag /sAts+tsha gdab pa'i cho ga /sbyin sreg gi cho ga bsdus pa/ mnyam par bzhag pa'i rim pa'i man ngag /dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ mtshan brjod kyi cho ga mdo dang bsres pa/ rab
62b6(dkar chag): tu gnas pa'i cho ga /ngan sngags byad kyi 'khor los bsad pa'i cho ga /tshe 'phos pa la phan gdags pa'i bdun tshigs kyi cho ga /sdig pa sbyong ba'i sbyin sreg ro sreg gi cho ga ngan song sbyong ba 'gro ba rigS drug gi cho ga rnams slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes
62b7(dkar chag): gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su badzra dang / lo tsA ba gu rub chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur / 'di'i la la rgya gzhung yin min the tshom za bar 'dug na'ang /bla ma gong ma rnams rgya gzhung du bzheng cing /sngar gyi rnams la'ang bris 'dug pas bzhugs
63a1(dkar chag): su bcug pa yin /slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i byang chub sems kyi bsgom don bcu gnyis pa tshigs su bcad pa bzhi ? pa'i 'grel pa/ 'di mdo phyogs su bzhed pa mi 'thad de/ gzhung nas
63a2(dkar chag): rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du gsal bar gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /'grel pa bar pa'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i skor la/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i gsang ba dang ldan pa'i sgrub thabs/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa bklag pa'i sgom khog /rim pa gnyis
63a3(dkar chag): kyis phye ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rgyas pa/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yon tan 'byung gnas zhes bya ba rnams slob dpon dpal ldan byang chub mchog gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta smri ti'i rang 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rab gnas kyi cho ga/
63a4(dkar chag): slob dpon shAn+ta girb+has? mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs gsang ldan gyi 'grel pa ye shes gsal ba/ sgrub thabs gsang ba ldan pa'i thig gi cho ga rab tu gnas pa dang gsum smri tis mdzad cing de nyid kyis rang 'gyur du bsgyur ba/ 'phags pa 'jam
63a5(dkar chag): dpal gyi sgrub thabs dge bsnyen ma snyan grags dge mas mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal rin po che'i sgrub thabs dge bsnyen ma grags sbyin mas mdzad pa smri ti dz+nyA na kArti'i rang 'gyur/ mtshan brjod 'grel chen gyi skor / nam mkha' i dri med che ba'i dkyil
63a6(dkar chag): chog slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+ha ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ de dag dang rjes su mthun pa/ 'jam dpal rdo rje 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sems can thams cad kyi bde ba bskyed pa zhes
63a7(dkar chag): bya ba rnams bzhugs so// //ku pa la mtshan brjod 'grel pa chung ba'i skor byang chub sems kyi sgom don bcu gnyis pa slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i cho ga mdo dang bsres
63b1(dkar chag): pa zhes bya ba slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa bar pa'i skor gsang ldan gyi dka' 'grel don bsdus sgron ma zhes bya ba paN+Di ta de wa a kA ra tsan+d+ra dang/ klog skya'i 'gyur/ gsang ldan gyi tho yig don bsdus su
63b2(dkar chag): mdzad pa smri tis mdzad pa de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi dkyil chog slob dpon shAn+ti garb+has mdzad pa smri ti'i rang 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi sgrub thabs gsang ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba pradz+nyA gu rus mdzad pa/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'khor lo'i
63b3(dkar chag): rim pa/ mtshan brjod kyi sgrub thabs rdo rje las sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba slob dpon zla bzang grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mahA dze na dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims gzhon nu'i 'gyur/ mtshan
63b4(dkar chag): brjod 'grel pa a ba d+hU tI pa'i rjes su 'brang ba'i skor la/ 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs dang/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ye shes gsal ba zhes bya ba dang/ 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' de kho na nyid kyi sgrub thabs dang gsum/ slob dpon
63b5(dkar chag): gnyis med sbas pas mdzad pa/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon mya ngan med ba'i dpal gyis mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' dang po'i sangs rgyas kyi sgrub thabs dang/ mchod rten grub pa'i cho ga gnyis slob dpon a ba d+hU tI pas mdzad
63b6(dkar chag): pa/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs paN+Di ta a sho sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba ? zha rgya gar brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje dgra nag gi sgrub thabs/ mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs/ gtor ma'i cho ga /spyod lam la sogs
63b7(dkar chag): pa'i rnal 'byor/ bum pa'i cho ga rnams slob dpon mya ngan med pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa/ ye shes sems dpa' i sgrub thabs slob dpon gnyis med sbas pas mdzad pa/ de rnams paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gar chos bzang gi 'gyur/ 'di'i
64a1(dkar chag): dgra nag 'jigs byed rnams kyang 'di nyid du bzhugs par bya'i gzhan du mi 'khyad bar bya'o/ /mtshan brjod kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon mi g.yo ser ges mdzad pa mar pa do ba'i 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i
64a2(dkar chag): sgrub thabs slob dpon pra b+hA kA ras mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgyud kyi sgrub thabs gnyan dad ma grags kyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod klog pa'i man ngag kha che paN chen gyis
64a3(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ rnam pa nyi shus byang chub pa'i sgrub thabs/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs/ de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /mtshan brjod kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la bstod pa dang bzhi/ paN+Di ta so ma sh+rIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mahA dza na
64a4(dkar chag): dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'ong kyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal gyi gtor chog gcig rnams so/ /mtshan yang dag par brjod pa rnal 'byor gyi/ /rgyud du bkral ba'i 'grel skor bcu gnyis dang/ /sgrub skor la sogs brgyad cu rtsa gsum ste/ /gril bas
64a5(dkar chag): chos skor dgu bcu rtsa lnga bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ /mtshan brjod rnal 'byor gyi rgyud kyi skor du bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o// //thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud kyi bshad
64a6(dkar chag): sbyar gsang ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ /paN+Di ta pradz+nyA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur /rtsa rgyud de nyid bsdus pa'i dum bu gnyis pa khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dum bu las ngan 'gro dgug
64a7(dkar chag): cing sdig pa sbyang ba las 'phros pa ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud kyi skor la /ngan song yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud kyi don gyi 'bru 'grel zhes bya ba slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad zer ba/ 'di paN+Di ta chos gsung ba la lo tsA bas zin
64b1(dkar chag): bris byas pa yin nam yang zer ro/ /'phags pa ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba zhes bya ba /cho ga zhib mo'i rgyal po chen po'i rgya cher 'grel pa snying po rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba dza land+ha ra'i slob dpon kA? ma d+he nus mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bI nA ya tsan+d+ra
64b2(dkar chag): dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //khu pa la ngan song yongs su sbyor ba'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa mdzes pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba slob dpon rdo rje go chas mdzad zer ba shlo ka drug stong dang bcu bzhi pa dang/ ngan song
64b3(dkar chag): yongs su spyod ba'i gzi brjid kyi rgyal po'i brtag pa snang ba'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa/ paN+Di ta bIrya ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba dbang phyug rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur gnyis bzhugs/ sbyong rgyud kyi bshad pa byed lugs chung 'di drag pa 'dra'o// //gu pa la
64b4(dkar chag): ngan song thams cad yongs su spyod ba'i gzi brjid kyi rgyal po'i 'grel pa brtag pa bshad pa zhes kyang bya/ gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad zer ba/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra ka la sha dang/ lo tsA ba khyung po chos brtson gyi 'gyur /dkyil
64b5(dkar chag): 'khor spyi'i rim pa slob dpon su ra b+ha dras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nu'i 'gyur /ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad zer ba gtsug dgu'i gzhung
64b6(dkar chag): dang cha 'dra ba/ paN+Di ta smri ti'i rang 'gyur zer / dpe la la na paN+Di ta su b+hU ti sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang bo'i 'gyur zer ba snang ngo/ /ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i cho ga thugs rje'i phreng ba zhes bya ba
64b7(dkar chag): slob dpon chen bo kun dga' snying pos mdzad zer ba/ paN+Di ta ki ra NA ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba dge tshul khyung grags kyi 'gyur / 'di gnyis snga ma cung drag bar snang ngo/ /ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i ro'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon kun dga' 
65a1(dkar chag): snying bos mdzad zer ba/ paN+Di ta ka na ka warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i lung las ro sbyang zhing sgyeg/ ba'i thabs kyi cho ga mdo dang bsres nas slob dpon kun
65a2(dkar chag): dga' snying bos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ /ngan song thams cad yongs su spyod ba'i thabs zhes bya ba sbyin sreg gi dkyil 'khor gyi chog slob dpon skal bzang dga' bas mdzod pa bla ma ni na sh+rI dang
65a3(dkar chag): lo tsA ba g.yung drung 'od kyi 'gyur/ /gtsug tor dgu'i rgyud la brten pa'i ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga zhes bya ba slob dpon kun dga' snying bos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+hA ? dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang
65a4(dkar chag): bo'i 'gyur 'di rtsod med yang dag pa yin no/ /ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i rim pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas ma zad pa/ many+dzu sh+rI warma dang/ bran ka mu ti'i 'gyur/ ngan song sbyong ba'i ro'i sbyin
65a5(dkar chag): sreg gi dkyil chog slob dpon d+harma kIrtis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma pA la dang/ lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur / slob dpon kun snying gis mdzad ba'i dkyil chog gi 'grel ba bsnyen pa yan chad rdzogs pa'i 'phro zhig 'di bod ma 'dra ba zhig 'dug
65a6(dkar chag): ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris pas bris so/ /ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i cho ga'i bya ba mdor bsdus ba/ ngan song 'dI phyi ma slar rnyed na rdzong/ thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta 'gro kun dga' ba bzang pos
65a7(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ mnga' ris pa rdo rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ba'i snying bo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bai ro tsA na rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsA ba glan chung gi 'gyur la stag las 'di'i byi mo ?  rdzong/ bcos pa/ de la brten nas
65b1(dkar chag): slob dpon dA ri bas mdzad pa'i shes rab snying po'i sgrub thabs/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag rdo rje lta bu zhes bya ba slob dpon kam? las mdzad pa/ ngo? bo rje dang dag ba'i sogs kyi 'gyur/ de kho na nyid gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba kampa la'i yum
65b2(dkar chag): gyis mdzad pa/ mdo rgyas 'bring gi gleng gzhi'i sangs rgyas byang sems rnams rnal 'byor rgyud du dgongs pa bkral te/ dkyil 'khor la bkod nas ston pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga zhes bya ba slob dpon kun dga' snying bos
65b3(dkar chag): mdzad pa dang/ de la brtan nas slob dpon ratna kIrtis mdzad pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /bal bo mahA pA na'i rang 'gyur/ rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga slob dpon dad pa'i 'byung gnas go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka na ka warma
65b4(dkar chag): dang/ lo tsA ba pa tsha ba nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul brgya lnga bcu pa rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du dgongs pa bkral pa slob dpon ye shes bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ yi ge brgya pa'i cho ga slob dpon pad+ma'i rdo rje lcags kyus
65b5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ yang yi ge brgya ba'i cho ga bsdus pa gcig /bzlas pa'i phreng ba'i mtshan nyid dang/ sku khrus kyi cho ga gnyis / paN+Di ta bA ra he ta dang/ nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur / gtsug tor dri med kyi gzungs las 'byung ba'i mchod
65b6(dkar chag): rten sgrub ba'i cho ga rnal 'byor gyi rgyud dang bsdebs nas slob dpon zhi ba snying pos mdzad ba/ las kyi sgrib pa thams cad rgyun gcod par byed pa'i gzungs rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du dgongs pa bkral ba mi 'khrugs pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas pa dang bsdus ba gnyis jo
65b7(dkar chag): po rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur /de'i dkyil chog las kyi sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 
66a1(dkar chag): mi 'khrugs pa'i cho ga'i tho yig slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa dang/ bcom ldan 'das mi 'khrugs pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dze ta ris mdzad pa/ gnyan dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ mi 'khrugs pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga
66a2(dkar chag): jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje chos kyi rnal 'byor gcig pa'i sgrub thabs lo chung legs pa'i shes rab kyis bsgyur ba 'di/ mdzad byang med pas/ sngar gyi rnams kyis bris 'dug pas bzhugs su bcug pa yin /rgyan dam pa sna tshogs pa rim par phye ba zhes
66a3(dkar chag): bya ba'i yi ga'i dkyil chog slob dpon s+thir ma tis mdzad pa/ bam po gcig pa cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur yin zer ba/ 'di rnying ma'am bod ma zhig yin pa 'dra ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris 'dug pas bzhugs su bcug pa yin no//
66a4(dkar chag): thams cad gsang ba ngan song sbyong rgyud dang/ /sher phyin mi 'khrugs pa la sogs pa'i gzhung/ /'grel pa dag dang sgrub thabs la sogs skor/ /bcu phrag gsum la brgyad kyis brgyan pa bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag
66a5(dkar chag): tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ thams cad gsang ba dang ngan song sbyor ba la sogs pa'i skor gyi le'u ste bco brgyad pa'o/ /spyod pa'i rgyud kyi skor la// //du pa la rtsa ba'i rgyud rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud
66a6(dkar chag): kyi bsdus don slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa / paN+Di ta shI len+d+ra po d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/
66a7(dkar chag): skal bzang bab dags mdzad pa'i mchod pa'i chog paN+Di ta padmA ka ra ? rma dang rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgrub thabs rgyal ba'i 'od kyis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// //cu pa la rnam par snang mdzad mngon
66b1(dkar chag): par byang chub pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rtses rang lo tsA bas bcos pa'i 'gyur/ 'jam dpal gsang rgyud kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon lta sbas kyi mdzad pa sgrub thabs kun gyi gter zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra ? rma dang/
66b2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nu'i 'gyur /'jam? dpal gsang rgyud kyi dkyil chog slob dpon don yod zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs khro bo gshin rje gshed? kyi sbyin sreg gi rim pa dang/ dngos grub kyi tshul nges par bstan pa slob dpon don
66b3(dkar chag): yod zhabs kyi mdzad pa/ khro bo rnam par rgyal pa'i rtog pa gsang ba'i rgyud kyi rgya cher bshad pa gsham ma tshang pa gcig rnams bzhugs so/ /rnam snang mngon byang rgyus kyi 'grel pa gnyis/ /'jam dpal gsang ba'i rgyud kyi chos skor bzhi/ /khro bo rnam
66b4(dkar chag): rgyal rtog pa'i 'grel pa gcig /spyod pa'i rgyud kyi chos skor bdun bzhugs so// //bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi skor gyi le'u ste bcu dgu pa'o/ /bya ba'i rgyud kyi skor la// //
66b5(dkar chag): chu ba la bya ba spyi'i rgyud bsam gtan phyi ma rim par phye ba'i bshad pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bidyA ka ra pra b+hA dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ dpung bzang gis zhus pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus don slob dpon sangs rgyas
66b6(dkar chag): gsang bas mdzad pa/ dpung bzang gi zhus pa'i rgyud kyi tshig don bshad pa'i brjed byang/ dpung bzang gis zhus pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus pa'i don dgrol ba'i brjed byang/ 'di bod kyi byas pa yin nam sems/ so so'i dgongs 'grel la/ dang po sku'i rigs
66b7(dkar chag): 'jam dpal gyi skor la /'jam dpal dpa' bo gcig sgrub kyi 'grel pa/ paN+Di ta su b+hA kA ras mdzad pa/ dA na shA la'i rang 'gyur/ gsung gi rigs thugs rje chen po'i skor gyi 'grel pa ni mi snang ngo/ /thugs kyi rigs phyag na rdo rje'i skor la/
67a1(dkar chag): phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi gzungs kyi 'grel pa zhes bya ba slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ phyag na rdo rje'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa paN+Di ta karma badzras mdzad pa/ phyag na rdo rje
67a2(dkar chag): dang phyogs mthun pa rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi skor la/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa mkhan po bo d+hi sa twas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa
67a3(dkar chag): rdo rje sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon pad+ma 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa rin chen gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dpal many+dzu sh+rI 'gyur la/
67a4(dkar chag): slad kyis paN+Di ta 'byon te ta ngul dang/ lo tsA ba dang 'og bsod nams mos pa'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi don rnam par phye ste bshad pa zhes bya ba dang/ de'i rgya cher 'grel pa gnyis/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/ rdo rje
67a5(dkar chag): rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon rdo rje go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi don rnam par bshad pa slob dpon bde ba'i myu gus mdzad pa/
67a6(dkar chag): rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa rnam par 'joms pa'i man ngag ces bya ba smri tis mdzad pa de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel ba rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon sa pa ri bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de
67a7(dkar chag): ba pur+Na ma ti dang/ lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur /rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs rim par phye ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba slob dpon ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sangs rgyas gsang ba dang/ lo tsA ba
67b1(dkar chag): dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur la/ sh+rad+d+hA? dang rin chen bzang pos bcos zer ba / de dag dang 'brel pa'i gtsug tor la sogs pa'i gzungs kyi skor la / kun nas sgor 'jug pa'i 'od zer gtsug tor dri ma med par snang ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po dang
67b2(dkar chag): dam tshig la rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza ya de wa dang/ lo tsA ba langs bande tshul khrims brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar can gyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon shu
67b3(dkar chag): dpag ma badzras mdzad pa/ zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //ju pa la stong chen mo rab tu 'joms pa'i 'bum 'grel / rma bya chen mo'i 'bum 'grel/ gsang sngags rjes su 'dzin pa'i mdo'i 'bum 'grel/
67b4(dkar chag): bsil ba'i tshil gyi mdo'i 'bum 'grel rnams slob dpon las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje'i rang 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //nyu pa la sgo drug pa'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ sgo
67b5(dkar chag): mdza' yas pa bsgrub pa'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa tshig le'ur byas pa dang/ sgo mdza' las pa bsgrub pa'i gzungs kyi rgya cher 'grel ba/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa// paN+Di ta pradz+nyA wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ chos
67b6(dkar chag): spyod thams cad kyi mngon par rtogs pa'i man ngag gi rgyud kyi 'grel pa gzi brjid snang ba zhes bya ba klu'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ dge tshul khyung grags kyi 'gyur/ 'di rtsa 'grel gnyi ga brdzun ma yang dag pa gcig 'dug ste /nag tsho lo tsA ba yang dag
67b7(dkar chag): tu bzhed pa yin zer nas sngar gyi rnams kyi bris 'dug pas 'di yang bzhugs su bcug pa yin/ de ltar bya ba'i rgyud so so'i 'grel pa rnams bkod nas /da ni de dag gi sgrub thabs dkyil chog la sogs pa'i skor la/ bya ba'i rgyud kyi lha sum chen lngar
68a1(dkar chag): grags pa las/ dang po rigs kyi gtso bo gsum la/ sku'i rigs kyi gtso bo rnam par snang mdzad yin pas/ de dang phyogs mthun pa/ dam tshig gsum bkod pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i yi ge brgya pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon kred+ha
68a2(dkar chag): da Na d+his mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dpal go mi 'chi med dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di spyod pa'i rgyud dang bskyed chog rnams mthun par bkod 'dug na'ang/ rgyud 'grel dag las dam tshig gsum bkod bya rgyud du gsungs 'dug pas 'dir
68a3(dkar chag): bris so/ /gsung gi rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dpag med kyi skor la/ tshe dpag med kyi bstod pa/ tshe dpag med kyi sgrub thabs/ tshe dpag med kyi gzungs cho ga rnams slob dpon dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rI many+dzu dang/ lo tsA
68a4(dkar chag): ba lce dga' ba'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ rigs kyi bdag po gsum la/ sku'i rigs kyi bdag po 'jam dpal gyi skor la/ 'jam dpal rdo rje blo gros 'phel ba zhes bya ba 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi dpyad 'phags pa
68a5(dkar chag): lhas mdzad pa/ shlo ka brgya pa/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo gcig sgrub slob dpon mar me mdzad ya shes kyis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal shes rab 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs paN+Ti ta zla ba'i 'byung gnas
68a6(dkar chag): spas da'i mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal g.yo ba'i 'khor lo'i man ngag paN chen shAkya sh+rIs mdzad pa/ ngag gi dbang phyug la bu mo brgyad kyis bstod pa dang/ 'phags pa 'jam
68a7(dkar chag): dpal la khye'u bcu drug gi bstod pa dang/ dag gi dbang phyug gtso 'khor lnga pa'i bstod pa thig le bum pas mdzad pa/ gur gum gzhon nu lta bu'i bstod pa/ slob dpon seng ge mi g.yo bas mdzad pa rnams ni jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 'jam
68b1(dkar chag): pa'i dbyangs kyi bstod pa byin rlabs dang bcas pa zhes bya ba slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sum ti kIrti dang/ lotsA ba blo ldan shes rab dang/ mar? pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po zhes bya ba'i bstod pa slob
68b2(dkar chag): dpon rdo rje mtshon chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta 'bum phrag gsum pa dang/ rdog lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi bstod pa yang dag pa'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba slob dpon phyogs su blang pos mdzad pa/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs kyi cho ga slob dpon
68b3(dkar chag): sh+rad+d+ha ka ra wa rmas mdzad pa/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs slob dpon mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ baN+Di ta bi b+hA ti tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal dkar po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon ma tig mdzad pa/ dA na shI la'i
68b4(dkar chag): rang 'gyur/ a ra pa tsa na'i mchod chog nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsung gi rigs kyi bdag po thugs rje chen po'i skor la/ don yod zhags pa lha lnga'i bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstod
68b5(dkar chag): pa yid 'phrog sdig 'joms zhes bya ba slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ don yod zhags pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha bcu bdun la bstod pa dri ma med pa'i 'od/ 'jig rten mgon po'i bstod pa yid 'phrog sdig 'joms
68b6(dkar chag): slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dA na shI la'i 'gyur / thugs rje chen po la bstod cing bskul ba nyer bzhi pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta par me sha ra dag/ 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug la bstod pa
68b7(dkar chag): slob dpon tsanrya Di bas mdzad pa/ sgra mkhan chen po rgyal ba snyan gyi zhal snga nas dang/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ don zhags lha lnga'i bstod pa paN+Di ta e re btis mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta a mo g+ha badzra dang/ ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/
69a1(dkar chag): 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug la bstod pa grub thob tsarthA Tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstod pa snyan ngag mkhan sh+rI badzra de bas mdzad pa/
69a2(dkar chag): paN+Di ta lak+Sh+mI ka ra dang/ shong ston lo tsA'i 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug la bstod pa dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa/ nor bu gling gi thugs rje chen po lha lnga la bstod pa zhes pa slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ spyan ras gzigs dbang la bstod pa
69a3(dkar chag): slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ thugs rje chen po la smre sngags su gsol ba tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ yang smre sngags su gsol ba slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ snying rje la bstod pa dge bsnyen sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ phyag stong spyan stong
69a4(dkar chag): gi sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI pa ka ra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon pad+mas mdzad ba/ rgyal ba mchog dbyangs kyi 'gyur/ sbyan ras gzigs bcu gcig
69a5(dkar chag): zhal gyi sgrub thabs dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI paM kar sh+rI dz+nyAn dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ spyan res gzigs dbang phyug la bstod pa dge slong ma zla mdzes kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta tsan+d+ra sh+rI dang/ byams pa gling pa'i
69a6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ thugs rje chen po la klu rgyal nor rgyas kyi bus bstod pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ thugs rje chen po'i bstod pa dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug la bstod pa 'jigs
69a7(dkar chag): pa brgyad skyobs dang/ thugs rje chen po la bstod pa dge slong ma 'di'i phyi mo slar rnyed na rdzong dpal mos mdzad pa rnams dang thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs brgya rtsa brgyad pa zhes pa la thog mar/ kha sarpa Ni'i sgrub thabs tshig bcad bzhi pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug
69b1(dkar chag): gi sgrub thabs thugs rje chen po ye shes sems dpa' i sgrub thabs spyan gzigs 'khor lo gsum bsgom/ thugs rje chen po lha lnga'i sgrub thabs 'jig rten mgon po tshad med bzhi'i sgrub thabs/ yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ sems ngal bso ba'i thugs rje
69b2(dkar chag): chen po'i sgrub thabs/ thugs rje chen po yi ge med pa'i sgrub thabs/ stong pa nyid bsgom pa'i man ngag /kha sarbA ni me 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs/ kha sarbA Ni sku gsum gyi gdams pa/ thugs rje chen po mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs / nam mkha' dri
69b3(dkar chag): med kyi sgrub thabs/ nam mkha' mdzod kyi sgrub thabs/ zhal bcu gcig pa'i sgrub thabs / /ba? sarpA Ni ye shes 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ thugs rje chen po yid bzhin nor bu'i sgrub thabs/ thugs rje chen po ? la ke ra'i rtse mo'i sgrub thabs/ dpal
69b4(dkar chag): 'khor lo sgyur ba'i sgrub thabs/ lus kyi 'khor lo 'bar ba dka' thub can gyi sgrub thabs/ rtag tu bya ba'i rnal 'byor/ 'jig rten mgon po sgrub pa'i man ngag/ thugs rje chen po'i gtor ma'i cho ga/ thugs rje chen po'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga /thugs rje chen po'i
69b5(dkar chag): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mchod pa'i cho ga /spyan ras gzigs kyi smon lam du bya ba/ sbyan ras gzigs bdud rtsi brnyes pa'i zas kyi cho ga/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug sh+rI mi tra'i gdams pa// lus sbyin pa'i cho ga /thugs rje chen po'i chu sbyin kyi cho ga/
69b6(dkar chag): thugs rje chen po'i chab gtor gyi cho ga /me'i mchod pa'i cho ga /sku gzugs kyi cho ga /sku gzugs dang/ mchod rten gyi cho ga /ye shes spar ba'i gdams pa/ dri ma rnam dag gi cho ga /chags nyams gso ba /ting nge 'dzin myur du bskyed pa'i
69b7(dkar chag): gdams ngag /ting nge 'dzin brtan par byed pa'i gdams ngag/ sems brtan par byed pa byin gyis brlab pa mi zad pa'i cho ga /'khor lo 'bar ba/ ngag gi mthu bskyed pa'i man ngag /gsang sngags myur du 'grub pa'i cho ga /rmi lam di ma med pa'i sgom
70a1(dkar chag): pa/ rmi lam gyi lta ba log pa rnam par bzlog pa/ khro ba bsal ba /thugs rje chen po'i gdug pa 'dul ba'i cho ga /skye bo gdul dka' ba rnams kyi snying gi dregs pa zhi bar byed pa'i man ngag /dpal 'khor lo rnam dag gi//
70a2(dkar chag): sgrub thabs / snying gi dug sbyong ba/ lus kyi 'khor lo bcing ba dang/ 'grol ba'i man ngag /dpal rdo rje thod pa'i dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs /dpal mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa'i sgrub thabs/ kha sarpA Ni pad+ma kha 'byed pa'i man ngag /thugs rje chen
70a3(dkar chag): po'i gzugs brnyan la brten pa'i sgrub thabs/ dpal me tog gdan gyi sgrub thabs/ me tog la brten pa'i sgrub thabs /sbyil bu can gyi sgrub thabs/ thugs rje chen po rje sgra'i sgrub thabs/ nyi zla sgron ma'i cho ga/ /grags pa bskyed pa'i cho ga /gzi
70a4(dkar chag): brjid bskyed pa'i cho ga /sems can mgu bar byed pa'i cho ga /rmi lam ston par byed pa/ yid 'gyod pa bsal ba/ longs spyod mi zad ba sgrub pa'i thabs/ dpag bsam gyi shing can gyi sgrub thabs/ bum pa bzang po can gyi sgrub thabs/lam
70a5(dkar chag): chen po'i sgrub thabs / padmo'i sdong po can gyi sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug wa ti can gyi sgrub thabs/ spyan ras gzigs dri ma 'jig pa'i bum pa'i cho ga /rdo rje 'bar ba srung ba chen po'i man ngag /srung ba'i 'khor lo/ /rang bsrung pa'i cho ga /gzhan
70a6(dkar chag): bskyang? ba'i cho ga /srung skud kyi cho ga /gzhon nu bsrung pa'i cho ga /spyan ras gzigs kyi nang bsrung ba'i cho ga /spyan ras gzigs kyi nad bsal ba'i cho ga/ spyan ras gzigs kyi klu gso ba'i cho ga/ mdze'i nang gso ba/ gzhan las rnam par rgyal ba'i
70a7(dkar chag): gdams ngag /pha rol gyi gnod pa bsrung ba/ pha rol gyi sde gzhom pa/ pha rol dbang du bya ba/ chom rkun bcing ba/ slob ma la shes rab bskyed pa/ sbyan ras gzigs khros khas ser ba bzlog pa'i cho ga rmi lam dri ma med pa bsgom pa/ slob ma byin
70b1(dkar chag): gyis brlab pa'i man ngag /ye shes gzhug pa'i cho ga ting nge 'dzin gyi byin rlabs/ ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bsgyur/ dpal ye shes 'bar ba'i 'khrul 'khor/ skye ba'i sdam? pa'i mog /'chi ba blu ba'i gdams pa// dpal lha'i grong khyer du 'jug pa/ rdo rje skar
70b2(dkar chag): mda'i man ngag /tshe 'das pa la bya ba'i cho ga /ro sreg pa'i cho ga /sbyin sreg gi cho ga /bkra shis kyi cho ga /sAts+tsha gdab pa'i che ga /rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga rnams la brgya dang bzhi'o/ /'di dag la rnal 'byor bla med dang/ rnal 'byor gi khongs su gtogs pa'ang
70b3(dkar chag): snang mong kyi/ thugs rje chen po phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir bris so/ /thugs rje chen po phyag stong spyan stong gi sgrub thabs ta thA ga ta badzras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nyi ma 'byung gnas zla ba dang/ lo tsA ba dge tshul khyung grags kyi 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug yid
70b4(dkar chag): bzhin nor bu 'khor los sgyur ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dzo ta ris mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pur+Na kIrti dang/ sna rnam rdo rje bla ma'i 'gyur / 'jig rten dbang phyug zhal gcig phyag bzhi ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ yi
70b5(dkar chag): ge drug pa'i rgyud kyi rim pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo bstan pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta ma hA dzan dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od kyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug kha sarpA Ni'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta dI pi kar sh+rI dz+nyen dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi

71b1(dkar chag): brjod kyi man ngag dang nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po rdo rje sgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba rnams slob dpon bIrya tsan+d+ras mdzad pa dang/ phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs sh+rad+d+hA kar warmas mdzad pa dang/ rten 'brel rdzas kyi srung ba rnams jo bo rje dang/ rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur/

71b7(dkar chag): phyag na rdo rje gtum pa'i sbyin sreg slob dpon nyin mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ phyag na rdo rje rdo rje snying po zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta dz+nyA na sh+rIs mdzad pa/ gos sngon po can gyi rig sngags gtad pa'i cho ga /paN+Di ta nag po ba dang nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/
72a1(dkar chag): phyag na rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga stong nyid ting nge 'dzin snying rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang/ lo tsA ba ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ khro bo rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sgrub thabs/ de'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga/ gtor
72a2(dkar chag): ma'i cho ga /srung ba'i cho ga las thams cad pa rnams slob dpon ba su ta badzras mdzad pa/ pradz+nyA sh+rIdz+nyA na kI rti'i rang 'gyur/ phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon su tsan+d+ra b+ha dras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi
