88b7(dkar chag): a mo b+ha badzras mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho'i 'gyur/ tshogs bdag chags pa rdo rje'i bstong ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ nag tsho'i 'gyur/ tshogs bdag sgrin gyi sgron ma'i sgrub thabs bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ jo bo rdze
89a1(dkar chag): dang nag tsho'i 'gyur/ tshogs bdag 'jur bgegs sel ba'i sgrub thabs/ in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa jo bo rje dang rgya brtson seng gi 'gyur/ rmugs 'dzin 'tshol ba'i sgrub thabs/ sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dAna shI la'i rang 'gyur/
89a2(dkar chag): dzam b+ha la'i sgrub thabs slob dpon a b+ha yA kA ra guptas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a laM ka de ba dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims 'byung gnas sbras pa'i 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra dang/ chag chos rje dpal gyis bcos pa/ dzam b+ha la la bstod pa btsun
89a3(dkar chag): pa zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mu ti ta sh+rI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas/ pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ dzam b+ha la'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal po a rya ma tis mdzad pa/ gnyan dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ dzam b+ha la'i sgrub thabs/ sbas pa bum 'khyil zhes bya ba slob
89a4(dkar chag): dpon nor sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ dzam b+ha la'i sgrub thabs/ bsdus pa kha che shAkya sh+rIs mdzad pa de nyid dang/ byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ rmugs 'dzin chu'i dbang po la 'phrin
89a5(dkar chag): las nyi shu'i sgo nas khyad par gyis bstod pa/ slob dpon nor 'dzin dpal gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa rmugs 'dzin la bstod pa paN+Di ta dz+nyA na badzras mdzad pa/ 'phags pa dzam+b+ha la'i
89a6(dkar chag): bstod pa/ mi'i dbang po nyi ma rnam par gnon pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ rmugs 'dzin 'tshol ba'i man ngag gi bstod pa dA byang chub sems dpas mdzad pa/ nor rgyun ma'i bstod pa/ paN+Di
89a7(dkar chag): ta dza mA ris mdzad cing/ de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ gnod sbyin gzhan gyis mi thub ba'i sgrub thabs kyi rgyud paN+Di ta dza mA ri'i 'gyur/ rdo rje bkod pa'i rgyud las dkyil 'khor bdun ba'i rim pa rnam par bye ba'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ legs ldan nag
89b1(dkar chag): po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon snang mdzad myu gus mdzad pa/ 'di rnying ma yin pa 'dra'o/ /sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhi sogs kyi/ /spyi yi rnam gzhag sngags kyi theg pa yi/ /dam tshig la sogs gsal bar ston pa'i gzhung/ /bcu phrag gnyis la
89b2(dkar chag): gcig gis brgyan pa bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar? chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ sde snod dang/ rgyud sde spyi'i rnam gzhag dang/ sngags kyi theg pa'i dam tshig la sogs ston pa'i skor gyi le'u ste nyi shu
89b3(dkar chag): rtsa gnyis pa'o// //gnas chen du bgrod tshul dang/ bla ma la gsal ba 'debs pa'i skor la/ po Ta la kar 'gro ba'i lam yig /rje btsun spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a b+hi yu
89b4(dkar chag): ka ta de ba sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ grub thob brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i gsol 'debs bla ma rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ man lung gu ru'i bstod pa/ chos 'byung rab gzigs zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta bi ma la sh+rI sa mdzad pa/ paN+Di
89b5(dkar chag): ta gau ta ma badzra dang/ lo tsA bgrags pa byang chub kyi 'gyur/ maN+Dal dang/ sAts+tsha la sogs nyin zhag phrugs gcig gi chos spyod kyi skor la/ maN+Dal gyi cho ga /slob dpon kaM b+ha la'i zhal sngna nas mdzad pa 'gyur rnying/ slob dpon sangs rgyas
89b6(dkar chag): gsang bas mdzad pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga /dzai ta ri dgra las rgyal bas mdzad pa'i maN+Dal gyi chog /paN+Di ta u tu lo pa dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje gdan par grags pa rin chen 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa'i maN+Dal
89b7(dkar chag): gyi chog /dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon srid gsum rnam par dag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i las dang po pa'i tshogs bsog bya ba'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa slob dpon a b+ha yA kA ras mdzad pa'i byang chub gzhung lam shlo ka sum brgya nyi shu
90a1(dkar chag): rtsa lnga ba/ kha che paN chen dang chag dgra bcom gyi 'gyur/ kha che paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i maN+Dal gyi chog /de nyid dang byams ba'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ gang zag gcig gi nyin gcig gi bya ba de kho na nyid bsdus ba'i man/
90a2(dkar chag): ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon shI la swa b+hI was mdzad ba/ gtor ma'i cho ga sna tshogs kyi skor la/ rgyud sna tshogs las btus pa'i gtor ma'i chog 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta karma badzra dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul
90a3(dkar chag): khrims kyi 'gyur/ chos skyong thams cad kyi gtar ma'i cho ga /slob dpon ba li? A tsaryas mdzad ba/ rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ rgyal po chen po bzhi'i gtor ma'i? cho ga /jo bo rje dang/ dge bshes ston ba'i 'gyur/ gtor mchen
90a4(dkar chag): po'i las kyi rim pa'i 'grel ba/ slob dpon mi bskyod bas mdzad da ni gsar bcug ra kIrti dang lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ gtor ma cha gsum 'bring po sh+rad+d+hA ka ra wa rmas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
90a5(dkar chag): chu gtor 'jam dpal ma'i rtsa ba dza ya se nas mdzad pa/ rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ chu gtor 'jam dpal ma'i 'grel ba/ phyag rgya chen po'i rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/
90a6(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ yang chab gtor 'jam dpal ma'i 'grel ba /bi dA dz+nyA nas mdzad pa paN+Di ta shAn+ti garb+ha dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bdud rtsi 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i gtor chog jo bo rjes mdzad cing bsgyur
90a7(dkar chag): te/ khu dngos grub kyis gtan la phab pa/ chab gtor dri med jo bo rjes mdzad ba/ de nyid dang tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ klu gtor gyi chog jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bkra
90b1(dkar chag): shes dang bde legs su byed ba'i skor la/ dkon mchog gsum gyi bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad slob dpon zla 'od kyis mdzad pa/ rigs lnga'i bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud kyi lha sum cu rtsa bdun gyis bkra shis kyi
90b2(dkar chag): tshigs su bcad pa/ 'phags ma sgrol mas gsungs ba'i bkra shis brgyad ba/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya sh+rI badzra dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims seng ge'i 'gyur/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi bkra shis kyi tshogs su bcad pa rnams bzhugs so/ /bla
90b3(dkar chag): ma'i gsol 'debs nyin zhag phrugs gcig gi /bya rim chos skyod nor lha bkra shis kyi/ /tshigs bcad la sogs bstan bcos dri ma med/ /bcu phrag bzhi la bdun gyis brgyan pa bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag
90b4(dkar chag): tshangs ba'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ las dang bo ba'i bya ba'i rim pa dang/ chos skyong dang/ nor lha dang/ bkra shis la sogs ba'i skor te/ le'u nyi shu rtsa gsum ba'o// //da ni gsar bcug dbang dang grol byed rim gnyis kyi
90b5(dkar chag): cha la gnyer ma kho sna tshogs kyi skor la// //bu ba la rje btsun sangs rgyas la rgyun chags kyi tshigs su bcad bas bstod ba 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa zha lu lo chen gyi 'gyur/ mi pham mgon po'i bstod pa 'chi blu ma
90b6(dkar chag): zhes pa dpal 'jigs med grags bas mdzad pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bstod pa slob dpon klu'i blo'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po nags kyis rin chen dang/ byams pa gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde'i 'gyur/ paN
90b7(dkar chag): chen nags rin gyi thugs dam rten bla ma'i bris thang rgya ba mig de nyid kyis mdzad ba rnams phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa byams pa gling ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde'i 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi snying po'i 'grel pa 'phags pa spyan ras
91a1(dkar chag): gzigs dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po sh+rI b+ha dra bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dbang gi rab tu byed pa zla ba mgon po dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal gyi rang gi ste
91a2(dkar chag): ba'i 'dod ba mdor bstan pa yongs su bstan pa mi'i dbang po grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu sh+rI dang lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong chos grags dpal bzang pos dpal? sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba/ rdo rje'i chag gi rnam par dbye ba paN+Di ta ? yod
91a3(dkar chag): rdo rjes mdzad pa/ ti bu gsang sngags sdong po'i drung du ras chung rdo rje grags kyis zhus shing bsgyur ba las slad kyi paN+Di ta d+ha na shI la'i drung du/ bal po mtsho kha ras pas zhus te spyan drangs pa/ gnyis su med pa'i rnal 'byor zhes bya ba'i dus kyi 'khor
91a4(dkar chag): lo'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po sh+rI kA la tsakrar ti bas mdzad pa/ dus 'khor zhabs ba chung du dang/ lo tsA ba rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags kyi 'gyur/ tshigs bcad bcu pa zhes bya ba'i lam gyi rim pa bud+d+ha guptas mdzad pa/ de'i slob ma burna?
91a5(dkar chag): wa dza la gnyis la zhus te tA ra nA thas bsgyur ba/ dpal 'khor lo sdom ba'i dkyil 'khor rgyas ba'i sgrub thabs yid bzhin nor bu kha che'i paN+Di ta 'jigs med grags bas mdzad pa nA ro ba chen po dang/ mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyis bsgyur ba las slad kyi bsod
91a6(dkar chag): snyoms pa mi bskyod bas bcos pa/ bde mchog nam mkha' lding gi sgrub thabs pradz+nyA rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ bal bo'i mkhan po mu thi ta sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dpa' bo gcig ba'i sgrub thabs g+harb+ha ri bas mdzad pa/ mar ba
91a7(dkar chag): chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dpa' bo gcig pa'i sbyin sreg dang gtor ma'i cho ga g+harb+ha ri pas mdzad pa/ rab gnas kyi cho ga slob dpon mdzes dags mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kI rta dang dge slong pradz+nyA kIrti'i 'gyur/ sbyin srag+gi chog slob dpon sundA?
91b1(dkar chag): ri nandas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po su ma ti kirti dang lo tsA ba seng ge rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs DoM bi he ru kas mdzad pa/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i sgrub ther ? nA ro pas mdzad pa de nyid dang/ mang po chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur ? bde
91b2(dkar chag): mchog rim lnga rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen dang lo tsA ba byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i dbang chog slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+ha ma badzra? dang lo tsA ba
91b3(dkar chag): zhang zhung gi 'gyur/ rtsa ltung gi bshags pa slob dpon in+d+ra bo d+his mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi bstod pa sh+rI dza land+ha ra bas mdzad pa/ 'khor lo bde mchog gi rnam 'phrul dang/ yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i rgyu mtshan bstan pa nA ro bsam zad pa mar
91b4(dkar chag): ba'i 'gyur/ pra khrid lung bstan te lo bas mdzad pa/ chos drug gi man ngag nA ro pa dang mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ gtor ma tshogs mchod kyi rim dang dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi mdzad pa lo chen rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog
91b5(dkar chag): mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud kyi rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang nA ro pa dang mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ chos drug rdo rje'i tshig rkang ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ni gu ma dang/ glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ phyag chen rdo rje'i tshig rkang ye shes kyis mkha' 'gro ma las glan dar
91b6(dkar chag): ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ phyag chen bsam mi khyab te lo pas mdzad pa/ chos spyod mi dge rang grol grub chen rA hu las mdzad pa de nyid dang/ mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom ba'i gsang sgrub ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma ni gu mas
91b7(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang mchog de nyid kyis mdzad pa/ glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'chi med rdo rje'i tshig rkang ni gu mas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rang shar phyag rgya chen po rdo rje'i tshig rkang ni gums mdzad pa/
92a1(dkar chag): blan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ rang grol phyag rgya chen po ni gu mas mdzad pa/ lam khyer gyi chos gsum ye shes kyi DA ki mas mdzad pa glan dang ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ sgyu ma lam rim gyi rtsa ba dang de'i 'grel pa ye shes kyi
92a2(dkar chag): mkha' 'gro ma ni gu mas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ rtsa kha 'byed pa'i man ngag dang/ rtsa rlung sogs bsgom pa/ thabs lam gtum mo bsgom pa/ thabs lam bsgom pa'i rnal 'byor/ 'khrul 'khor te ni gu
92a3(dkar chag): ma'i zhal gdams le tshan lnga/ smon lam bka' rgya ma ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma ni gu mas mdzad pa/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa bcu gsum ma'i dkyil chog paN chen nags rin gyis mdzad pa/ 'gos lo gzhon nu dpal gyis bsgyur ba las/
92a4(dkar chag): slad kyis byams pa gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sdes mdzad pa po/ de nyid kyi spyan sngar zhib tu nyan te gtan la phab pa/ rnam par grol ba'i snye ma zhes bya ba'i glu dza lan+d+ra ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha gupta dang/ sa rgya nA tha/ kam+ba la ni rbA Na sh+rI
92a5(dkar chag): rnams dang/ bod kyi lo tsA ba jo nang kun dga' snying pos bsgyur ba/ de nyid bdun pa'i 'grel ba sangs rgyas sbas pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang kun dga' snying po'i 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil chog dang/ man ngag slob dpon
92a6(dkar chag): dril bu bas mdzad pa/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen dang 'gos lo'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi bstod pa rnal 'byor ba mi bskyod rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dbang gi bya ba mi bskyod rdo rjes mdzad pa gnyis ye shes mkha' 'gro'i rang 'gyur/ bde mchog
92a7(dkar chag): gi bstod pa dan+ta ka /paN+Di ta bir ya b+ha dra dang/ rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ mngon rtogs snying po kha che dgon pa pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i mngon rtogs kyi 'grel ba rnam
92b1(dkar chag): bshad/ snying po kha che dgon pa pa'i gsung bzhin dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog gi mngon rtogs lu i bas mdzad pa'i 'grel ba la ? bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nyi ma'i 'od zer dang/ chos rje dpal gyis
92b2(dkar chag): bsgyur ba/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i TIk+ka dang/ sgrub thabs gnyis slob dpon b+hu su kus mdzad pa/ 'chi blu'i cho ga nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dge slong shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba lu i bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ lo
92b3(dkar chag): tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyis bsgyur ba/ dbang bzhi'i rnam gzhag nags rin gyis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ chos 'khor lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi 'gyur// //phu ba la dpal ha ru ka dang/ phag mo'i ba san+ta ti la ga zhes bya ba slob
92b4(dkar chag): dpon nag po ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i gsang sgrub nA ro pas mdzad pa/ phag mo dbu bcad ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta sha ri bu tras zhal nas gsungs pa bzhin blo brtan bzhi
92b5(dkar chag): pas bsgyur ba/ phag dkar shes rab snang ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po kong kas byin gyi mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nor bu dpal ye shes dang/ lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ mkha' spyod ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs jo bo chen po sh+rI dz+nyAn dI baM ka ras mdzad pa/
92b6(dkar chag): paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo shes rab gsal byed kyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon kong kang rtas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ra tA rak+Shi ta dang/ lo tsAba zhad grub pa dpal bzang gi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs nA ro bas mdzad
92b7(dkar chag): pa/ ma rab chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs A tsArya dmar po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor ma drug gi sgrub thabs paN+Di ta sum ti kIrti dang dag sh+rIs mdzad pa su ma ti kIrti dang/ mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i
93a1(dkar chag): las kyi cho ga slob dpon ra kri tas mdzad pa/ rigs pa 'dzin ma rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta dza ya dang/ lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ phag mo rig pa 'dzin ma rtsen ma'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon gnyis med rod rjes
93a2(dkar chag): mdzad ba/ phag mo don kun grub pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang/ chos 'khor lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rdo rje rnam par sgegs mo zhes pa paN chen nags kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta
93a3(dkar chag): de nyid dang/ byams pa gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sdes bsgyur zhing gtan la phab pa/ phag mo'i bstod pa rim pa gnyis pa paN chen nags rin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ chos 'khor lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje
93a4(dkar chag): phag mo mchod pa'i sgrub thabs ye shes rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa jo nang kun snying gi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rim pa lnga pa zhes pa don pa'i gdams dag /paN+Di ta bud+d+ha gupta dang/ lo tsA ba dza nang kun snying gi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal
93a5(dkar chag): 'byor ma sbas pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta gupta nA tha dang/ jo nang kun snying gi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs snyan ngag mkhan chen po brtse ba can gyis mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta pur+Na nan+ta dang/ jo nang kun snying gi 'gyur/ dpal kyi rdo rje'i dka' 
93a6(dkar chag): 'grel rin chen sbyor ba'i 'phreng ba slob dpon chen po dam tshig rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nag po'i zhabs de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sngags kyi bstan bcos gsang ba'i mdzod ces pa slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/
93a7(dkar chag): paN+Di ta dz+nyA na sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ dpal kye rdo rje'i gtor na ? chog slob dpon sh+rI an nda badzras mdzad pa/ phyag rgya bzhi'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa/ paN+Du ta ga ya d+har dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo
93b1(dkar chag): zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ gsang ba'i dbang gi rab tu byed ba barbi pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+har dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi rgyal bu sprin shugs can dang/ bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas bcas kyi gtan la phab pa/ he ru ka dran pa
93b2(dkar chag): gcig ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon garb+ha ri bas mdzad pa/ dpal mchog tu gyur ba'i ngo bo nyid go 'phang rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin slob dpon rta mchog zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ lhan cig skyes pa grub pa slob dpon dam tshig rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid
93b3(dkar chag): dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ snying po brgya pa Arya de bas mdzad pa/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen dang byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba'i sde'i 'gyur/ go bar byed pa'i snying po brgya ba'i rnam par bshad pa dpal he
93b4(dkar chag): ru ka de ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po nags kyi rin chen dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sdes bsgyur ba/ dgyes ba rdo rje'i lus kyi don rab tu gsal ba slob dpon shan+ti guptas mdzad pa/ jo nang lo tsA ba kun dga' snying
93b5(dkar chag): po'i 'gyur/ dgyes rdor gyi bsdus don cung zad dran pa zhes pa slob dpon shan+ti guptas mdzad pa paN+Di ta pur+Na badzra dang lo tsA ba kun snying gi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i rdzogs rim gyi sgrub thabs/ sbyor ba bsdus pa slob dpon bde ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di

93b7(dkar chag): snying gi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa'i man ngag gsal ba slob dpon dngos grub brnyes pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha gupta dang lo tsA ba kun dga' snying pos bsgyur ba/ rnal 'byor mdor bstan slob dpon rA hul badzra'i
94a1(dkar chag): zhal snga nas zla ba'i snying po la gdams pa/ de kho na nyid bzhi pa DoM bi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha gupta dang/ ni rba na sh+rI'i sngar mar me mdzad kyis 'grel ba dang bstun te twa ra nA thas bsgyur ba/ bdag med ma'i byin rlabs slob dpon
94a2(dkar chag): zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i bstod pa arya de bas mdzad pa/ bdag med ma'i stobs kyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon bde ba chen po'i zhal gyi man ngag/ paN+Di ta pur+Na badzra dang/ jo nang kun dga' snying po'i 'gyur/ ku ru
94a3(dkar chag): kul+le'i sgrub thabs slob dpon ku mA ra bo d+his mdzad pa/ rje btsun ma 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ bai ro tsA na badzra gyi rang 'gyur/ ku ru kul+le'i las sbyor kyi man ngag paN+Di ta don yod rdo

94a5(dkar chag): dz+nyA nas mdzad pa/ dpal sangs rgyas thod ba'i rgyud kyi rdzogs rim rnal 'byor mdor bsdus pa zhi ba sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ni ra ba na sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba kun snying gi 'gyur// //bu pa la dur khrod khu byug rol pa'i rgya cher 'grel ba bdud rtsi'i

94b4(dkar chag): sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ sgyu 'phrul phyag rgya bsam gtan slob dpon bi ma las mdzad pa/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i sgrub thabs rin chen dra ba mngon rdzogs bim la mi tras mdzad pa bod kyi lo tsA ba nyang po klu'i rgyal mtshan dang/ ban ka ra mu rti lcog ro klu'i

95b1(dkar chag): 'od kyi snang ba/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba gsal ba'i me long/ 'jam dpal gshes gnyen gyi lta ba rnam bkod/ pad+ma'i man ngag lta phreng gi 'grel/ sh+rI sid+hi'i thugs kyi sgo lcags/ bde ba gsal mdzad kyi theg chen shes rab kyi rim pa/ d+harma
95b2(dkar chag): bo d+hi'i shes rab sgron ma dang/ bkol mdo bim la'i rang spyi gtan la 'bebs pa mtshan nyid sgron ma/ thig pa'i brdar sha gcod pa thugs kyi sgron ma/ nges don gyi lta ba btsal ba yang dag sgron me/ gtan tshigs sgron me rtsa 'grel/

96a1(dkar chag): skras chen/ khrus lung rgya mtshan rnams dang/ kun snying gi can phreng chen mo/ /de'i 'grel pa bi ma las mdzad pa/ dur khrod bde ba'i gnas kyi mdo byang/ bi ma la'i tshig rkang bcu dgu pa/ dkyil 'khor rgyan gyi lung phran/

98a4(dkar chag): paN+Di ta d+harma sh+ri mi tra dang/ dpyal chos bzang gi 'gyur/ ngag dbang grags pa'i 'chi blu'i bsdus don gnyis/ man ngag ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa dpe ris dang bcas pa paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra sh+rIdz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/

98a6(dkar chag): nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis bcos pa/ lus ngag yid gsum byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag dang/ sems dpa' gsum gyi ting nga 'dzin la mnyam par bzhag pa gnyis sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa 'gyur gong mtshungs/ 'jam dpal gshin rje
98a7(dkar chag): gshed kyi sgrub thabs 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa sh+rI sid+ha dang/ lo chen bai ro tsa na'i 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i mngon rtogs dngos grub snye ma slob dpon gsang bas byin gyis mdzad/ gshin rje gshed dmar po'i 'khrul 'khor
98b1(dkar chag): gyi de nyid nges bar bshad pa byang chub snying pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ chag lo chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ gshin chog DoM? bi he ru kas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta di k+Shu mang+ga la dang lo tsA ba 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ gshin rje mthar byed kyi 'khrul 'khor gyi cho ga
98b2(dkar chag): paN+Di ta nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang /chag lo chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ yi dwags thams cad rdo rjes bcing pa nag po pas mdzad pa/ pradz+nyA? sh+rI dz+nyA na'i rang 'gyur/ las gshin gyi mchod chog darpaN? a tsaryas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo
98b3(dkar chag): tsA ba zhe sdang rdo rje'i 'gyur/ gshin rje tshe bdag gi sgrub thabs gtor chog /dkyil chog dran pa gsal ba rnams/ paN+Di ta nag po'i zhabs dang/ lo tsA ba gnyan dang ma grags kyi 'gyur/ mtshan ma gyen bsgreng rdo rje'i tshig dbye a mo g+ha badzra gyis
98b4(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ rdo rje tsa rtsi ka'i sgrub thabs /bram ze dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje phag mo dkar mo'i sgrub thabs rnams
98b5(dkar chag): dang la 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ gnod sbyin mo kun nas 'khyil pa mched gsum gyi sgrub thabs klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa dang/ de'i 'grel pa rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/
98b6(dkar chag): gnod sbyin yang 'phrog ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon in+d+ra po d+his mdzad pa/ kha che paN chen dang/ lo tsA pa tshul khrims gzhon nu'i 'gyur// //zu pa la mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa paN+Ti ta don yod zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ zha lu lo
98b7(dkar chag): chen d+harma mA la b+ha dra'i 'gyur/ 'jam dpal smra ba'i seng ge'i sgrub thabs dam pa rgya gar gyis dmzad pa/ zha ma seng rgyal gyi 'gyur 'jam dpal ngag gi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje rnal 'byor mas gsungs pa 'gyur byang med pa/ 'jam dbyangs
99a1(dkar chag): dkar po'i sgrub thabs dang sbyar ba'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta ma tis mdzad pa/ paN chen shAkya sh+rI dang khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sbyin dbye ba'i cho ga slob dpon chen po smri tidz+nyA na ki rtis
99a2(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo gcig grub? kyi bstod pa/ gser gyi phreng ba dag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa/ 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin
99a3(dkar chag): chen dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i sde'i 'gyur /thugs rje chen po'i rgyud pad+ma zab pa dang pad+ma rgyal po'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba'i rang byed dza lan d+ha ras mdzad pa/ rgya gar phyag na dang/ pradz+nyA kIrti'i 'gyur/
99a4(dkar chag): yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs jo bo chen po dpal mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i sgrub thabs kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po shAkya sh+rIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ don yod
99a5(dkar chag): zhags pa'i sgrub thabs/ bi b+huti tsan+d+ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ don mos zhags pa'i sgrub thabs mdo las bsdus pa/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang/
99a6(dkar chag): ba ri lo tsA'i 'gyur/ spyan ras gzigs kha sarbA ti'i sgrub thabs jo bo chen po dI paM ka ra sh+rIdz+nyA nas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ kha sarbA Ni lha lnga'i sgrub thabs pad+ma ka ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po nags kyi rin chen
99a7(dkar chag): dang/ chos 'khor lo tsA pa 'jam dpal ye shes kyis bsgyur ba las/ slang kyis byams pa gling ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sdes bcos shing gtan la phab pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstong pa rin po che'i 'phreng ba paN chen nags rin gyis mdzad pa/ de
99b1(dkar chag): nyid dang/ byams pa gling pa bsad nams rgya mtsho'i sdes bsgyur ba/ sems kyi phyag rgya zhes pa dri ma med pa'i lung chen po slob dpon bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ni rba na dang/ lo tsA ba jo? nang kun dga' snying po'i 'gyur/ yi ge bzhi pa'i man ngag slob
99b2(dkar chag): dpon rwa kan+tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sangs rgyas spas pa dang /jo nang lo tsA ba kun dga' snying po'i 'gyur/ phyag na rdo rje gtum po khros pa'i sgrub thabs/ yid bzhin nor bu slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ phyag rdor gos sngon can gyi sgrub thabs dpal mar me mdzad
99b3(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ phyag na rdo rje las sgrub pa'i thabs birya sh+rIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po dI paM ka ra sh+rIdz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur /rdo rje gtum po'i sgo nas phyir bzlog pa'i 'khor lo slob dpon
99b4(dkar chag): las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa/ uSh+NI Sha'i man ngag gi sgrub thabs sh+rI sid+d+has mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba bai ro tsA na'i 'gyur/ rnam 'joms kyi sgrub thabs dang khrus chog ratna kIrtis mdzad pa/ bal po'i paN+Di ta mahA pa na'i rang 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi
99b5(dkar chag): dkyil chog /rdo rjes go chas mdzad pa lo chen rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma nor sbyin ma'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta chen po sa hadza sh+rI sa mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta ku mA ra sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang po'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma u gra'i mchod pa'i cho ga
99b6(dkar chag): slob dpon rdo rje gdan ba sh+rI sha ri pu tra ma hA swa mis mdzad pa/ de nyid kyis rang 'gyur/ sgrol ma dmar mos 'gro ba dbang du bsdu ba'i 'khor lo'i cho ga sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ sngags kyi don la 'jug pa dang/ dbang gi man ngag /dam tshig
99b7(dkar chag): spas pa/ gzhal yas khang sbyin pa/ chu gtor gyi cho ga /sbyin sreg gi cho ga /lha mchod pa'i rim pa/ tshe bsgrub pa'i thabs/ 'chi ba blu ba /'chi kha ma'i ltas bcos/ ro sreg pa/ bdun tshigs kyi cho ga/ sAts+tsha'i cho ga ste/ paN+Di ta chen po mar me mdzad ye
100a1(dkar chag): shes kyis mdzad pa'i sngags lugs bcu gsum du grags pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i bstod ba mu tig phreng ba tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho'i 'gyur/ tsan drag go mis mdzad
100a2(dkar chag): ba'i sgrol ma mdzub ker ma'i bstod pa dang/ sgrol bstod smon lam thams cad grub pa/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa dang byed go chas mdzad pa/ rig pa'i khu byug gi 'byung/ 'jigs pa brgyad skyob kyi bstod ba btsun pa zla bas mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa
100a3(dkar chag): jo bo chen po mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud d+haka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ sgrol mnyer gcig gi bstod pa/ dga' ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa/ ak+Sho b+hya(dkar chag): badzras mdzad pa/ dam
100a4(dkar chag): tshig sgrol ma'i bstod pa/ jo bo chen po mar me mdzad ye shes dang/ mtshur gyi 'gyur/ sgrol bstod gnyan d+harma kIrti'i 'gyur/ sgrol bstod klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ sgrol bstod rin chen rgyan phra nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i bkra shis surya
100a5(dkar chag): sh+rI dang long bza' dge slong tshul khrims brtsegs kyi 'gyur /seng ldeng nags sgrol gyi bstod ba tshigs bcad bcu drug pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 'phags ma sgrol ma'i mtshan nges ba zhes bya ba stong phrag bcu gnyis pa las phyung ba/ jo nang lo tsA ba
100a6(dkar chag): kun snying gi 'gyur/ dbyangs can ma'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta nag po'i khol gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na shI la dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ mgon po tshe dpag med kyi sgrub thabs mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa tshe dpag
100a7(dkar chag): med kyi dkyil chog yongs su bzung ba zhes bya ba ma gcig grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zla ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba glan dang ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ tshe dpag med kyi dbang bzhi bsgyur ba'i cho ga'i las khrigs ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma grub
100b1(dkar chag): pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa/ rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wa la tsan+d+ra dang/ lotsA ba glan dang ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs paDNit bde chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ 'gos lo gzhon nu dang la
100b2(dkar chag): gyi 'gyur/ mi g.yo ba'i mngon par rtogs pa rab tu dga' ba mngon par brjod pa nags kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ 'gos lo gzhon nu dpal gyi 'gyur/ khro bo'i rgyal po mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po dpal

100b4(dkar chag): khro bo chen po'i sgrub thabs/ don dam ba zhes pa slob dpon chen po dI paM ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ni rbA Na sh+rI dang/ lo tsA ba tA ra nA tha'i 'gyur/ gur mgon lha bcu bdun ma'i sgrub thabs/ bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad ba/ a tsarya rA hu la dmar
100b5(dkar chag): po dang/ lo tsA ba gyi ljang gi 'gyur/ nag po chen bo'i gsang sgrub bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ a tsArya ra hu la dmar po dang/ lo tsA ba kyi ljang gi 'gyur/ mgon po nag po'i sgrub thabs /slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta 'bum phrag
100b6(dkar chag): gsum pa dang/ lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba ga 'od kyi 'gyur /zhal bzhi ba'i dam tshig dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ gnyan lo dar ma grags kyi 'gyur /
100b7(dkar chag): nag po chen po'i srog gi spu gri'i sgrub thabs/ bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa mal gyi khyad tshas/ nag po chen po'i sbyin sreg bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta la lit badzra dang/ lo tsA bgyi ljang dbu dkar gyi 'gyur / dpal

101b7(dkar chag): pa'i nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs dpal ldan sha ba ri bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a ta ya badzra dang/ lo tsA ba phur bu 'od kyi bsgyur ba/ ye shes mgon po'i gsang sgrub sha ba ri pas mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa rdam pa sgra sgrog ces pa bram ze mchog sred kyis
102a1(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ mgon po'i bstod pa bla ma rA hu las mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa bram ze sa ra has mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa dpal sha ba ri pas mdzad pa/ phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis

102b5(dkar chag): dpon a ba d+hU ti pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI paM kar sh+rI dz+nyA na dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bgegs kyi rgyal bo'i sgrub thabs nag po spyod pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta g.ya g+har dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ sna tshogs nor bu bde mchog

102b7(dkar chag): kyi rgyal bo'i sgrub thabs nag po pas mdzad pa /paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i bstod pa slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ bgegs bdag chen po'i sbu? bri ba'i man ngag yid bzhin nor bu slob dpon

103a2(dkar chag): bdag gi sbyin sreg nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang/ lo tsA ba 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ shin tu myur ba'i bgegs kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs pi paM ka ras mdzad pa/ shin tu myur ba'i bgegs kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs bi? ro tsA na'i
103a3(dkar chag): rang 'gyur/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i 'khor lo'i gsal byed DoM b+hi he ru kas mdzad pa/ sngags kyi rgyal po'i dam tshig dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ gsal byed nyi ma'i 'khor lo rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA rtha pir
103a4(dkar chag): dang/ lo tsA ba ba ri'i 'gyur/ tshogs bdag zhi ba'i sgrub thabs jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ tshogs kyi bdag po yid bzhin nor bu'i sgrub thabs nag po pas mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag sbyin sreg /tshogs bdag gi bstod pa nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/
103a5(dkar chag): tshogs bdag gsang sgrub jo bos mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag gi bstod pa a mo g+ha badzra gyis mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag 'dod pa'i dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bai ro tsA na dang/ lo tsA ba ba ri chos grags kyi 'gyur/

103a7(dkar chag): chos kyi grags pa'i 'gyur/ rim pa drug pa dza ba ris mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de ba pur+Na dang lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ gnod sbyin a pa ra tsi ta'i sgrub thabs rgyal po in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa/ nor lha lnga'i gsang sgrub/ paN+Di ta bin? ya tsan+d+ra dang /
103b1(dkar chag): lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa dzam+b+ha la'i bstod pa bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma hA dza na dang/ lo tsA ba mal gyo blo gros grags kyi 'gyur/ nor bdag gtso 'khor lnga'i bstod pa mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa/
103b2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur/ gnod sbyin nag mos bsang pa'i thabs las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa/ khro bo khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi sgrub thabs las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wa la tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba glan dar mtshul khrims kyi 'gyur/

111b7(dkar chag): stong nyid bdun cu pa'i 'grel pa/ dpal ldan zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a b+ha yA ka ra dang/ lo tsA ba bsnur dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ stong nyid bdun cu ba'i 'grel ba slob dpon gzhan la phan bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta
112a1(dkar chag): de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu mchog gi 'gyur/ paN+Di ta dza ya A nandas mdzad pa rtog ge tho ba/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba khu mdo sde 'bar gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //rab la dbu ma 'jug pa'i
112a2(dkar chag): 'grel bshad don gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ kha che'i paN+Di ta dza ya A nandas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ o tsA ba kun dga' grags kyis bsgyur ba bzhugs so// //la pa la byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa la 'jug pa slob dpon zhi
112a3(dkar chag): ba lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de wa dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur ba las/ slad kyis paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po dang/ shAkya blo gros kyis yul dbus kyi dpe 'grel pa dang mthun par bcos pa las/ slad kyi paN+Di ta
112a4(dkar chag): su ma ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi bcas pa/ shlo ka stong du grags pa/ bam po gnyis su byas pa dang/ de'i dka' 'grel shes rab 'byung gnas blo gros kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sum ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug dang gnyan dar
112a5(dkar chag): ma grags gnyis kyis stod smad bgos nas bsgyur ba/ byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i rnam par bshad pa'i dka' 'grel slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur bzhugs so// //sha pa la spyod 'jug gi legs
112a6(dkar chag): par sbyar ba shlo ka chig stong lnga brgya bdun cu rtsa lnga/ slob dpon dge ba lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sh+rI ku mA ra dang/ lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i rtogs par dka' ba'i gnas gtan la phab ba'i gzhung/ paN+Di ta nag
112a7(dkar chag): pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i dka' 'grel bai ro tsA na rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ spyod 'jug gi shes rab le'u'i dka' 'grel/ paN+Di ta mi mnyam khol po dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab
112b1(dkar chag): kyi 'gyur/ spyod 'jug gi shes rab le'u dang/ bsngo ba'i le'u'i dka' 'grel mdzad byang 'gyur byang med pa gcig/ spyod 'jug gi don sum cu rtsa drug tu bsdus pa gser gling pa'i bla ma chos skyong gis mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/
112b2(dkar chag): gtso ba'i don gcig tu bsdus pa bla ma gser gling pas mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ spyod 'jug gi dgongs 'grel khyad par gsal byed ces bya ba/ paN+Di ta bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ras mdzad pa/ de nyid kyi rang 'gyur du bsgyur ba rnams bzhugs
112b3(dkar chag): so// //sa pa la bden pa gnyis rnam par 'byed pa slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa dang/ de'i rang 'grel bden pa gnyis rnam par gtan la dbab pa dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa slob
112b4(dkar chag): dpon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa bam po gsum pa/ dbu ma rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon chen po zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ banDe dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ dbu ma rgyan gyi 'grel ba slob dpon chen po zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa/
112b5(dkar chag): shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ bande dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ dbu ma rgyan gyi dka' 'grel slob dpon kam la shI las mdzad pa shlo ka stong sum brgya brgyad cu pa bam pa bzhi pa/ paN+Di ta su ren+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ pradz+nyA warma dang/ bande dpal brtsegs rak+Shi
112b6(dkar chag): ta'i 'gyur/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa'i dbu ma snang ba/ paN+Di ta shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad ba'i dbu ma de khon nyid snang ba zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las
112b7(dkar chag): mdzad ba'i chos thams cad rang bzhin med par nyid du grub pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tras bsgyur ba rnams bzhugs so// //ha pa la sku gsum la 'jug ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i bsten bcos slob dpon
113a1(dkar chag): klu'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA warma dang bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ sku gsum 'grel pa slob dpon ye shes zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA? wa rma dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid la 'jug pa'i 'grel ba
113a2(dkar chag): slob dpon dpal sbas kyis mdzad ba/ dbu ma'i lugs kyi snying po mdor bsdus pa'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon bidyA ka pra b+hAs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ rnam pa med ba'i tshigs le'ur byas pa la yul gyi paN+Di ta dga' 
113a3(dkar chag): pa'i dpal gyi mdzad pa/ lta ba tha dad pa rnam par phye ba mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon dbu ma'i seng ges mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bya ro sh+rI mi tra dang/ dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gzhung rnam par 'byed ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon
113a4(dkar chag): dzai tA ris mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ dbu ma rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon tsan+d+ra ha ri bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba ting 'dzin bzang po'i 'gyur/ bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa zhes bya ba jo bo rjas mdzad
113a5(dkar chag): pa de nyid dang/ rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur/ thub pa dgongs pa'i rgyan shlo ka stong phrag phyed dang drug pa slob dpon a b+ha yas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ spong zho gsal ba grags kyi 'gyur la/ dus phyis dbang blo brtan gyis legs bar bcos shing gtan
113a6(dkar chag): la phab pa/ tshad ma rnams 'joms rtsa 'grel gnyi ga ma tshang ba'i dum bu gcig /theg pa chen po'i mtshan nyid kun las btus sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kar+Na pa ti dang/ lo tsA ba brany+dzA sid+ha'i 'gyur/ sems brtag pa slob dpon tshul
113a7(dkar chag): khrims 'phags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka na ka dang/ lo tsA ba rma chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ theg pa thams cad du snang bar byed pa'i bye brag tu bshad pa zhes bya ba bram ze'i btsun pa rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba ting nge 'dzin bzang po'i
113b1(dkar chag): 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //a pa la lta ba gtso cher gtan la phab nas/ sgom pa'i rim pa ston pa'i bstan bcos ni/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i sgom rim/ paN+Di ta lo ta dang/ lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor sgom pa'i lam slob dpon ye
113b2(dkar chag): shes snying pos mdzad pa/ cig car 'jug pa rnam par mi rtog pa'i sgom don paN+Di ta bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma tA shI la dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i kun rdzob byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i man ngag pad+ma sdangs ba zhes
113b3(dkar chag): bya ba dang/ paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ don dam byang chub sems bsgom pa'i rim pa rin chen sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ tshad med bzhi bsgom ba'i
113b4(dkar chag): rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa'i sgom rim dang po/ sgom rim bar ma/ sgom rim tha ma/ rnal 'byor sgom pa la 'jug pa dang bzhi/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA warma dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa
113b5(dkar chag): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag rdo rje lta bu zhes bya ba dpal kam+ba las mdzad pa/ lus yongs su dpyad pa'i sgom rim nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ mi sdug ba bsgom pa'i rim pa 'gyur rnying/ pha rol tu phyin
113b6(dkar chag): pa'i theg pa'i bsgom pa'i rim pa'i man ngag slob dpon ye shes grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bla na med pa bsgom pa zhes bya ba slob dpon ma hA ma tis mdzad la/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba chos
113b7(dkar chag): kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ ting nge 'dzin tshogs kyi le'u slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i ting nge 'dzin tshogs kyi le'u paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba chos kyi
114a1(dkar chag): shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bsam gtan gyi chos drug rnam par bzhag pa slob dpon chen po a ba d+hU tI bas mdzad pa dang/ de'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta dA na shI las mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang po'i
114a2(dkar chag): 'gyur/ dbu ma'i man ngag jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ dran pa gcig pa'i man ngag jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ dbu ma'i man ngag rin po cha'i za ma tog kha phye ba
114a3(dkar chag): zhes bya ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA brgya btson 'grus seng ge dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon shes rab thar pas mdzad pa /paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ ting nge
114a4(dkar chag): 'dzin gyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs rnam par bzhag pa/ rgya'i hwa shad zab mo la sogs pa dang/ lo tsA ba rnam par mi rtog pa'i 'gyur/ sgom pa'i rim pa mdo kun las btus ba rnal 'byog spyod pa'i bsam gtan rje btsun la ros mdzad pa/ byang chub sems
114a5(dkar chag): dpa' i bslab bya dang/ sbyod pa gtsho cher ston ba'i skor ni/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i mdo kun las btus pa/ bam po lnga pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes de'i 'gyur/ de'i 'grel ba rin po che'i snang
114a6(dkar chag): ba'i rgyan zhes bya ba lung gi tshad mas rab tu sbyar ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa shlo ka sum stong lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa/ paN+Di ta nag po pa dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ 'di ltar sems tsam du smra ba'i paN+Di tas brtsams
114a7(dkar chag): mdo kyang/ rtsa 'grel stabs gcig pa'i phyir 'dir bris so/ /byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA ka ra warma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
114b1(dkar chag): 'di sgom pa'i bstan bcos yin yang dus phyis rnyed pas spyod pa'i po ti'i gsham du bzhugs su bcug pa yin no/ /mdo kun las btus pa'i don bsdus pa/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i 'gyur/ rim gyis 'jug pa'i sgom
114b2(dkar chag): don slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA warma dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //ki p la slob dpon zhi ba las mdzad pa'i bslab pa kun las btus pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa dang/ bslab pa kun las btus pa'i
114b3(dkar chag): bam po bcu bzhi pa paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ dA na shI la dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sdes bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi paN+Di ta thig le bum pa dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bcos pa/ bslab pa kun las btus pa las 'byung ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i yi ge brgya
114b4(dkar chag): pa'i srung ba dang/ sdig pa bshags pa'i chog slob dpon zhib lhas mdzad pa/ bslab pa kun las btus pa'i mngon par rtogS pa bla ma gser gling bas mdzad ba/ jo bo rje dang tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bslab pa kun las btus pa'i phyogs tsam zhig blangs
114b5(dkar chag): pa'i bshad pa bslab ba'i me tog snye ma paN+Di ta bai ro tsA na rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrta dang/ lo tsA ba zham seng rgyal dang/ klog skya gzhon nu 'bar gyis bsgyur ba las phyis mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bcos pa/ 'phags pa dpa' bos mdzad pa'i pha rol
114b6(dkar chag): tu phyin pa'i don bsdus pa/ bai ro tsA na rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ las dang po ba'i sa sbyangs pa dgra las rgyal ba gsang ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nag po ba dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams dag tu
114b7(dkar chag): byas pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa'i byang chub lam gyi sgron ma/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ de'i rang 'grel paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ dge slong tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ jo bo rjes mdzad ba'i snying po bsdus/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba
115a1(dkar chag): tshul khrims 'byung gnas de bcos bsgyur ba/ jo bo rjes mdzad ba'i snying po nges par bsdu ba/ paN+Di ta de nyid dan/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' i nor bu'i phreng ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa dang/ byang chub semS

115a3(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs yi ger bsdus pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs shin tu bsdus pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa dang/ rang gi bya ba'i rim pa la bskul pa
115a4(dkar chag): dang bcas pa yi ger bris pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur mdo de'i don kun las btus pa'i man dag jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ mi dge ba bcu'i las
115a5(dkar chag): kyi lam bstan pa jo bo rjes mdzad ba/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ las rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya dang/ tshul khri ba/ de nyid dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/  spyod pa bsdus ba'i sgron mjo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ tshul

115a7(dkar chag): gyi rim pa mdor bsdus pa kha che shAkya sh+rIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'di la chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur cig kyang yod mod kyi 'di dang gcig tu 'dug pas ma bris so/ /theg pa chen bo'i man ngag tshigs su bcad pa kha
115b1(dkar chag): che'i paN+Di ta shAkya sh+rIs mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba byams ba'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha sh+rI dz+nyA nas mdzad ba'i rgyal ba'i lam la 'jug pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba chag dgra bcom gyi 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' i spyod yul yongs su dag pa'i mdo'i don
115b2(dkar chag): mdor bsdus pa slob dpon dpal sgra gcan 'dzin bzang pos mdzad pa/ kha che shAkya sh+rI dang/ gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ skyabs 'gro dang sems bskyed la sogs ba'i chog ga'i skor la/ byang chub tu sems bskyed ba'i chog 'phags pa klu sgrub
115b3(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ren+d+ra bo d+hi dang lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' i sdom pa'i chog slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su N+ya sh+rI mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba dang ma grags kyi 'gyur/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang/ yi dam blang ba'i chog slob
115b4(dkar chag): dpon dgra las rgyal bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sum ti kIrti dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ byang chub tu sems bskyed ba dang/ byang chub sems dpa' i sdom pa'i chog jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ dge blos bsgyur ba tshul khrims rgyal bas btsos
115b5(dkar chag): pa/ byang chub sems dpa' i sdom pa bzung ba'i chog /paN+Di ta 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa/ kha che shAkya sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ chag dgra bcom gyi 'gyur/ gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba bdun cu pa slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ lo
115b6(dkar chag): tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ skyabs 'gro yan lag bdun pa/ slob dpon bim la mi tras mdzad pa ltung ba bshags pa'i cho ga paN+Di ta de ba shAn+tis mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ ltung ba bshags ba'i tsheg ngo bo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid
115b7(dkar chag): dang tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ kha ton dang glegs bam bklag pa'i sngon du bya ba'i chog jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i sAts+tsha gdab ba'i cho ga jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ bla ma'i bya ba'i rim pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ sdom pa gsum gyi rim pa paN+Di ta rnyog med rdo rjes mdzad
116a1(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di ta a tu lo dA pa dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ chos spyod yan lag bzhi pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug sh+rI dza ga ta mi tra A nandas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ dam chos spyod
116a2(dkar chag): pa la 'jug pa'i yan lag bdun pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta shAkya sh+rI b+ha dras mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //gi pa la jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa 'grags pa bzhugs/ 'di gong 'og nas 'byung ba
116a3(dkar chag): rnams zlos mod kyis bshad bka' stabs su yod cing dpe phyi ma sogs la bsam nas/ sngar gyi bstan 'gyur rnams su pu ti tha dad du bris pa bzhin du 'dir yang bris so/ /de'ang 'di nyid na bzhugs pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs ni/ byang chub lam gyi sgron ma
116a4(dkar chag): slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma jo bo rjes mdzad pa de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa/
116a5(dkar chag): de nyid dang/ lo tsA brgya brtson 'grus seng ges bsgyur pa/ dbu ma'i man ngag jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ snying po bsdu ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa de nyid dang/ lo tsa' ba tshul khrims 'byung gnas deb tse'i 'gyur/ snying po nges par
116a6(dkar chag): bsdu ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' i nor bu'i phreng ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams ngag tu byas pa/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ 'khor ba las yid ches par 'byung bar

120b4(dkar chag): sa mu dras mdzad pa/ 'phags pa 'da' ka ye shes kyi mdo'i don gsal ba zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa slob dpon zhi ba lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma rA dza dang/ lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ byang chub kyi ltung ba bshags pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon 'phags pa

120b6(dkar chag): las kyi sgrib pa rnam par sbyod pa'i cho ga'i bshad pa zhes bya ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ nag tsho lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ phung po gsum pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang/ tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa dkon
120b7(dkar chag): mchog brtsegs pa chos kyi rnam grangs le'u stong phrag brgya pa las 'od srungs kyi le'u'i rnam par bshad pa slob dpon blo brtan gyis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// //nyi pa la ting nge 'dzin rgyal po'i 'grel ba grags pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba 
121a1(dkar chag): slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi bshad sbyar 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan
121a2(dkar chag): shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi bshad pa slob dpon phyogs kyis glang pos mdzad pa/ bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi rgyal po'i rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba bande dpal
121a3(dkar chag): brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi rgyal po'i rgya cher 'grel ba slob dpon rgyan bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na garb+ha dang/ bande dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi 'grel ba slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/
121a4(dkar chag): paN+Di ta A nanda dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong b+ha dra pA la'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //ti thi di gsum la mdo sde dgongs ba zab mo nges par 'grel pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ rgya'i mkhan po won tsheg gis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba 'gos chos grub kyi
121a5(dkar chag): 'gyur/ dam pa'i chos pad+ma dkar po'i 'grel ba sing+ga gling gi slob dpon sa'i rtsa lag gi mdzad pa dang gnyis bzhugs so// //ni ba la 'phags pa lang+gar gshegs pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon ye shes dpal bzang pos mdzad pa bzhugs
121a6(dkar chag): so/ //pa pi la mdo sde lang+gar gshegs pa'i 'grel pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po rgyan zhes bya ba rgya'i mkhan po dz+nyA na badzras mdzad pa bzhugs so/ /yod dang med pa'i mdza' gnyis legs spangs ba'i/ /nges don rtsod med legs par rnam phye
121a7(dkar chag): ba'i/ /'khor lo gsum pa'i dgongs 'grel gtso che ba/ /gsal byed bstan bcos bzhi bcu tham pa bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ bka' tha ma'i mdo sde sna tshogs kyi 'grel pa'i skor te le'u
121b1(dkar chag): gsum pa'o// //gnyis pa spyi'i dgongs 'grel la/ bka' 'khor lo gsum pa'i don gtso bor ston cing /sbyir theg chen thams cad kyi dgongs pa 'grel ba/ rnal 'byor spyod pa sems tsam ba dang tshul mthun par ston pa'i bstan bcos la/ /
121b2(dkar chag): phi pa la bcom ldan 'das byams pa mgon pos mdzad pa/ mdo sde rgyan gyis rab tu byed pa/ bam po gsum pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sid+hi dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs la sogs pa'i 'gyur/ mgon po byams pas mdzad pa'i dbus dang mdza' rnam par
121b3(dkar chag): 'byed pa'i bstan bcos/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ chos dang chos nyid rnam par 'byed pa 'phags pa byams pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta pAra hi ta dang
121b4(dkar chag): lo tsA ba gzu dga' bo rdo rjes btsos pa/ chos dang chos nyid rnam bar 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa mgon po byams pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mahA dza na dang/ lo tsA ba zha ma seng rgyal gyi 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i rgyud phyi ma de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po ston bar
121b5(dkar chag): byed ba'i mdo zab mo rnams kyi dgongs pa 'grel pa theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma'i bstan bcos mgon po byams bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta saM dza na dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ rgyud bla ma'i 'grel pa slob dpon 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa/
121b6(dkar chag): paN+Di ta sang dza na dang/ lo tsA pa blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan gyi bshad pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa shlo ka sum stong drug brgya lnga bcu pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs la sogs pa'i 'gyur rnams
121b7(dkar chag): bzhugs so// //bi pa la dbus dang mdza' rnam par 'byed pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzina mi tra dang/ shI lan+d+re bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ chos dang chos nyid rnam par 'byed pa'i 'grel pa/ slob
122a1(dkar chag): dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma hA dza na dang/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ mdo sde rgyan gyi 'grel bshad slob dpon btsun pa ngo bo nyid med pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs
122a2(dkar chag): la sogs pa'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //mi tsi gnyis la mdo sde rgyan gyi 'grel bshad slob dpon blo gros brtan pas mdzad par grags pa/ mkhan pa mu ne tsan+d+ra dang/ lo tsA ba lce bkra shis kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //
122a3(dkar chag): tshi la mdo sde rgyan gyi tshig dnag po gnyis kyi bshad pa slob dpon gzhan la phan pa bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu mchog gi 'gyur/ theg pa chen po mdo sde rgyan gyi don bsdus pa slob dpon dz+nyA na sh+rIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/
122a4(dkar chag): lo tsA ba chos kyi brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ dbus mdza' i 'grel bshad slob dpon blo brtan gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa dgongs pa nges par 'grel ba'i mdo las 'phags pa
122a5(dkar chag): byams pa'i le'u nyi tshe bshad pa/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// //dzi pa la 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa'i sa sde lnga'i dang po rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa'i dngos gzhi mang po pa shlo ka brgyad stong dgu brgya brgyad cu
122a6(dkar chag): rtsa bzhi pa bzhugs so// //wi pa la nyan thos kyis shlo ka drug stong rnams bzhugs so// //zhi pa la byang chub sems dpa' sa dang po pa'i go rim/ shlo ka drug stong bdun brgya lnga bcu pa paN+Di ta pradnyA wa rma dang/ bande ye shes sde'i
122a7(dkar chag): 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //zing dang 'i pa'i stod la/ rnam par gtan la dbab pa bsdu pa bam po bzhi bcu rtsa gsum pa paN+Di ta pradz+nyA warma dang/ su ren+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ smad la gzhi bsdu pa'i nang gi mde sde bsdu ba bam?
122b1(dkar chag): ngo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa sho ka drug stong bdun brgya dgu bcu rtsa gsum pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nye wa rma dang/ dzin mi tra dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur bzhugs so// //yi pa la gzhi bsdu ba'i nang gi 'dul ba bsdu ba paN+Di ta pradz+nyA warma dang/ dzi na mi tra dang/ ban+dze ye shes
122b2(dkar chag): sde'i 'gyur/ rnam grangs bsdu ba shlo ka bdun brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ rnam par bshad pa bsdu ba shlo ka lnga brgya bdun cu rtsa lnga pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA warma dang/ su ren+d+ra bod+hi dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur te/ de ltar sa sde lnga la shlo ka bzhi khri lnga stong bam po brgya dang lnga
122b3(dkar chag): bcu bzhugs so/ /sa'i stod 'grel ji snyad pa bzhugs/ 'di la sngon gyi gna' mchan las dzi na mi tras mdzad par bshad/ byang chub sems dpa' i sa'i 'grel pa sbyin pa'i rim par phye ba dgu pa yan chad slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa/ ji snyed
122b4(dkar chag): 'gyur ba jo bo rje dang/ nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ byang sa'i tshul khrims le'u'i 'grel pa slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ byang sa'i tshul khrims le'u'i rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon rgyal ba'i
122b5(dkar chag): sas kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ pradz+nyA warma dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/ //rip la byang chub sems dpa' i sa'i 'grel pa slob dpon rgya mtsho sprin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba tshul
122b6(dkar chag): khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //li pa la slob dpon 'phags pa thogs med kyi mdzad pa'i theg pa chen po'i sdom theg bsdus bam po bzhi pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra po d+hi dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ slob dpon
122b7(dkar chag): 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa'i theg pa thun mong gi sdom chos mngon pa kun las btus pa bam po lnga pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ bandai ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ theg bsdus kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ shlo
123a1(dkar chag): ka nyis stong chig brgya brgyad cu pa/ bam po brgyad pa/ paN+Dita jo bo rje dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ theg pa chen po bsdus pa'i bshad sbyar dge bsnyen btsun pa ngo bo nyid med pas mdzad pa/ shlo ka nyis
123a2(dkar chag): stong bdun brgya bdun cu rtsa bzhi pa dzi na mi tra dang/ shI lan+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ theg bsdus kyi gnas dang po'i bshad pa don gsang ba rnams par phye ba bsdus te bshad pa ji snyed pa bzhugs so/ /'di la sngon gyi dkar chag las slob
123a3(dkar chag): dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa zer ba snang ste min pa 'dra'o// //shi pa la chos mngon pa kun las btus pa'i bshad pa bam po dgu pa slob dpon rgyal ba'i sras kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/
123a4(dkar chag): bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ kun las btus kyi rtsa ba dang/ 'grel pa rgyal sras ma gnyis bsres pa'i bshad pa lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur gnyis bzhugs so// //sip la slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis
123a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa'i thams cad rnam rigs tsam du ston pa sum cu pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ phyi rol gyi don 'gog pa nyi shu pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/
123a6(dkar chag): paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra po d+hi dang/ dA na shI la dang/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ nyi shu pa'i rang 'grel slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis
123a7(dkar chag): mdzad pa'i rang bzhin gsum nges par bstan pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas bcas kyi 'gyur/ phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bad+hi dang/ dA na shI la dang/ lo tsA
123b1(dkar chag): ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i rnam par bshad pa'i rigs pa mdo sde'i dum pa brgya pa paN+Di ta bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang/ sarba dz+nyA de wa dang/ lo tsA ba rtsangs de wen+d+ra rak+Sha tis bsgyur cing/ many+dza sh+rI wa rmas zhus pa/ rnam par
123b2(dkar chag): bshad pa'i 'jigs? pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ bam po bcu pa paN+Di ta bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang/ shAkya sid+ha dang/ lo tsA brtsangs de wen+d+ra rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i las gyur pa'i rab tu byed pa/ paN+Di ta shud+d+ha sid+ha

123b4(dkar chag): cing/ phyis rgya nag chen po'i lha btsun chos kyi rin chen gyis brgya'i skad las bod kyi skad du bsgyur gsum cu pa'i bshad pa slob dpon blo ldan gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra po d+hi dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ rab tu byed pa nyi shu pa'i
123b5(dkar chag): 'grel bshad slob dpon dul ba'i lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ dA na shI la dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //hib la phung po lnga'i bye brag tu bshad pa bam po bzhi pa slob
123b6(dkar chag): dpon blo brtan gyis mdzad pa/ phung po lnga'i rnam par 'grel pa slob dpon sa'i rtsa lag gis mdzad pa/ phung po lnga'i rnam par 'grel pa slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ dA na shI pa dang/ bande ye shes sde'i
123b7(dkar chag): 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //mi pa la rnams bshad rigs pa'i 'gre pa bam po bco lnga pa/ paN+Di ta bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang/ shAkya sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba de wen+d+ra rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ tshigs bcad bzhi stong tshig brgya pa bzhugs so// //
124a1(dkar chag): ku pa la sum cu pa'i 'grel bshad bam po lnga pa slob dpon dul ba lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang/ dA na shI la dang/ bande ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ las grub pa'i rab tu byed pa'i 'grel pa blo bzang dang
124a2(dkar chag): tshul gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba rtsangs de wen+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing bande dpal brtsegs kyis gtan la phab pa/ slob dpon shAn+ti pas mdzad pa'i/ dbu ma'i rgyan gyi 'grel bshad dbu ma'i lam grub pa zhes bya ba 'di la bod na sems
124a3(dkar chag): tsam rgyan zhes grags pa / le tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ de ltar rnal 'byor spyod pa sems tsam pa'i lta ba gtan la 'bebs pa'i bstan bcos rnams bstan nas/ sgom pa gtan la 'bebs pa'i bstan bcos ni/ slob dpon 'phags pa thogs med
124a4(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa'i bsam gtan gyi sgron ma/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta d+harma sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ de'i don 'grel rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag /slob dpon
124a5(dkar chag): chos kyi dbang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza bad+dA na dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa'i man ngag /slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas
124a6(dkar chag): kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sgom pa'i don mdor bsdus nas bstan pa/ slob dpon ye shes zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA wa rma dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa'i man ngag /slob dpon shAn+ti pas
124a7(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rab 'byor zhi ba dang/ lo tsA ba ting 'dzin bzang po'i 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag slob dpon shAn+ti pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang/ lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dge ba'i sdong po zhes bya ba'i
124b1(dkar chag): rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon ratna kI rtis mdzad pa/ spyod pa dang bslab bya ston pa'i skor la/ byang chub sems dpa' i sdom pa nyi shu pa/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bidya ka ra sid+ha dang/ lo
124b2(dkar chag): tsA ba many+dzu sh+rI wa rma'i 'gyur bam po gnyis pa/ sdom pa nyi shu pa'i dka' 'grel gnas brtan byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta k+She la ka ga na dang/ lo tsA ba mang 'or byang chub shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di dag rtsom pa po rnams sems tsam gyi lta ba 'dzin
124b3(dkar chag): pa ma yin yang/ bong na 'di dag sems tsam lugs su grags 'dug pa dang /brjod bya'ang byang chub sems dpa' i sa'i tshul khrims le'u'i skabs dang mthun par 'dug pas 'dir bris so/ /chos rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon ratna kI rtis
124b4(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba mchims yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur/ dbu ma rgyan gyi man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a mo g+ha dang / 'o ru lo tsA'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //
124b5(dkar chag): 'di sems tsam gyi lta ba ston pa'i bstan bcos yin kyang/ dus phyis rnyed pas po ti'i bsham du bzhugs pa yin no/ /chos rnams gzung dang 'dzin pa las grol ba'i/ /rnam rig tsam du ston pa'i lta sgom spyod/ /gsal byed byams pa thogs
124b6(dkar chag): med rjes 'brang gzhung/ /bcu phrag drug la gsum gyis brgyan pa bzhugs/ /bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag tshangs pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba las/ theg pa chen po sems tsam gyi skor gyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o// //gsum
124b7(dkar chag): pa bka' 'khor lo dang po bden pa bzhi'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i bka' i dgongs pa 'grel pa'i bstan bcos la/ dang po lhag pa shes rab kyi bslab pa ston pa mngon pa'i bstan bcos ni// //khu pa la 'phags pa maung+gal kyi bu chen pos
125a1(dkar chag): mdzad ba'i gdags pa'i bstan bcos la 'jig rten bzhag pa bam po dgu /'di la dkar chag chen mo nas bam po bdun zhes 'byung/ rgyu gdags pa bam po drug po dzin mi tra dang/ pradz+nyA warma dang/ lo tsA ba ye
125a2(dkar chag): shes sde la sogs pa'i 'gyur/ las gdags pa paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ dA na shI la dang/ pradz+nya warma dang/ ye shes sde la sogs pa'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/ /'di dag bye brag tu smra ba rnams bka' ru'i 'dod la/ mod sde ba rnams bstan
125a3(dkar chag): bcos su bzhed do// //gu du gnyis la slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i chos mngon pa mdzod kyi tshig le'ur byas pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ de'i rang 'grel bam po sum cu pa /
125a4(dkar chag): paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ chos mngon pa mdzod kyi 'grel pa mdo dang mthun pa zhes bya ba slob dpon 'dul bzang gis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// //cu chu gnyis la mngonpa mdzod ki
125a5(dkar chag): 'grel bshad don gsal ba zhes bya ba shlo ka khri brgya stong/ bam po drug cu pa/ rgyal po'i sras grags pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang/ lo tsA ba bande dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur bzhugs so// //ju nyu gnyis
125a6(dkar chag): la chos mngon pa mdzod kyi 'grel bshad mtshan nyid kyi rjes su 'brang ba zhes bya ba slob dpon gang ba spel gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka na ka warma dang/ lo tsA ba pa tsa ba nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur bzhugs so// //tu thu gnyis la chos
125a7(dkar chag): mngon pa mdzod kyi 'grel bshad nye bar mkho ba zhes bya ba mdo dang sbyar ba/ bal po'i paN+Di ta zhi gnas lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza ya sh+rI dang/ lotsA pa khams pa shes rab 'od zer gyi 'gyur dang/ chos mngon pa mdzod kyi 'grel pa gnang kyi sgron ma zhes
125b1(dkar chag): bya ba/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rnal 'byor zla ba dang/ lo tsA ba 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i 'gyur/ chos mngon par mdzod kyi 'grel bshad mtshan nyid kyi rjes su 'brang ba zhes ba ba slob dpon gang ba spel gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka na warma dang/

125b3(dkar chag): pa la 'jug pa'i rab tu byed pa rnams bzhugs so// //gnyis pa lhag pa sems kyi bslab pa gtso bor ston pa mdo sde'i sde snod kyi dgongs 'grel la// //du pa la tshad du brjod pa'i tshoms dgra bcom pa chos skyabs kyis bsdus pa
125b4(dkar chag): shlo ka stong lnga brgya bzhi bcu pa/ paN+Di ta badyi ka ra pra d+hA dang/ /lo tsA ba rin chen chog gi 'gyur la/ /dpal brtsegs ki gtan la phag pa/ 'di bye brag tu smra ba rnams kyis bka' nyid du bzhed do/ /ched du brjod pa'i tshoms kyi 'grel pa slob dpon shes rab
125b5(dkar chag): go chos mdzad pa'i stod bzhugs so// //nu pa la ched du brjod pa'i tshems kyi 'grel pa slob dpon shes rab go chas mdzad pa/ shlo ka stong phrag bcu gnyis dang lnga brgya pa/ paN+Di ta dzina ra d+ha na dang/ lo tsA ba bande shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur gyi

125b7(dkar chag): chags su bcad pa bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma ka ra dang/ lo tsA ba bsnde ye shes snying po'i 'gyur la/ bande dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa 'di'i phyi ma slang? ? no rdzong/ dang/ de'i 'grel pa dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di 
126a1(dkar chag): ta d+harma ka ra dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes snying po'i 'gyur la/ bande dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa rnams bzhugs so// /gsum pa lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa gtso bor ston pa 'dul ba'i sde snod kyi dgongs
126a2(dkar chag): 'grel la bka' so so'i dgongs 'grel dang/ spyi'i dgongs 'grel gnyis kyi bka' lung so so'i dgongs 'grel la rtsa ba'i lung gi dgongs 'grel dang/ bshad pa'i lung gi dgongs 'grel gnyis las/ dang po la/ rtsa ba'i lung so sor thar
126a3(dkar chag): pa'i dgongs 'grel ni// //bu ba la so sor thar pa'i mdo'i gzhung 'grel gyi stod bzhugs so// //phub la so sor thar pa'i mdo'i gzhung 'grel slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad par grags pa/ shlo ka dgu stong bam po nyi shu rtsa
126a4(dkar chag): bdun pa paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de wa dang/ lo tsA ba klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur gyi smad dang/ so sor thar ba'i 'grel pa slob dpon khyad par bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ 'dul ba bsdus pa zhes bya ba bam po bcu gsum pa/ paN+Di ta shI len+d+rA bo
126a5(dkar chag): b+hi dang/ shAkya bra b+ha dang/ lo tsA ba bai ro tsA na rak+Shi tas bsgyur ba las/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na sh+rI b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba rgyal ba shes rab dang/ shAkya bshes gnyen gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// //bu mu tsu gsum la so sor thar pa'i
126a6(dkar chag): mdo'i rgya cher 'grel pa 'dul ba kun las btus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dri med bshes gnyen gyis mdzad ba bam po lnga bcu bar grags pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ sarba dz+nyA de ba dang/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur dang/ so sor thar
126a7(dkar chag): ba'i 'grel ba mdzad byad med pa gcig rnams bzhugs so// //tshub la so sor thar ba'i 'grel pa mi brjed pa'i dran byed mdzad byad med pa gcig/ paN+Di ta dza rand+ha? na dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ so sor thar pa'i 'grel

126b2(dkar chag): 'dul ba bya ba'i phung po mjug ma tshang ba gcig/ 'dul ba la bstod pa chos kyi tshong dpon gyis mdzad pa dang/ de'i 'grel pa dul ba lngas mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// //dzu bla dge slong ma'i so sor thar pa'i 'grel pa mdzad
126b3(dkar chag): bya ba dang 'gyur byang med pa gcig bzhugs/ gnyis pa bshad pa'i lung gi dgongs 'grel la/ lung bzhi'i 'grel pa mdo sde 'dzin pa dge legs pa shes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ gso sbyong gi gzhi dgag dbye'i 'phro bam po bcu gnyis pa yan
126b4(dkar chag): chad bzhugs so// //wu ba la 'dul ba lung rnam 'byed kyi 'brel pa slob dpon dul ba ltas mdzad pa/ shlo ka lnga stong chib brgyab bam po bcu bdun pa paN+Di ta dzin mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur bzhugs so// //
126b5(dkar chag): zhu pa la 'dul ba lung phran tshogs kyis 'grel pa slob dpon tshul khrims bskyangs kyis mdzad pa// //paN+Di ta sh+rI bud+d+ha shAn+ti dang/ lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'dul ba lung bla ma'i bye brag/ lung zhu ba'i 'grel pa mdo sde 'dzin pa dge legs
126b6(dkar chag): bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ mgo mjug gnyis ka nas mtshang ba gcig bzhugs so// //gnyis pa 'dul ba'i bka' lung spyi'i dgongs 'grel ni// //zu pa la rtsa ba'i lung dang bshad pa'i lung thams cad kyi dgongs 'grel mtshan nyid gtan la 'bebs

127a1(dkar chag): mdzad ba shlo ka sum stong bdun brgya/ bam po dgur byas pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur bzhugs so// //lu yu gnyis la 'dul ba mdo'i 'grel pa rang gi rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba
127a2(dkar chag): slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa shlo ka stong phrag bcu bzhi pa/ paN+Di ta a lang+ga de ba dang/ lo tsA ba ga rod tshul khrims 'byung gnas sbas pa'i 'gyur bzhugs so// //ru lu gnyis la 'dul ba mdo'i rgya cher 'grel ba slob dpon chos
127a3(dkar chag): kyi bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ shlo ka nyi khri chig stong bam po bdun cu pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang/ lo tsA ba klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur bzhugs so// //shu ba la 'dul ba mdo'i 'grel pa slob dpon shes rab 'byung gnas kyis
127a4(dkar chag): mdzad pa bzhugs so// //su pa la 'dul ba mdo'i 'grel chung yon tan 'od mar grags pa bzhugs/ 'di bod mar the tshom za'o// //hu pa la 'dul ba tshig le'ur byas pa me tog phreng rgyud/ dpal 'phags pas ga'i ltas
127a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ bam po lnga pa/ slob dpon shAkya 'od kyis mdzad pa'i dge tshul gyi tshig le'ur byas pa sum pa rgyab dang/ de'i 'grel pa 'od ldan bam po brgyad pa gnyis paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de wa dang/ lo tsA brtsangs de wan+d+ra rak+Shi nyi? 'gyur/ sum brgya ba'i

127a7(dkar chag): mdzad kyang zer/ kha che dge 'dun bzang pos mdzad kyang zer ba/ paN+Di ta mu ne warma dang/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa don brgyad ma slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa/ yang lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa thams cad yod par smra ba'i dge tshul
127b1(dkar chag): gyi bya ba zhes bya ba/ 'di bod kyi mkhan po chen po dag gi brjed byang yin pa 'dra'o/ /dge tshul gyi bslab pa'i gzhi'i mdo/ /mdo sde 'dzin pa dge legs bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mahA dza na dang/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu mchog gi 'gyur/ gleng gzhi dang

130b1(dkar chag): ma la shI las mdzad pa'i dang bskyed sgron ma gnyis/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thos pa'i phan yon ston pa dpe'i phreng ba las/ sangs rgyas mchog gi dpe paN+Di ra d+harma sh+rli b+ha dra dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims yon tan gyi 'gyur la/ rin chen bzang pos bcos pa/ dkon
